### [1] [A Zipf-preserving, long-range correlated surrogate for written language and other symbolic sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02213)
*Marcelo A. Montemurro,Mirko Degli Esposti*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种能够同时保持符号序列频率分布和长程相关性的替代模型（surrogate model），通过将分形高斯噪声（FGN）映射到经验直方图来生成保留一阶统计量和长程标度特性的替代序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有替代模型通常只能保持频率分布或相关特性中的一种，无法同时保留两者。语言中的齐普夫定律（Zipf's law）和DNA中的长程相关性需要同时考虑这两种约束条件。

Method: 通过将分形高斯噪声（fractional Gaussian noise, FGN）映射到经验直方图，采用频率保持分配（frequency-preserving assignment）方法生成符号序列的替代序列，同时保留经验符号频率和去趋势波动分析（detrended fluctuation analysis, DFA）指数量化的长程相关结构。

Result: 在英语和拉丁语代表性文本以及基因组DNA上验证了模型有效性，替代序列成功再现了原始序列的碱基组成和DFA标度特性，同时随机化了短程依赖性。

Conclusion: 该方法为解构符号系统的结构特征提供了原理性工具，可用于检验语言、DNA和其他符号领域中标度律和记忆效应起源的假设。

Abstract: Symbolic sequences such as written language and genomic DNA display characteristic frequency distributions and long-range correlations extending over many symbols. In language, this takes the form of Zipf's law for word frequencies together with persistent correlations spanning hundreds or thousands of tokens, while in DNA it is reflected in nucleotide composition and long-memory walks under purine-pyrimidine mappings. Existing surrogate models usually preserve either the frequency distribution or the correlation properties, but not both simultaneously.
  We introduce a surrogate model that retains both constraints: it preserves the empirical symbol frequencies of the original sequence and reproduces its long-range correlation structure, quantified by the detrended fluctuation analysis (DFA) exponent. Our method generates surrogates of symbolic sequences by mapping fractional Gaussian noise (FGN) onto the empirical histogram through a frequency-preserving assignment. The resulting surrogates match the original in first-order statistics and long-range scaling while randomising short-range dependencies.
  We validate the model on representative texts in English and Latin, and illustrate its broader applicability with genomic DNA, showing that base composition and DFA scaling are reproduced. This approach provides a principled tool for disentangling structural features of symbolic systems and for testing hypotheses on the origin of scaling laws and memory effects across language, DNA, and other symbolic domains.

</details>

# astro-ph.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Isocurvature Constraints on Dark Matter from Evaporated Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02322)
*G. Franciolini,D. Racco*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了暗物质（DM）通过原初黑洞（PBH）完全蒸发产生的机制，重点分析了该框架中可能产生的等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations）及其对暗物质产生的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于重新评估通过原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）蒸发产生稳定暗物质粒子的情景，特别关注该框架中可能出现的等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations）问题。原初黑洞形成时继承了不可观测小尺度上的泊松涨落（Poisson fluctuations），这些涨落在存在耦合长短波模的原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）时，可能成为宇宙学尺度上等曲率扰动的来源。

Method: 研究方法包括详细分析等曲率扰动在该框架中的作用机制，特别是原初黑洞形成时的泊松涨落如何通过原初非高斯性耦合到长波模式，进而产生宇宙学尺度的等曲率扰动。同时重新评估了该情景下的多种约束条件。

Result: 研究发现等曲率扰动不可避免地会通过霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）转移到暗物质粒子中，这凸显了等曲率约束对通过原初黑洞蒸发产生的暗物质粒子的潜在影响。研究还重新评估了来自暗物质过量产生的约束，包括原初黑洞蒸发和暴胀期间（后）的引力产生（freeze-in），以及温暗物质（warm DM）和标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational waves）过量产生的限制。

Conclusion: 研究结论强调了等曲率约束对通过原初黑洞蒸发产生暗物质粒子情景的重要性，表明这种机制产生的暗物质粒子会受到严格的宇宙学观测限制。同时，研究重新评估了该情景下的多种约束条件，为理解暗物质通过原初黑洞蒸发的产生机制提供了更全面的限制框架。

Abstract: We revisit the scenario in which stable particles of a dark sector are produced through the complete evaporation of light primordial black holes (PBHs) formed in the early Universe. We investigate in detail the role of isocurvature perturbations that may arise in this framework. PBHs inherit Poisson fluctuations on unobservable small scales at formation; however, in the presence of primordial non-Gaussianity that couples long- and short-wavelength modes, these fluctuations can source isocurvature perturbations on cosmological scales. Such perturbations are unavoidably transferred to the dark sector particles emitted via Hawking evaporation. We highlight the potential impact of isocurvature constraints on dark sector particles produced through PBH evaporation. Along the way, we re-assess the constraints on this scenario arising from the overproduction of dark matter (DM), accounting for both PBH evaporation and gravitational production (freeze-in) during (after) inflation, as well as bounds from warm DM and the overproduction of scalar-induced gravitational waves.

</details>


### [3] [Diffusive dark fluids with Planck-2018 and DESI BAO DR2 Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02828)
*Shambel Sahlu,Amare Abebe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究通过结合普朗克2018年宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）数据和DESI DR2的重子声学振荡（BAO）数据，对扩散暗流体宇宙学模型（一种相互作用暗能量框架）进行了约束分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在约束扩散暗流体宇宙学模型，该模型属于相互作用暗能量框架，其中两种暗成分通过扩散过程进行能量转移。研究扩展了S. Sahlu等人（2026）的工作，采用更新的观测数据进行更精确的参数约束。

Method: 方法包括使用普朗克2018年宇宙微波背景辐射（Cosmic Microwave Background, CMB）数据与暗能量光谱仪（Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument, DESI）DR2（2024）的重子声学振荡（Baryon Acoustic Oscillation, BAO）数据进行联合分析。通过计算尺度依赖的密度对比和物质功率谱，并与ΛCDM模型比较，评估相互作用对宇宙演化和结构形成的影响。

Result: 研究发现，扩散模型得到的哈勃常数（H₀）值分别为67.3876^{+1.0765}_{-1.0709}和68.3804^{+0.5639}_{-0.5852} km·s⁻¹·Mpc⁻¹，与普朗克2018年值（H₀ = 67.4±0.5 km·s⁻¹·Mpc⁻¹）的差异分别为0.0105σ和1.29σ。研究还观测到相互作用对宇宙演化和结构形成的影响。

Conclusion: 通过结合CMB和BAO数据，本研究成功约束了扩散暗流体模型，发现该模型在哈勃常数测量方面与普朗克数据存在不同程度的差异，并揭示了暗成分相互作用对宇宙结构形成的可观测效应。

Abstract: In this paper, we constrain the diffusive dark fluid cosmological model, which is the interacting dark energy framework, wherein energy is transferred between the two dark components through a diffusion process. We extended the work by S. Sahlu et al. (2026) by employing Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data from the Planck 2018 measurements in combination with Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) data from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) DR2 (2024).From the results, we found that the discrepancies in $H_0$ measurements are $0.0105σ$ and $1.29σ$ between the Planck 2018 value $(H_0 = 67.4\pm0.5\ \mathrm{km,s^{-1},Mpc^{-1}})$ and our diffusive model values, $H_0 = 67.3876^{+1.0765}_{-1.0709}$ and $68.3804^{+0.5639}_{-0.5852}$, respectively. We also the we observe that the effects of the interaction on cosmic evolution and structure formation; we emphasize this by computing the scale-dependent density contrast and the matter power spectrum, compared with the $Λ$CDM model.

</details>


### [4] [Testing gravitational wave polarizations with LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03165)
*Shingo Akama,Maxence Corman,Paola C. M. Delgado,Alice Garoffolo,Macarena Lagos,Alberto Mangiagli,Sylvain Marsat,Manuel Piarulli,Gianmassimo Tasinato,Jann Zosso,Giuseppe Gaetano Luciano,Nils A. Nilsson,Leandros Perivolaropoulos,Kristen Schumacher Aloh,Benjamin Sutton,Roxane Theriault,Amresh Verma,Yiqi Xie,Mian Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究量化了激光干涉空间天线（LISA）探测引力波中非张量极化模式及张量极化修正的能力。通过参数化后爱因斯坦（PPE）形式体系建模对广义相对论（GR）的偏离，并基于四种修正引力理论推导约束。结果显示LISA对张量极化振幅修正的约束精度可达10⁻⁴-10⁻²，对矢量极化的约束精度比标量极化高2-3倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在评估激光干涉空间天线（LISA）探测引力波中非张量极化模式的能力，以及检验张量极化对广义相对论（General Relativity）的偏离。通过量化LISA对多种极化模式的探测精度，为未来空间引力波天文台测试修正引力理论提供理论依据。

Method: 采用参数化后爱因斯坦（Parametrized Post-Einsteinian, PPE）形式体系，对张量、矢量和标量极化模式中偏离广义相对论（GR）的效应进行建模。该参数化受到四种修正引力理论（Horndeski、Einstein-aether、Rosen双度规和Lightman-Lee理论）的后牛顿波形启发。将修正一致地应用于旋进（inspiral）、并合（merger）和铃宕（ringdown）三个阶段，确保波形对齐和渐近处理，随后进行Fisher预报分析。

Result: 对于张量极化，LISA对振幅修正的约束精度在10⁻⁴-10⁻²之间，具体取决于修正的频率演化特性（针对红移z=1、质量10⁵-10⁷ M⊙的系统）。LISA仅能区分呼吸（breathing）和纵向（longitudinal）标量极化模式，且仅限于质量M≲10⁴ M⊙的相对较轻双星系统。矢量极化的约束精度比标量极化高约2-3倍，振幅测量精度范围为10⁻⁸-10⁻²。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，激光干涉空间天线（LISA）具备通过引力波极化模式在强场区域探测引力理论的能力。该工作为未来空间引力波观测约束修正引力理论参数空间提供了定量预测，展示了LISA在多极化模式探测方面的独特潜力。

Abstract: In this paper we quantify the ability of the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) to test the presence of non-tensorial polarizations as well as modifications to the tensor ones in gravitational waves emitted from massive black hole binaries. We employ the Parametrized Post-Einsteinian (PPE) formalism to model deviations from General Relativity (GR) for tensor, vector, and scalar polarizations. Our PPE parametrization is inspired by post-Newtonian waveforms from four modified gravity theories: Horndeski, Einstein-aether, Rosen's bimetric, and Lightman-Lee. We consistently implement these modifications across the inspiral, merger, and ringdown phases, ensuring proper waveform alignment and tapering. Subsequently, we perform Fisher forecasts to derive expected constraints on deviations from General Relativity and map these constraints to the parameter spaces of the four gravity theories. For tensor polarizations, LISA achieves constraints on amplitude modifications ranging between $\sim 10^{-4}-10^{-2}$ precision level, depending on the frequency evolution of the modifications, for systems with $10^5-10^7 {\, \rm M}_\odot$ at $z = 1$. We find that LISA can distinguish breathing and longitudinal scalar polarizations only for relatively light binaries with $M \lesssim 10^4 {\, \rm M}_\odot$, beyond which these modes become degenerate in the detector response. Importantly, constraints on vector polarizations are approximately 2-3 times more precise than for scalar polarizations. For both vector and scalar modes, amplitude measurements reach precisions ranging between $\sim 10^{-8}-10^{-2}$, depending on the frequency evolution of the modifications, for systems with $10^5-10^7 {\, \rm M}_\odot$ at $z = 1$. These results demonstrate LISA's potential to probe gravity in the strong-field regime via gravitational wave polarizations.

</details>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Multiplet Recombination and the CFT Distance Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02304)
*Fabio Mantegazza,Enrico Marchetto,Elli Pomoni,Torben Skrzypek,Timo Weigand*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了四维 ${\cal N}=2$ 超共形场论（superconformal field theories）在无限距离极限下的结构，特别关注部分解耦极限（partial decoupling limits），揭示了弱耦合和强耦合区域分别产生多项式简并和指数简并的态塔（towers of states）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于量子引力（quantum gravity）和CFT距离猜想（CFT Distance Conjecture），旨在探索具有高维共形流形（conformal manifolds）的四维 ${\cal N}=2$ 超共形场论及其AdS对偶在无限距离极限下的行为。

Method: 方法聚焦于部分解耦极限，其中规范场部分（gauge sector）变得弱耦合而相互作用部分（interacting sector）持续存在。通过分析 ${\cal N}=2$ 超共形代数中的多重态重组（multiplet recombination），并利用最简单的双节点箭袋规范理论（two-node quiver gauge theory）进行显式单圈计算（one-loop computation）验证。

Result: 弱耦合区域贡献了CFT距离猜想预测的多项式简并（polynomial degeneracy）的无质量高自旋态塔（massless higher-spin tower）。关键新发现是相互作用区域出现受保护的BPS态塔（protected BPS tower），其特征是指数简并（exponential degeneracy）和AdS尺度的质量。

Conclusion: 当非受保护的长多重态（unprotected long multiplets）在弱耦合下达到幺正性界限（unitarity bound）时，它们重组为受保护的短多重态（protected short multiplets），这一机制解释了无限距离极限下态塔的结构特征。

Abstract: Motivated by quantum gravity and the CFT Distance Conjecture, we study infinite-distance limits in four-dimensional ${\cal N}=2$ superconformal field theories with higher-dimensional conformal manifolds and their AdS duals. We focus on partial decoupling limits where a gauge sector becomes weakly coupled while an interacting sector persists. We analyse the structure of towers of states emerging in these limits. The weakly coupled sector contributes, among others, the massless higher-spin tower predicted by the CFT Distance Conjecture exhibiting polynomial degeneracy. The key novelty is the appearance of a protected BPS tower in the interacting sector, characterised by exponential degeneracy and masses at the AdS scale. This structure follows from multiplet recombination in the ${\cal N}=2$ superconformal algebra: As unprotected long multiplets hit the unitarity bound at weak coupling, they recombine into protected short multiplets. We verify this picture through an explicit one-loop computation in the simplest two-node quiver gauge theory with a two-dimensional conformal manifold.

</details>


### [6] [A Quantum Weyl Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02311)
*Ivo Sachs,Marc Schneider*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子场论方法探测碰撞平面波时空的奇异性，发现Khan-Penrose解的奇点无法被量子探测，而Ferrari-Ibáñez解的奇点可以穿越，并提出了基于Weyl张量库仑部分的量子Weyl猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过量子场论方法探测碰撞平面波时空的奇异性，特别是Khan-Penrose和Ferrari-Ibáñez这两种具有不同奇异性强度的解，以理解量子理论如何影响时空奇点的可穿越性。

Method: 采用量子探测（quantum probing）方法分析碰撞平面波时空，重点研究Khan-Penrose解和Ferrari-Ibáñez解这两种具有不同奇异性特征的时空几何。

Result: 研究发现Khan-Penrose解的奇点与Schwarzschild奇点类似，无法被量子场论探测，而Ferrari-Ibáñez解的奇点可以被穿越。基于此提出了量子Weyl猜想：Weyl张量的库仑部分（Coulomb part of the Weyl tensor）是分类时空量子探测特性的关键几何性质。

Conclusion: 研究提出了量子Weyl猜想，认为Weyl张量的库仑部分是决定时空量子探测特性的核心几何特征，并利用该猜想为平面波的可能反作用（backreaction）场景提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We perform a quantum probing of colliding plane-wave space-times. In particular, we consider the Khan-Penrose and the Ferrari-Ibáñez solutions, which admit a strong and a weak singularity after the two waves collide. While we find that, like Schwarzschild, for the Khan-Penrose solution the singularity cannot be probed by quantum field theory, the Ferrari-Ibáñez singularity can be traversed. Our results culminate in a quantum Weyl conjecture: The significant geometric property to classify space-times with respect to quantum probes is given by the Coulomb part of the Weyl tensor. We then use this conjecture to sketch a possible backreaction scenario for plane waves.

</details>


### [7] [Perturbative semiclassical entropy of dynamical black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02320)
*Avinandan Mondal,Kartik Prabhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究渐近平坦时空中具有分岔Killing视界的微扰量子引力，通过引入边界荷作为辅助"观测者"自由度，构建了与Killing对称性不变的观测量，并计算了经典-量子相干态的冯·诺依曼熵，该熵满足类似热力学第一定律的关系，并与微扰黑洞的Hollands-Wald-Zhang熵相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究渐近平坦时空中具有分岔Killing视界的微扰量子引力理论，旨在理解引力约束在视界观测代数中的角色，并探索量子引力背景下熵的统计力学起源。

Method: 将微扰引力约束纳入时空未来视界右半部分的观测量代数中，使用与视界Killing场相关的边界荷作为辅助"观测者"自由度，构建与Killing对称性不变的"修饰"观测量，生成Type-$\text{II}_{\infty}$冯·诺依曼因子。

Result: 计算了由度规微扰和"观测者波函数"构建的经典-量子相干态的约化密度矩阵的冯·诺依曼熵，该熵满足类似热力学第一定律的类比关系，并证明该熵通过微扰穿过视界和未来类光无穷远的通量与微扰黑洞的Hollands-Wald-Zhang熵相关联。

Conclusion: 在微扰量子引力框架下，通过引入辅助观测者自由度，可以构建与Killing对称性不变的观测量代数，其相干态的冯·诺依曼熵具有热力学性质，并与黑洞微扰熵存在明确的物理联系。

Abstract: We consider perturbative quantum gravity as a quantum field theory of linearized metric perturbation on an asymptotically flat spacetime with a bifurcate Killing horizon. We include the perturbative gravitational constraints into the algebra of observables restricted to the right half of the future horizon of the spacetime. We use the boundary charge, associated to the horizon Killing field, as an auxiliary "observer" degree of freedom. The observables "dressed" with the additional charge are invariant under the Killing symmetry and generate a Type-$\text{II}_{\infty}$ von Neumann factor. We compute the von Neumann entropy of the reduced density matrix of a classical-quantum coherent state constructed from the metric perturbations and the "observer wavefunction". This von Neumann entropy satisfies an analogue of the first law of thermodynamics. We further show that this entropy is related to Hollands-Wald-Zhang entropy of the (second order) perturbed dynamical black hole through the flux of perturbations through the horizon and future null infinity.

</details>


### [8] [One-loop aspects of de Sitter axion wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02335)
*Victor Ivo,Haifeng Tang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了轴子（axion）支持的德西特（de Sitter）虫洞的欧几里得路径积分（Euclidean path integral）在一圈（one-loop）阶的行为。通过数值计算路径积分的相位，并分析了不同几何极限下的物理解释，包括将虫洞视为带有两个局域算符插入的球面，以及"最大通量（maximal flux）"解对应的爱因斯坦静态宇宙（Einstein static universe）不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究轴子支持的德西特虫洞在一圈阶的量子性质，特别是路径积分的相位行为。这有助于理解虫洞在量子引力中的角色，以及它们与有效场论（EFT）描述之间的关系。

Method: 采用数值方法计算虫洞解及其"多虫洞（multiple wormholes）"推广的路径积分相位。在几何近似为带小柄的球面时，建立虫洞作为带有两个局域算符插入的球面的有效描述。对于最大通量解，解析地确定涨落谱。

Result: 当几何近似为带小柄的球面时，虫洞相位可视为球面上的Polchinski相位乘以有效局域算符位置积分的额外相位。对极位（antipodal）构型是不稳定的极值点。在最大通量极限下，涨落谱可解析求解，且路径积分相位完全由爱因斯坦静态宇宙的已知不稳定性解释。

Conclusion: 轴子支持的德西特虫洞在一圈阶的量子行为可通过有效局域算符描述理解。虫洞相位包含几何贡献和算符位置涨落贡献。最大通量解的不稳定性与爱因斯坦静态宇宙的不稳定性直接相关，为虫洞量子性质提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We discuss aspects of the Euclidean path integral around axion-supported de Sitter wormholes, at one-loop order. We numerically compute the phase of the path integral around these solutions, as well as for a certain "multiple wormholes" generalization, and interpret this phase in different regimes. When the geometry is well approximated by a sphere with a small handle, the wormhole admits an effective description as a sphere with two local operator insertions, whose positions fluctuate around the antipodal configuration. The antipodal configuration is an extremum of the position integral for the operators, but we show that it is an unstable one. Accordingly, the phase of the wormhole solution can be viewed as the Polchinski phase in the sphere, multiplied by an additional phase from the integral over positions of the effective local operators. Using our expressions for the one-loop determinant, we also estimate the EFT coefficients of the dual bilocal operators in odd spacetime dimensions, to one-loop order. Lastly, we also discuss "maximal flux" solutions, which have $S^{1}\times S^{D-1}$ geometry. Their Lorentzian continuations are Einstein static universes, so we call them "Einstein wormholes". In this limit, we determine the spectrum of fluctuations analytically and show that the phase of the path integral around this solution is entirely accounted for by the well-known instability of the Einstein static universe.

</details>


### [9] [Solution of Quantum Quartic Potential Problems with Airy Fredholm Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02374)
*Ori J. Ganor*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文引入了与特定四次势量子力学问题哈密顿量对易的Fredholm积分算子，这些算子用Airy函数表达，其特征值呈指数衰减，可用于高精度数值分析，并导致节点变量和权重的一维无限链对偶描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为具有四次势的量子力学问题引入新的数学工具，以改进数值分析精度并揭示系统的对偶描述结构，涵盖从简谐振子到多变量势场乃至量子场论等广泛物理系统。

Method: 通过构造与特定哈密顿量对易的Fredholm积分算子（Fredholm integral operators），这些算子用Airy函数表达，并建立与无限一维链的对应关系，其中节点包含变量，节点和连接具有权重。

Result: 所引入的积分算子特征值呈指数衰减，适用于高精度数值分析；同时揭示了系统存在对偶描述，即可以表示为具有节点变量以及节点和连接权重的无限一维链。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了与四次势量子系统对易的Fredholm积分算子，不仅提供了有效的数值分析工具，还揭示了系统的一维链对偶描述，适用于从非简谐振子到非局域相互作用量子场论等多种物理系统。

Abstract: Fredholm integral operators that commute with the Hamiltonians of certain quantum mechanical problems with quartic potentials are introduced. The operators are expressed in terms of an Airy function, and their eigenvalues fall off exponentially fast. They may help with high-accuracy numerical analysis, and their existence leads to dual descriptions in terms of infinite one-dimensional chains with variables on nodes, and weights on nodes and links. The systems discussed include the anharmonic quartic oscillator as well as multivariable potentials and higher dimensional systems, including certain quantum field theories with nonlocal interactions.

</details>


### [10] [The Routh of the Attractor Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02559)
*Arghya Chattopadhyay,Alessio Marrani,Sourav Roychowdhury*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究阐明了四维时空中静态、球对称、渐进平坦的极端黑洞背景下Maxwell-Einstein-scalar理论有效动力学的多个方面，将受吸引子机制（Attractor Mechanism）支配的一维有效径向动力学通过Routhian形式体系严格表述，并分析了三个有效泛函的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在澄清四维时空静态、球对称、渐进平坦极端黑洞背景下Maxwell-Einstein-scalar理论有效动力学的各个方面，特别是将受吸引子机制支配的一维有效径向动力学置于严格的数学框架中。

Method: 采用Routhian形式体系（Routhian formalism），这是基于部分Legendre变换、介于Lagrange和Hamilton形式之间的框架，特别适用于存在循环变量（cyclic variables）的情况。通过Ferrara-Gibbons-Kallosh有效黑洞势$V_{BH}$的临界点来研究吸引子机制。

Result: 阐明了三个有效泛函的相互作用：$V_{BH}$、Sen熵泛函$\mathcal{E}$和相关的有效Routhian泛函$\mathcal{R}$。这些泛函在事件视界处的临界值决定了极端黑洞的Bekenstein-Hawking熵和Wald熵。

Conclusion: 该研究为极端黑洞背景下Maxwell-Einstein-scalar理论的有效动力学提供了严格的数学框架，通过Routhian形式体系将吸引子机制置于更坚实的理论基础之上，并揭示了不同熵泛函之间的内在联系。

Abstract: We investigate and clarify various aspects of the effective dynamics of Maxwell-Einstein-scalar theories in the background of static, spherically symmetric and asymptotically flat extremal black holes in four space-time dimensions. This rigorously places the one-dimensional effective radial dynamics governed by the Attractor Mechanism, through the critical points of the Ferrara-Gibbons-Kallosh effective black hole potential $V_{BH}$, into the Routhian formalism, a framework which is intermediate between the Lagrange and Hamilton ones, based on a partial Legendre transform, and especially relevant in presence of cyclic variables. We elucidate and analyze the interplay of a trio of effective functionals: the aforementioned $V_{BH}$, Sen's entropy functional $\mathcal{E}$, and the relevant effective Routhian functional $\mathcal{R}$. Through their critical values at the event horizon, such functionals determine the Bekenstein-Hawking and the Wald entropy of the extremal black hole.

</details>


### [11] [Emergent Gribov horizon from replica symmetry breaking in Yang--Mills theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02838)
*Rodrigo Carmo Terin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文展示了Serreau-Tissier（ST）副本扇区能够动态生成杨-米尔斯理论中的Gribov-Zwanziger（GZ）型视界泛函，通过副本超场积分和Faddeev-Popov算符行列式展开，在副本对称相产生局域Curci-Ferrari屏蔽质量，在副本破缺相产生诱导视界相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索Serreau-Tissier（ST）副本扇区如何为杨-米尔斯（Yang-Mills, YM）理论中的Gribov-Zwanziger（GZ）视界泛函提供微观生成机制。该工作试图理解副本动力学如何自然地诱导出Gribov尺度，并为红外行为提供统一的描述框架。

Method: 通过积分掉副本超场（replica superfields），在调节参数ζ中对Faddeev-Popov（FP）算符的行列式进行展开。在ζ的线性阶，该方法产生具有与Gribov视界泛函相同颜色和洛伦兹结构的非局域核。此外，还采用了超空间推导来确认诱导视界项的起源。

Result: ST扇区根据动力学选择的副本相产生两种不同结果：在副本对称相产生局域Curci-Ferrari（CF）屏蔽质量；在副本破缺相产生诱导视界相互作用。后者通过BRST不变的局域化表述，得到精化Gribov-Zwanziger（RGZ）解耦型的树级胶子传播子，而前者简化为有质量的FP/CF形式，从构造上避免了红外尺度的双重计数。

Conclusion: 研究证实了诱导视界项起源于ST超行列式，为Gribov尺度在副本框架内的涌现提供了微观机制。该工作建立了副本扇区与Gribov-Zwanziger形式之间的直接联系，为理解杨-米尔斯理论的红外行为提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We show that the Serreau--Tissier (ST) replica sector can dynamically generate a Gribov--Zwanziger (GZ)--type horizon functional in Yang--Mills (YM) theories. After integrating out the replica superfields, the expansion of the determinant of the Faddeev--Popov (FP) operator in the regulator $ζ$ produces, at linear order in $ζ$, a nonlocal kernel with the same color and Lorentz structure as the Gribov horizon functional, thereby defining an induced Gribov scale. Depending on the replica phase selected by the dynamics, the ST sector yields either (i) a local Curci--Ferrari (CF) screening mass (replica-symmetric phase) or (ii) an induced horizon-like interaction (replica-broken phase). In the latter case, the resulting BRST-invariant local formulation leads to a tree-level gluon propagator of the refined Gribov-Zwanziger (RGZ) decoupling type, whereas in the former it reduces to the massive FP/CF form, avoiding double counting of infrared scales by construction. A superspace derivation confirms that the induced horizon term originates from the ST superdeterminant, providing a microscopic mechanism for the emergence of the Gribov scale within the replica framework.

</details>


### [12] [Torsion-Induced Modification to Friedmann Equations in $AdSL_{4}$ Gauged Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02864)
*Oktay Cebecioğlu,Salih Kibaroğlu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于AdSL₄代数的引力规范理论扩展，推导了包含挠率修正的Friedmann方程，发现挠率可产生类de Sitter加速解，其有效物态参数ω_B=-1/3，连接了时空挠率与宇宙弦状动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究AdSL₄规范引力中引力场方程的解，该理论是基于AdSL₄代数的广义相对论规范理论扩展。关注挠率（torsion）如何通过规范场B^{ab}修正引力方程，并探索其在宇宙学背景下的物理含义。

Method: 采用AdSL₄规范引力理论框架，其中反对称规范场B^{ab}通过关系K^{ab}=μB^{ab}诱导时空挠率。在空间均匀且各向同性的宇宙学背景下，推导修正的Friedmann方程，明确包含挠率贡献。

Result: 加速度方程允许类de Sitter解，其中宇宙加速完全源于扩大的四维时空对称性的规范理论结构。规范场B^{ab}的动态分量自然成为有效宇宙学常数的来源，无需引入奇异物质源。挠率驱动的宇宙学相可产生有效物态参数ω_B=-1/3。

Conclusion: AdSL₄规范引力中的挠率修正可在宇宙学背景下产生加速膨胀，建立了时空挠率与宇宙弦状动力学之间的直接联系。规范场分量自然地提供了有效宇宙学常数，为宇宙加速机制提供了纯几何解释。

Abstract: We study the solution of the gravitational field equations in $AdSL_{4}$-gauged gravity, a gauge-theoretic extension of general relativity based on the $AdSL_{4}$ algebra. In this formulation, the antisymmetric gauge field $B^{ab}$, associated with additional $AdSL_{4}$ tensorial generators, induces space-time torsion via the relation $K^{ab}=μB^{ab}$, where $K^{ab}$ denotes the contorsion 1-form. The presence of torsion modifies both the spin connection and curvature, leading to an extended set of Einstein-Cartan field equations. Focusing on spatially homogeneous and isotropic cosmological backgrounds, we derive the modified Friedmann equations which explicitly incorporate the torsional contribution. The resulting acceleration equation admits de Sitter-like solutions in which cosmic acceleration originates purely from the gauge-theoretic structure of enlarged four-dimensional space-time symmetries. Within this formulation, the dynamical components of the gauge field $B^{ab}$ emerge naturally as a source of the effective cosmological constants, without the introduction of exotic matter sources. Furthermore, our analysis shows that the torsion-driven cosmological phase in $AdSL_{4}$-gauged gravity can reproduce an effective equation-of-state parameter $ω_{B}=-1/3$, establishing a connection between space-time torsion and cosmic-string-like dynamics.

</details>


### [13] [Dimensional Reduction is Supersymmetric at Three Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02892)
*Mrigankamauli Chakraborty,Sven-Olaf Moch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文解决了维度约化正则化（dimensional reduction, DR）在三圈水平上破坏超对称性的长期争议，证明该问题源于克利福德代数（Clifford algebra）处理的微妙性而非DR本身，修正后的计算恢复了完整的超对称行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期研究指出维度约化正则化在超杨-米尔斯理论（Super Yang-Mills, SYM）的三圈水平上无法保持超对称性，具体表现为N=2 SYM中Yukawa耦合与鬼-胶子β函数的不匹配，这引发了关于DR是否破坏超对称性的长期争议。

Method: 通过修正克利福德代数处理中的微妙问题，重新进行三圈计算，并分析该问题对N=4 SYM的影响，同时与现有四圈结果进行一致性检验。

Result: 修正后的三圈计算恢复了完整的超对称行为，证明DR本身不破坏超对称性；该问题对N=4 SYM的影响最早出现在五圈水平，这与现有四圈结果一致。

Conclusion: 研究证实维度约化正则化在已检验的圈数范围内（包括三圈及以下）能够保持N=1、2和4超杨-米尔斯理论的超对称性，解决了长期存在的争议。

Abstract: We resolve the long-standing claim that regularisation by dimensional reduction (DR) fails to preserve supersymmetry in Super Yang-Mills (SYM) theories at three loops. Earlier results reported a mismatch between the Yukawa and ghost-gluon $β$ functions in $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYM, suggesting a breakdown of supersymmertry. We show that this discrepancy does not originate from DR itself but from subtleties in the treatment of the Clifford algebra. A corrected three-loop calculation restores full supersymmetric behaviour, and we demonstrate that the same issue would first affect $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM only at five loops, consistent with existing four-loop results. Our findings confirm that DR preserves supersymmetry for $\mathcal{N}=1, 2$ and $4$ SYM through the loop orders examined.

</details>


### [14] [Lorentz violating quadratic gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02980)
*R. B. Alfaia,Willian Carvalho,A. C. Lehum,J. R. Nascimento,A. Yu. Petrov,P. J. Porfírio*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究大黄蜂模型（bumblebee model）与二次引力（quadratic gravity）耦合的微扰重整化（perturbative renormalization）和经典动力学，重点关注洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz symmetry violation）的物理效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索洛伦兹对称性破缺的理论框架，通过大黄蜂模型（bumblebee model）与二次引力（quadratic gravity）的耦合，分析矢量场诱导的非零真空期望值（vacuum expectation value, VEV）如何导致时空中出现优先方向，从而实现洛伦兹对称性的自发破缺（spontaneous breaking of Lorentz symmetry）。

Method: 采用维度正规化（dimensional regularization）方法，在平直空间附近展开度规，计算大黄蜂场和引力子场两点函数（two-point functions）的单圈发散部分（one-loop divergent parts），特别关注内部线中洛伦兹破缺插入（Lorentz-violating insertions）的作用。同时推导经典场方程并寻找精确解。

Result: 研究确定了在存在优先背景方向时重整化引力和大黄蜂扇区所需的抵消项（counterterms），并明确了洛伦兹破缺相互作用如何反馈到二次引力的紫外结构（UV structure）中。在经典方面，发现施瓦西几何（Schwarzschild geometry）在适当的大黄蜂构型下仍然是精确解，即使存在非最小耦合（non-minimal couplings）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了洛伦兹破缺相互作用对二次引力紫外结构的反馈机制，并通过单圈结构分析了理论的操作子内容（operator content）。研究结果为扩展到宇宙学和更低对称性背景提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper we explore the perturbative renormalization and study the classical dynamics of the bumblebee model coupled to quadratic gravity, a theoretical setting that allows the violation of Lorentz symmetry. Such a violation arises from a vector field whose potential is engineered to induce a nonzero vacuum expectation value (VEV), thereby leading to the emergence of a preferred direction in spacetime and, consequently, to the spontaneous breaking of Lorentz symmetry. Working in dimensional regularization and expanding the metric around flat space, we compute the one-loop divergent parts of the two-point functions of the bumblebee and graviton fields, with special emphasis on the role of Lorentz-violating insertions in internal lines. These results determine the counterterms required to renormalize the gravitational and bumblebee sectors in the presence of a preferred background direction, and make explicit how Lorentz-violating interactions feed back into the UV structure of quadratic gravity. On the classical side, we derive the field equations and identify exact solutions supported by bumblebee backgrounds. In particular, we show that the Schwarzschild geometry remains an exact solution for an appropriate bumblebee configuration, even in the presence of non-minimal couplings. We close with a discussion of the operator content suggested by the one-loop structure and of prospective extensions to cosmological and less symmetric backgrounds.

</details>


### [15] [Evolution and scattering of excited topological defects: Interaction between internal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03003)
*D. Miguélez-Caballero*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文系统分析了拓扑孤子（topological solitons）内部模式（internal modes）被激发时的行为，包括(1+1)维kink的辐射发射和kink/antikink散射动力学，以及(2+1)维涡旋（vortex）的内部模式结构和辐射特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究拓扑孤子内部模式被激活时的动力学行为，旨在理解这些非线性系统中能量交换和辐射发射的机制。特别关注内部模式激发如何影响孤子的辐射特性和散射过程。

Method: 采用双φ⁴模型（double φ⁴ model）研究kink的辐射发射，利用MSTB模型分析kink/antikink碰撞动力学。对于(2+1)维涡旋，基于Abelian-Higgs模型研究其内部模式结构，并将(1+1)维的解析技术扩展到二维场论中。

Result: 揭示了耦合常数变化对kink辐射振幅和频率的影响，阐明了kink/antikink散射中的共振能量交换机制（resonant energy exchange mechanism）。对于涡旋，通过特征函数的角依赖简化了问题，并计算了辐射振幅、频率以及内部模式振幅的辐射衰减。

Conclusion: 论文系统建立了拓扑孤子内部模式激发与辐射发射之间的理论框架，成功将(1+1)维解析方法扩展到高维情形，并通过数值模拟验证了所有解析结果，深化了对拓扑孤子动力学行为的理解。

Abstract: This thesis presents an extensive analysis of the behavior of topological solitons when one or more of their internal modes are activated. The first part of this manuscript is devoted to the study of the simplest topological solitons in (1+1) dimensions: kinks. Specifically, we investigate how these solutions emit radiation when one of their internal modes is initially excited, within the framework of the double $φ^4$ model. The simplest kink solution in this theory exhibits a complex internal mode structure that depends on a coupling constant appearing in the potential governing the dynamics. We will show how the amplitude and frequency of the emitted radiation are affected by changes in this coupling constant. We also examine the dynamics of wobbling kink/antikink scattering when the kinks possess more than one internal mode. To this end, we study kink/antikink collisions in the context of the simplest kink solution arising in the MSTB model. This analysis sheds light on the resonant energy exchange mechanism, allowing energy transfer between internal modes and the translational mode. The second part of this thesis focuses on excited vortex solutions in (2+1) dimensions. We begin with a detailed study of the internal mode structure associated with vortex solutions in the Abelian-Higgs model. We demonstrate how the problem can be significantly simplified by choosing an appropriate angular dependence for the eigenfunctions. Furthermore, we investigate the radiation emitted by a vortex when its internal mode is initially activated. To achieve this, we extend the analytical techniques used in (1+1) dimensions to field theories defined in two spatial dimensions. This enables us to compute the radiation amplitude, its frequency, and the decay of the internal mode amplitude due to energy loss via radiation. All analytical results are contrasted with data from numerical simulations.

### [16] [Spin Ruijsenaars-Schneider models are Coulomb branches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03048)
*Gleb Arutyunov,Lukas Hardi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文展示了3d $\mathcal{N}=4$项链型箭图规范理论的余调（cohomological）和K理论（$K$-theoretic）库仑分支（Coulomb branches）的泊松代数（Poisson algebras）分别提供了有理（rational）和双曲（hyperbolic）自旋Ruijsenaars-Schneider模型的运动方程。作者推测椭圆库仑分支的泊松代数将类似地再现椭圆自旋Ruijsenaars-Schneider模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立3d $\mathcal{N}=4$规范理论与可积系统之间的深刻联系，特别是探索项链型箭图（necklace quiver）规范理论的库仑分支如何为自旋Ruijsenaars-Schneider模型提供数学结构。

Method: 方法采用GKLO表示（GKLO representation）中的单极子算符（monopole operators）构造，使得仿射Yangian（affine Yangian）和量子环面（quantum toroidal）超可积结构（superintegrability structure）变得明显。通过分析余调库仑分支和K理论库仑分支的泊松代数来实现。

Result: 结果表明，余调库仑分支的泊松代数重现了有理自旋Ruijsenaars-Schneider模型的运动方程，而K理论库仑分支的泊松代数则重现了双曲自旋Ruijsenaars-Schneider模型的运动方程。构造过程同时揭示了相关的超可积结构。

Conclusion: 论文结论建立了3d $\mathcal{N}=4$项链型箭图规范理论与自旋Ruijsenaars-Schneider模型之间的精确对应关系，并推测椭圆库仑分支（elliptic Coulomb branches）的泊松代数将类似地产生椭圆自旋Ruijsenaars-Schneider模型。

Abstract: In this paper, we show that the Poisson algebras of cohomological and $K$-theoretic Coulomb branches of 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ necklace quiver gauge theories provide Poisson structures and Hamiltonians that reproduce the equations of motion of the rational and hyperbolic spin Ruijsenaars-Schneider models, respectively. The construction is carried out in terms of monopole operators in the GKLO representation, also making the affine Yangian (and, in $K$-theory, quantum toroidal) superintegrability structure manifest. We conjecture that the Poisson algebras of elliptic Coulomb branches similarly reproduce the elliptic spin Ruijsenaars-Schneider model.

</details>


### [17] [The multiloop sunset to all orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03183)
*Pierre Vanhove*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文推导了二维多圈日落费曼积分（multiloop sunset Feynman integrals）在任意质量配置和所有圈数下的精确收敛表示，适用于大欧几里得动量情况。这些表示避免了复杂的超越函数，适用于形式分析和高精度数值计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为二维多圈日落费曼积分建立精确的解析表示，这些表示应适用于任意质量配置和所有圈数，且能在大欧几里得动量下保持收敛性。此类表示对于形式分析和数值计算都具有重要价值。

Method: 方法包括推导出精确的收敛表示，将积分表达为对数质量比（logarithmic mass ratios）的对称多项式之和，这些多项式由外动量平方归一化，系数由解析级数展开确定。对于等质量情况，建立了维度提升关系（dimension-raising relation）。

Result: 主要结果包括：获得了二维多圈日落费曼积分的精确收敛表示；建立了等质量情况下L圈积分在D+2维与D维之间的维度提升关系；这些表示避免了复杂的超越函数，便于形式分析和数值计算。二维结果可作为维度移动关系（dimension-shifting relations）的边界条件。

Conclusion: 结论表明，所推导的表示形式简洁且实用，特别适用于形式分析和高精度数值计算。二维结果通过解析延拓到D = 4 - 2ε，能够系统性地重建四维日落费曼积分，为相关计算提供了有效工具。

Abstract: We derive exact, convergent representations of multiloop sunset Feynman integrals in two dimensions for arbitrary mass configurations and all loop orders valid for large Euclidean momentum. The integrals are expressed as sums of symmetric polynomials in logarithmic mass ratios, normalized by the external momentum squared, with coefficients determined by analytic series expansions. For the equal-mass case, we establish a dimension-raising relation expressing the $L$ loop sunset integrals in $D+2$ as the one in $D$ dimensions acted on a differential operator of order $L-1$.
  These representations are free of complicated transcendental functions, making them well-suited to both formal analysis and high-precision numerical evaluation. The two-dimensional results serve as boundary conditions for dimension-shifting relations, enabling systematic reconstruction of four-dimensional sunset integrals via analytic continuation to $D = 4 - 2ε$.

</details>


### [18] [Ultra slow-turn inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03204)
*Ana Achúcarro,Perseas Christodoulidis,Jinn-Ouk Gong,Oksana Iarygina*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 在多场模型中，通常认为快子型等曲率扰动（tachyonic isocurvature perturbations）意味着不稳定性，但本文发现超慢转（ultra slow-turn）模型中的指数衰减转率可以抑制这种潜在不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准多场模型中，快子型等曲率扰动通常表明存在不稳定性。本文重新审视已知反例的稳定性，旨在理解某些特殊模型如何避免这种不稳定性。

Method: 通过分析超慢转（ultra slow-turn）模型，研究指数衰减转率如何关闭潜在不稳定性。该方法聚焦于总熵扰动（total entropy perturbation）作为稳定性判据。

Result: 在超慢转模型中，即使等曲率扰动的有效质量平方为负，总熵扰动仍能正确推断模型稳定性。纤维暴胀（fibre inflation）、SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$)吸引子和模暴胀（modular inflation）等超引力或弦理论启发的模型均属于此类。

Conclusion: 超慢转模型中的指数衰减转率可以抑制快子型等曲率扰动带来的潜在不稳定性，为理解弦理论启发的暴胀模型稳定性提供了新视角。

Abstract: In standard multi-field models, tachyonic isocurvature perturbations generally indicate the presence of an instability. We revisit the stability of some known counterexamples and show that, in a certain class of models that we call ultra slow-turn, an exponentially decreasing turn rate can shut off this potential instability. We argue that the stability of a given model can be correctly inferred by the total entropy perturbation, even if the effective mass squared of the isocurvature perturbation is negative. Several recent supergravity- or string-inspired models such as fibre inflation, SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$) attractors and modular inflation fall into the ultra slow-turn class.

</details>


### [19] [Beyond thresholds: reconstructing UV physics from IR expansions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03277)
*Hiromasa Takaura,Wen Yin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在解析性和无质量奇异性假设下，紫外（ultraviolet）信息可以从低能展开系数中提取。通过逆拉普拉斯变换（inverse Laplace transform）和受控粗粒化（controlled coarse-graining）程序重组低能展开，使有效场论（effective field theory）截断之外的紫外行为变得可及。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于探索如何从低能物理观测中提取紫外信息，突破有效场论（effective field theory）的截断限制。传统上，有效场论仅描述低能物理，而紫外物理被视为被"积掉"的未知信息。

Method: 方法包括：1）假设解析性和无质量奇异性；2）通过逆拉普拉斯变换（inverse Laplace transform）重组低能展开；3）应用受控粗粒化（controlled coarse-graining）程序。这些技术使得紫外行为在有效场论截断之外变得可访问。

Result: 研究结果表明，可以直接从物理可观测量在质量阈值以下的低能展开中确定β函数（beta function）的符号和相关的动力学标度（dynamical scale）。这在QED和QCD类理论中得到了具体验证。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了紫外信息可以从低能展开系数中提取，突破了有效场论的传统限制。这一方法为从低能观测中推断高能物理提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We show that ultraviolet information can be extracted from low-energy expansion coefficients, assuming analyticity and the absence of massless singularities. By reorganizing the low-energy expansion through an inverse Laplace transform and a controlled coarse-graining procedure, we make ultraviolet behavior accessible beyond the cutoff of the effective field theory. In particular, we determine the sign of the beta function and the associated dynamical scale directly from the low-energy expansion of a physical observable below the mass thresholds in QED and QCD-like theories.

</details>

### [20] [Discovery of an electrically-controllable superconducting memory effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02450)
*Zheyu Wu,Hanyi Chen,Mengmeng Long,Daniel Shaffer,Dmitry V. Chichinadze,Andrej Cabala,Theodore I. Weinberger,Alexander J. Hickey,Jinxu Pu,Dave Graf,Vladimir Sechovsky,Michal Valiska,Gang Li,Rui Zhou,F. Malte Grosche,Alexander G. Eaton*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究展示了铀二碲化物（UTe₂）作为三重态超导体候选材料，在特定磁场条件下可通过电流脉冲在两种临界电流状态间切换，实现超导记忆功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导计算机的能效远超传统电子器件，但实现可读写记忆功能在超导平台中一直具有挑战性。本研究旨在探索超导材料中固有的记忆功能，避免依赖邻近的磁性或半导体界面。

Method: 研究使用铀二碲化物（UTe₂）块状单晶样品，在磁场作用下进入两个不同超导相之间的中间区域，通过施加直流脉冲来切换材料状态。通过调控刺激强度和持续时间来控制状态转换。

Result: UTe₂表现出可切换的亚稳态行为：直流脉冲可将材料推入具有增强临界电流（J_c）的状态，系统能长时间"记住"其处于高或低J_c状态。这种记忆功能源于两种不同涡旋物种之间的竞争，可被扰动推入非平衡高无序构型。

Conclusion: UTe₂的记忆功能是其超导序参量本身固有的特性，而非依赖外部界面。这一发现揭示了p波涡旋物质的丰富复杂性，并证明了设计具有超低功耗开关的新型超导记忆元件的可行性，对低温计算和量子硬件具有变革性意义。

Abstract: If a computer could be assembled from superconducting components, the energy efficiency would far surpass that of conventional electronics. Historic research efforts towards this goal yielded pivotal breakthroughs in the development and discovery of scanning tunnelling microscopy and high temperature superconductivity. Although recent strides have been taken in advancing superconducting diode and switching technologies, harnessing read/writeable memory functionality in superconducting platforms has remained challenging. Here we show that bulk single crystal specimens of the triplet superconductor candidate uranium ditelluride (UTe$_2$) possess such properties. Upon applying a magnetic field to access an intermediate regime straddling two distinct superconducting phases, we find that direct current pulses can push the material in and out of a metastable state possessing an enhanced critical current $J_c$. This switching is controllable by the strength and duration of the stimuli, with the system 'remembering' whether it is in the high or low $J_c$ state for extended periods. We interpret this to be due to competition between two distinct vortex species, which can be perturbatively pushed into a non-equilibrium high-disorder configuration with stronger pinning forces and thus higher $J_c$. Rather than requiring proximate magnetic or semiconducting interfaces, this memory functionality appears to be an intrinsic property of UTe$_2$ rooted in the superconducting order itself. Our findings underscore the rich complexity of putatively $p$-wave vortex matter and demonstrate the viability of engineering a new class of superconducting memory elements with ultralow-power switching, which could be transformative for cryogenic computing and quantum hardware.

</details>


### [21] [Possible Enhancement of Superconductivity in Ambient-Pressure La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ Thin Film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02685)
*Yichen Hua,Wenxin He,Jian-jian Miao,Changming Yue*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜超导体作为非常规超导系统，在常压下可达40K超导转变温度，已成为超导领域的研究热点，需要对其可能的配对机制进行进一步理论探索。

Method: 采用涨落交换（fluctuation exchange, FLEX）近似方法，系统分析La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜的双轨道双位点模型在弱关联区域的超导特性，重点关注其对空穴掺杂浓度的依赖性。

Result: 通过详细研究费米面拓扑结构发现，当d_z²轨道形成的δ口袋出现在Γ点附近时，其与γ口袋的嵌套以及α与β口袋间的嵌套共同增强了相应波矢处的s_±波配对。

Conclusion: 这种由嵌套驱动的自旋涨落诱导配对增强可能是增强超导性的可行机制，为理解La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜超导体的高转变温度提供了理论解释。

Abstract: As an unconventional superconducting system capable of reaching 40K under ambient pressure, the La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ film superconductor has become a recent focal point in the field of superconductivity, demanding further theoretical exploration of possible pairing mechanisms. In this work, we employ the fluctuation exchange (FLEX) approximation to systematically analyze the superconducting properties of the two-orbital, two-site model for the La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ film in the weakly correlated regime, focusing on its dependence on hole-doped concentration. Through a more detailed examination of the Fermi surface topology, we find that when a $δ$ pocket composed of the $d_{z^{2}}$ orbital emerges near the $Γ$-point, its nesting with the $γ$-pocket, along with the nesting between the $α$- and $β$-pockets, leads to a mutual enhancement of $s_{\pm}$-wave pairing at the corresponding wave vector. Furthermore, we propose that this nesting-driven enhancement of spin-fluctuation-induced pairing may be a viable mechanism to enhance superconductivity.

### [22] [Suppression of Spectral Gap and Flat Bands on a Cuprate Superconductor Side-Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03092)
*Gabriele Domaine,Mihir Date,Sydney K. Y. Dufresne,Natalie Lehmann,Daiyu Geng,Tohru Kurosawa,Amit Kumar,Jiaju Wang,Tianlun Yu,Chien-Ching Chang,Swosti P. Sarangi,Ding Pei,Yiran Liu,Julia Küspert,Shigemi Terakawa,Markel Pardo Almanza,Jiabao Yang,Izabela Biało,Matthew D. Watson,Timur K. Kim,Stephen M. Hayden,Kritika Singh,Banabir Pal,Matteo Minola,Johan Chang,Naoki Momono,Migaku Oda,Stuart S. P. Parkin,Andreas P. Schnyder,Niels B. M. Schröter*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究首次通过聚焦离子束铣削技术制备了铜氧化物超导体(110)侧表面，并利用角分辨光电子能谱观测其电子结构。研究发现超导能隙被抑制，但预期的零能平带峰也被抑制，这归因于高温超导体特有的体不均匀性（安德森型无序）而非表面几何粗糙度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物超导体的侧表面理论上应具有被抑制的d波序参数和零能拓扑平带，这些特性使其对对称性破缺序敏感。然而，由于高温超导体很少沿侧表面解理，这些表面从未被动量分辨、表面敏感的探测技术研究过。

Method: 采用聚焦离子束铣削（focused-ion-beam milling）技术定义可控的解理点，制备了过掺杂La₂₋ₓSrₓCuO₄ (x=0.22)的原始(110)侧表面，然后使用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission）进行测量。同时进行自洽Bogoliubov-de Gennes计算来模拟表面粗糙度和体不均匀性的影响。

Result: 观测到超导能隙在能量分辨率(~4 meV)内被抑制，但令人惊讶的是，预期的零能平带峰也被抑制，尽管表面具有高质量的地形特征。计算表明，解理表面的几何粗糙度太弱，不足以消除这些模式；而高温超导体特有的体不均匀性（建模为中等安德森型无序）可以将平带态展宽到无法检测的程度。

Conclusion: 该研究首次提供了铜氧化物侧表面的动量分辨电子结构视图，揭示了无序是当前阻碍平带及其相关关联序出现的关键因素。这一发现对于理解高温超导体表面态的实际观测条件具有重要意义。

Abstract: Side surfaces of cuprate superconductors are expected to display a suppressed $d$-wave order parameter and zero-energy topological flat bands with a large density of states, making them susceptible to symmetry broken orders. Yet such surfaces have never been investigated with momentum-resolved, surface-sensitive probes, because high-temperature superconductors rarely cleave along them. Using focused-ion-beam milling to define a controlled breaking point, we expose pristine (110) side surfaces of overdoped La$_{2-x}$Sr$_x$CuO$_4$ ($x=0.22$) suitable for angle-resolved photoemission. We observe the suppression of the superconducting spectral gap within our energy resolution ($\sim 4~\mathrm{meV}$), and surprisingly, the expected zero-energy flat band peak is also suppressed, despite the high topographic quality of the surface. Self-consistent Bogoliubov--de~Gennes calculations show that the measured geometric roughness of the cleaved surface is too weak to eliminate these modes. The calculations further demonstrate that bulk inhomogeneities characteristic of high-temperature superconductors, modelled as moderate Anderson-type disorder, can broaden the flat-band states beyond detectability. Our results provide the first momentum-resolved view of the electronic structure on a cuprate side surface and reveal disorder as the key factor currently preventing appearance of flat bands and their associated correlated orders.

</details>


### [23] [Fingerprint of $T_c$ advancement in Li-doped Bi-2223 superconductors prepared by cationic molecular mixing within Pechini sol-gel synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03124)
*N. K. Man,Huu T. Do,Nguyen V. Tu,Nguyen V. Quy*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种先进的溶胶-凝胶（sol-gel）合成方法，用于制备Li掺杂的Bi-2223超导体，避免了传统固相反应法的繁琐步骤。5 mol% Li掺杂样品表现出最高临界温度Tc = 111.4 K，并通过微观结构探测观察到了罕见的逐层晶体相生长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三层Bi-2223超导体在铋基铜酸盐中具有最高临界温度，是研究本征超导特性的理想原型。传统固相反应法虽然能制备高质量Bi-2223化合物，但涉及多次研磨、压制和煅烧步骤，过程繁琐且可能导致成分损失，因此需要寻找更简便的合成路径。

Method: 采用先进的溶胶-凝胶（sol-gel）合成方法，通过Pechini聚酯化路线实现金属阳离子的分子级混合，随后进行单步热解和烧结，制备了Li掺杂的Bi1.4Pb0.6Sr2Ca2(Cu1-xLix)3O10超导体（x = 0.0-0.20）。虽然单价Li⁺在Pechini方法中难以形成交联网络或螯合机制，但可作为探针阐明聚合过程中的主要化学过程。

Result: 5 mol% Li掺杂样品表现出最高临界温度Tc = 111.4 K，该结果通过交流磁化率和直流电阻率测量得到确认，与先前固相法制备的样品性能相当。研究还展示了在微观结构探测下观察到的罕见逐层晶体相生长现象，并通过低磁场宽频率范围的交流磁化率数据，利用Anderson-Müller模型和Cole-Cole图分析了量子磁通形成和磁通蠕变机制。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发了一种高效的溶胶-凝胶合成方法，用于制备Li掺杂的Bi-2223超导体，避免了传统固相反应法的繁琐性。该方法不仅获得了与固相法相当的临界温度，还提供了对晶体生长和超导机制的深入理解，为多组分复杂超导材料的合成提供了新途径。

Abstract: Trilayered Bi-2223 superconductor features the highest critical temperature $T_c$ among the bismuth-based cuprate collection and symbolizes an ideal prototype for studying intrinsic superconducting properties. The previous solid-state reaction method substantiated the growth of the high-quality Bi-2223 compounds but was accompanied by excessively laborious time and effort in terms of multiple grinding, pressing, as well as calcining stages, %causing risk of constituent loss, so finding a less tedious synthesis path is imperative. Here, we present an advanced sol-gel synthesis for assembling the multicomponent complexity of Bi1.4Pb0.6Sr2Ca2(Cu1-xLix)3O10 superconductors (Li-doped Bi-2223), with $x$ = 0.0--0.20, utilizing metallic cationic molecular mixing within the chemical Pechini polyesterization route followed by single-step pyrolysis and sintering stages. Although monovalent cations such as Li$^+$ pose limitations in establishing a perplex crosslinking network or chelating mechanism in the Pechini method, they represent a unique probe to elucidate the major chemical process during polymerization. We observe that a 5 molar~\% Li-doped sample pronounces the highest $T_c$ = 111.4 K among the series of samples, as confirmed by both ac susceptibility and dc resistivity measurements, and is equivalent to the value obtained by our preceding solid state fabrication. In addition, we showcase a rare observation of layer-by-layer crystalline phase growth under microstructure probe. Through analyzing the reliable ac susceptibility data at low magnetic fields in a wide range of frequency, we provide the quantum flux formation and flux creep mechanism by Anderson-Müller's model and Cole-Cole plot.

</details>


### [24] [Enhancing the Energy Resolution in Scanning Tunneling Microscopy: from dynamical Coulomb blockade to cavity quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03166)
*Xianzhe Zeng,Janis Siebrecht,Haonan Huang,Sujoy Karan,Joachim Ankerhold,Klaus Kern,Christian R. Ast*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过在低温扫描头集成局部电磁屏蔽和低通滤波，将扫描隧道显微镜在10mK温度下的能量分辨率提升至3.7μeV，并揭示了约瑟夫森电流与厘米尺度扫描头电磁腔模式的耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy）和扫描隧道谱学（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）在原子尺度探测凝聚态物质方面不可或缺，但在mK温度下，动态库仑阻塞（dynamical Coulomb blockade）机制通过隧穿电子与电磁环境的能量交换，从根本上限制了光谱精度。

Method: 研究通过在低温扫描头直接集成局部电磁屏蔽（local electromagnetic shielding）和低通滤波（low-pass filtering），有效抑制高频辐射并对隧道结进行电容分流（capacitive shunting）。

Result: 该方法将能量分辨率提升近一个数量级，在10mK温度下达到3.7μeV的基准值。改进的灵敏度揭示了约瑟夫森电流（Josephson current）与厘米尺度扫描头电磁腔模式（electromagnetic cavity modes）的耦合，建立了原子尺度隧穿过程与宏观腔量子电动力学（cavity quantum electrodynamics）的直接联系。

Conclusion: 这些进展为以前所未有的精度探索超低能量现象开辟了途径，实现了扫描隧道显微镜能量分辨率的显著提升，并揭示了微观隧穿过程与宏观电磁环境之间的量子耦合机制。

Abstract: Scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy have become indispensable tools for probing condensed matter at atomic length scales, yet achieving ultimate energy resolution remains a persistent challenge. At mK temperatures, the dynamical Coulomb blockade regime fundamentally limits spectroscopic precision through energy exchange between tunneling electrons and the electromagnetic environment. Here, we demonstrate that combining local electromagnetic shielding with low-pass filtering directly at the cryogenic scan head improves the energy resolution by nearly an order of magnitude, reaching benchmark values as low as 3.7$μ$eV at 10mK. We attribute this enhancement to efficient suppression of high-frequency radiation and capacitive shunting of the tunnel junction. Remarkably, this improved sensitivity reveals that the Josephson current couples to electromagnetic cavity modes of the centimeter-scale scan head, establishing a direct connection between atomic-scale tunneling processes and macroscopic cavity quantum electrodynamics. These advances open pathways for exploring ultra-low-energy phenomena with unprecedented precision.

</details>


### [25] [Emergent superconducting phases in unconventional $p$-wave magnets: Topological superconductivity, Bogoliubov Fermi surfaces and superconducting diode effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03221)
*Amartya Pal,Paramita Dutta,Arijit Saha*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该理论研究建立了p波磁体作为实现拓扑超导、Bogoliubov费米面和超导二极管效应的统一平台，揭示了丰富的非常规超导相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期发现的非常规动量依赖磁序扩展了磁性研究领域，其中p波磁体代表了一类新型奇宇称非共线补偿磁序，能够产生自旋分裂电子能带。本研究旨在探索p波磁体作为实现多种有趣超导相的平台潜力。

Method: 采用包含p波磁序、交换耦合和塞曼场的最小模型，进行自洽平均场分析。该方法在统一的微观框架下研究超导相变。

Result: 研究揭示了丰富的相图，包含非常规有限动量Fulde-Ferrell和Larkin-Ovchinnikov超导相。p波磁体可转变为拓扑超导相并锚定Majorana平边缘模，无需Rashba自旋轨道耦合和塞曼场。施加塞曼场后出现具有Bogoliubov费米面的无能隙FF和LO相，其特征是有限零能量准粒子态密度。非对称FF相中自然产生超导二极管效应。

Conclusion: p波磁体作为独特新颖的平台，能够承载拓扑超导相、无能隙超导态和非互易输运现象，为探索非常规超导物理提供了统一框架。

Abstract: The recent discovery of unconventional momentum-dependent magnetic orders has expanded the landscape of magnetism beyond conventional ferromagnetism and antiferromagnetism. Among them, $p$-wave magnets ($p$WMs) represent a novel class of odd-parity, non-collinear compensated magnetic order that generates spin-split electronic bands. In this work, our theoretical investigation establishes $p$WMs as a versatile platform for realizing intriguing superconducting phases including topological superconductivity (TSC), Bogoliubov Fermi surfaces (BFSs), and superconducting diode effect (SDE), within a unified microscopic framework. Employing a minimal model incorporating $p$-wave magnetic order, exchange coupling, and Zeeman fields, we perform a self-consistent mean-field analysis and uncover a rich phase diagram featuring unconventional finite-momentum Fulde-Ferrell (FF) and Larkin-Ovchinnikov (LO) superconducting phases. Remarkably, we also show that $p$WMs can undergo a transition to a TSC phase anchoring Majorana flat edge modes, a hallmark of two-dimensional TSCs, even without Rashba spin-orbit coupling and Zeeman field. Upon applying a Zeeman field, gapless FF and LO phases emerge with BFSs characterized by the appearance of finite zero-energy quasiparticle density of states. Furthermore, we demonstrate that SDE arises naturally in the asymmetric FF phase. Our analysis manifests that $p$WMs serve as a unique and novel platform to host TSC phase, gapless superconducting states, and non-reciprocal transport phenomena.

### [26] [Unraveling Lithium Dynamics in Solid Electrolyte Interphase: From Graph Contrastive Learning to Transport Pathways](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02284)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了GET-SEI通用框架：通过图对比学习（GCL）无预定义标签地发现局部原子环境；利用扩展动态模态分解（EDMD）建模锂跃迁动力学；采用过渡路径理论（TPT）量化反应性锂通量。

Conclusion: 随着新型高性能固态电解质不断涌现，GET-SEI为针对性SEI工程提供了一个广泛适用且可解释的工具，能够支持固态电池界面性能的优化设计。

However, a general framework for characterizing these distinct local environments and the associated transport mechanisms remains lacking. Here, we develop GET-SEI, a general framework that discovers local atomic environments without predefined labels through Graph contrastive learning (GCL), models lithium transition kinetics via Extended dynamic mode decomposition (EDMD), and quantifies reactive lithium flux through Transition path theory (TPT). Applied to different SSE/Li systems, including sulfides (Li6PS5Cl/Li, Li10GeP2S12/Li) and oxides (Li7La3Zr2O12/Li), the GET-SEI reveals dominant transport pathways and kinetic bottlenecks in each system, providing quantitative metrics for evaluating lithium transport efficiency. As novel high-performance SSEs continue to emerge, GET-SEI offers a widely applicable, interpretable tool for targeted SEI engineering.

### [27] [HERB: a unified framework for the evaluation of Hydrogen Embrittlement mechanisms driven by the Rice-Beltz concept](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02800)
*Kai Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个统一的多尺度氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement）理论框架HERB，该框架基于Rice-Beltz概念，整合了裂纹尖端附近的氢传输和塑性区内的空洞生长，将多种氢脆机制统一在一个理论中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement, HE）机制的多尺度图像长期存在争议，需要建立一个统一的理论框架来整合不同的失效机制。

Method: 建立了热力学一致的HERB框架，将Rice-Beltz模型与过渡态理论（transition state theory）结合，提出了预测氢影响位错发射的广义模型；在裂纹尖端前的无位错区（dislocation free zone）模拟氢传输，并考虑球形夹杂物捕获能的动态变化；将Hutchinson-Rice-Rosengren解与基于机制的应变梯度塑性理论（mechanism-based strain gradient plasticity model）结合，获得了几何必要位错（geometrically necessary dislocations）密度的半解析表达式。

Result: HERB理论仅通过裂纹尖端位错发射触发，统一了HEDE、HELP、NVC和HESIV等多种氢脆机制；研究表明氢影响的空洞动力学由位错密度主导，其行为介于Lifshitz-Allen-Cahn和Lifshitz-Slyozov-Wagner定律之间，尽管单个事件仍不可预测。

Conclusion: 该理论从根本上重塑了对氢/位错相互作用的多尺度理解，包括核心宽度（core width）、短程和长程水平，为解决氢脆机制争议提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: The multiscale picture of hydrogen embrittlement (HE) mechanisms has been under controversy for a long time. Here I report a thermomechanically-consistent HERB framework driven by the Rice-Beltz concept meanwhile incorporating the hydrogen transport near the crack-tip and void growth within the plastic zone. Triggered solely by dislocation emission from the crack tip, the HERB theory unifies multiple HE mechanisms, such as HEDE, HELP, NVC and HESIV within a single framework. Specifically, a generalized model for predicting the hydrogen-informed dislocation emission is established by incorporating the Rice-Beltz model with the transition state theory. Accounting for the dynamic variation of the trapping energy of spherical inclusions, hydrogen transport is modeled in the dislocation free zone in front of the crack tip. Semi-analytical expressions of the density of geometrically necessary dislocations are obtained by incorporating the Hutchinson-Rice-Rosengren solution with the conventional theory of mechanism-based strain gradient plasticity model. By exploring the feasibility of stochastic analysis, the present theory demonstrates that the hydrogen-informed void dynamics is dominated by the dislocation density between the limits of Lifshitz-Allen-Cahn and Lifshitz-Slyozov-Wagner laws, even though individual events remain unpredictable. These insights fundamentally reshape hydrogen/dislocation interactions across multiple scales, including the core width, short-range and long-range levels.

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了轨道自由度在轨道电子学中的核心作用，为基于过渡金属氧化物的下一代轨道电子学器件开发提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate the orbital-to-charge current conversion in Co$_{40}$Fe$_{40}$B$_{20}$\textbar CuO bilayers as a function of CuO thickness, employing orbital pumping via ferromagnetic resonance. The dynamic injection of orbital angular momentum into the CuO layer generates a transverse voltage through the Inverse Orbital Hall Effect (IOHE). By systematically varying the CuO thickness from 2 to 30~nm, we observe a pronounced dependence of the IOHE-induced voltage on the CuO layer thickness, indicating efficient orbital-to-charge conversion. These results highlight the key role of the orbital degree of freedom in orbitronics and provide insights into the potential of transition-metal oxides for next-generation orbitronic devices.

Here, we report the synthesis of a metallic polymeric nitrogen with one-dimensional feature (1D-PN) at 130-140 GPa and above 3000 K. Simulations predict a superconducting transition at 21.19 K under 113 GPa, higher than that reported in high-pressure experiments for non-metallic elements. At ambient pressure, this phase acquiring an energy density of as high as 8.78 kJ/g is not only kinetically stable but also thermodynamically more stable than cubic gauche nitrogen. This multifunctional property profile positions 1D-PN as a disruptive candidate for both electronic and energetic applications.

### [30] [Charge, Bonding, and Optical Properties of the B$_7$Ca$_2$ Cluster: An Alkaline-Earth Dimer Stabilized by a Single Boron Ring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02428)
*Peter Ludwig Rodríguez-Kessler*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论计算系统分析了B$_7$Ca$_2$硼团簇的电荷、成键和光学性质，发现钙原子通过电荷转移和多中心成键稳定芳香性硼环，为非过渡金属稳定硼团簇提供了范例。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The charge, bonding, and optical properties of the calcium-doped boron cluster B$_7$Ca$_2$ have been systematically investigated using density functional theory calculations. Extensive global basin-hopping searches identify a single-ring B$_7$ geometry stabilized by two calcium atoms symmetrically located on opposite sides of the boron ring as the global minimum. Electronic structure analysis reveals pronounced charge redistribution and strong Ca--B interactions that promote electron delocalization over the boron framework. Hirshfeld charge analysis indicates substantial electron donation from the electropositive calcium atoms to the electron-deficient B$_7$ ring, leading to effective electronic stabilization without the involvement of transition-metal $d$ orbitals. Optical absorption spectra further reflect the delocalized nature of the frontier electronic states. Real-space bonding analyses based on the electron localization function (ELF), Interaction Region Indicator (IRI), and the Laplacian of the electron density reveal a multicenter bonding pattern dominated by electron delocalization within the boron ring, with calcium acting primarily as an electrostatic and charge-donating stabilizer rather than forming localized two-center Ca--B bonds. These results establish B$_7$Ca$_2$ as a prototypical example of an alkaline-earth-metal-stabilized boron ring and highlight the ability of non-transition metals to stabilize aromatic boron clusters through charge transfer and multicenter bonding.

*Mohamed AbdulHameed,Benjamin Beeler*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，使用两种原子间势（interatomic potentials）来量化氮扩散和弗伦克尔对（Frenkel-pair）浓度，温度范围为1800-2600 K。

Conclusion: 氮亚晶格（nitrogen sublattice）无序为UN的高温热容提供了合理的本征机制，解释了观察到的超线性行为。

Abstract: The high-temperature heat capacity of uranium mononitride (UN) remains uncertain due to conflicting measurements and models above ~1700 K. To assess whether intrinsic defect formation contributes to the observed superlinear behavior of $C_P(T)$, we perform large-scale molecular dynamics simulations using two interatomic potentials to quantify nitrogen diffusion and Frenkel-pair populations from 1800--2600 K. Both models show increasing anion mobility, but the Tseplyaev potential yields substantially larger Frenkel concentrations, producing a defect heat-capacity contribution of up to ~10 J/(mol-K). This defect-driven term is consistent with the curvature seen in historical correlations and recent ab initio results, suggesting that nitrogen sublattice disorder provides a plausible intrinsic mechanism for the high-temperature heat capacity of UN.

### [32] [Thermal conductivity and tunable thermal anisotropy of magnetic CrSBr monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02444)
*Marta Loletti,Alejandro Molina-Sánchez,Juan Sebastián Reparaz,Xavier Cartoixà,Riccardo Rurali*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算研究了单层CrSBr（一种范德华磁性二维材料）的热导率，发现其存在显著的热各向异性（κ_xx/κ_yy ≈ 1.8），该各向异性源于声子速度和寿命的共同效应，并可通过调控薄片尺寸来调节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究单层CrSBr这种范德华（van der Waals）磁性二维材料的热导率特性，特别关注其热各向异性现象，这对于理解此类材料的传热行为及其潜在应用具有重要意义。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）方法，对单层CrSBr的热导率进行理论计算，分析其在不同方向上的热传输特性。

Result: 计算结果显示单层CrSBr存在显著的热各向异性，κ_xx/κ_yy比值约为1.8；该各向异性源于声子（phonon）速度和寿命的共同效应，并且可以通过控制薄片尺寸来调节，通过抑制长平均自由程（mean path）声子实现调控。

Conclusion: 单层CrSBr表现出明显的热各向异性，这种特性由声子动力学参数共同决定，且具有可调控性，为基于热各向异性的器件设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We present first-principles calculations of the thermal conductivity, ${\bm κ}$, of monolayer CrSBr, a van der Waals magnetic 2D material. We find a considerable thermal anisotropy, with a ratio $κ_{xx}/κ_{yy}$ of around 1.8. The anisotropy stems from a combined effect of phonon velocities and lifetimes and can be tuned by controlling the flake size by suppressing long mean path phonons.

</details>


### [33] [Strain-induced structural transitions in (111)-oriented (LaMnO$_3$)$_{2n}|$(SrMnO$_3$)$_n$ superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02448)
*Imran Ahamed,Shivalika Sharma,Fabrizio Cossu,Igor Di Marco*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算研究了(111)取向(LaMnO₃)₂ₙ|(SrMnO₃)ₙ超晶格(n=2,4,6)中由外延应变诱导的结构相变。所有超晶格在应变范围内均偏好半金属铁磁序，其中局域磁矩与体积呼吸畸变耦合。厚度在对外延应变的响应中起关键作用，特别是在氧八面体倾斜模式的变化上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究(111)取向(LaMnO₃)₂ₙ|(SrMnO₃)ₙ超晶格中外延应变诱导的结构相变，特别关注厚度(n=2,4,6)在决定氧八面体倾斜模式中的作用。探索强电子关联与结构效应之间的相互作用，特别是在不同应变条件下。

Method: 采用第一性原理电子结构计算(first-principles electronic structure calculations)方法，研究(111)取向的(LaMnO₃)₂ₙ|(SrMnO₃)ₙ超晶格，其中n=2,4,6。分析不同外延应变条件下超晶格的结构响应，特别关注氧八面体倾斜模式的变化。

Result: 所有超晶格在应变范围内均偏好半金属铁磁序(half-metallic ferromagnetic order)，局域磁矩与体积呼吸畸变(volume-breathing distortions)耦合。厚度n=2的超晶格始终采用a⁻a⁻a⁻倾斜模式，而a⁻a⁻c⁺模式仅在压缩应变下作为亚稳态存在。n=4的超晶格在平衡条件下偏好a⁻a⁻c⁺模式，但第三赝立方轴上的同相旋转非常脆弱，微小应变即可恢复a⁻a⁻a⁻模式。n=6的超晶格行为更复杂：压缩应变驱动从a⁻a⁻c⁺到a⁻a⁻a⁻的转变，而拉伸应变保持a⁻a⁻c⁺模式并显著增强两个不等价亚晶格间的结构差异。

Conclusion: 厚度在超晶格对外延应变的响应中起关键作用，影响氧八面体倾斜模式的选择和稳定性。在n=6超晶格的拉伸应变条件下，一个亚晶格中的Jahn-Teller畸变被抑制，导致增强的体积呼吸畸变和相应的电荷与自旋振荡。这表明在拉伸应变条件下，洪德物理(Hund's physics)可能更为相关，最大化了强电子关联与结构效应之间的相互作用。

Abstract: By means of first-principles electronic structure calculations, we hereby investigate the structural transitions induced by epitaxial strain in (111)-oriented (LaMnO$_3$)$_{2n}|$(SrMnO$_3$)$_n$ superlattices, with $n=2,4,6$. All superlattices in the explored range of strain are shown to prefer a half-metallic ferromagnetic order where the local magnetic moments are coupled to volume-breathing distortions. More in detail, our results reveal that thickness plays a crucial role in the response to epitaxial strain, which is particularly evident in the resulting tilt pattern of the oxygen octahedra. The thinnest superlattice, for $n=2$, always adopts the $a^-a^-a^-$ tilt pattern and the competing $a^-a^-c^+$ tilt pattern can be stabilized as a metastable state only in presence of compressive strain. Instead, the superlattice with $n=4$ favours the $a^-a^-c^+$ tilt pattern at equilibrium conditions, but the in-phase rotations around the third pseudocubic axis are so fragile that the $a^-a^-a^-$ pattern is recovered under a tiny amount of either compressive or tensile strain. The superlattice with $n=6$ exhibits a more nuanced behaviour: compressive strain drives a transition from $a^-a^-c^+$ to $a^-a^-a^-$, whereas tensile strain preserves the $a^-a^-c^+$ tilt pattern and significantly accentuates the structural differences between the two inequivalent sublattices within this symmetry. In fact, the Jahn-Teller distortions are quenched in one of the sublattices, leading to enhanced volume-breathing distortions and corresponding enhanced charge and spin oscillations. This suggests that Hund's physics may be more relevant in this regime of tensile strain, maximizing the interplay between strong electronic correlations and structural effects.

### [34] [A Nucleation Prediction Framework for Vapor-Deposited Metastable Polymorph](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02466)
*Hyeon Woo Kim,Han Uk Lee,Rohan Mishra,Sung Beom Cho*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于成核理论（nucleation theory）的框架，通过整合第一性原理反应能学（first-principles reaction energetics）和基底相互作用（substrate interactions），量化气相沉积（vapor deposition）过程中亚稳态多晶型（metastable polymorphs）的可及性，为从经验性发现转向理性设计提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气相沉积（vapor deposition）可用于合成具有新颖性质的亚稳态多晶型（metastable polymorphs），但由于缺乏连接热力学和过程动力学的预测性指导原则，相选择（phase selection）在很大程度上仍依赖经验。这阻碍了从经验性发现向理性设计的转变。

Method: 本文提出了一个基于成核理论（nucleation-based framework）的框架，将基于第一性原理的反应能学（first-principles-based reaction energetics）和基底相互作用（substrate interactions）整合到经典成核理论（classical nucleation theory）中。以Ga2O3为原型系统，识别反应驱动力（reaction driving force）作为控制多晶型成核和生长的关键动力学因素。

Result: 分析表明，具有大反应驱动力（large reaction driving force）的前驱体（precursors）在动力学上稳定了亚稳态α相（metastable α-phase），而低驱动力前驱体则允许热力学弛豫至稳定的β相（stable β-phase）。此外，前驱体流速（precursor flow rates）可放大过饱和度（supersaturation），拓宽动力学窗口以稳定难以获得的κ相（elusive κ-phase）。该框架在TiO2系统中得到进一步验证，正确预测了金红石（rutile）和锐钛矿（anatase）之间的竞争性成核。

Conclusion: 通过建立气相沉积过程中的定量可合成性窗口（quantitative synthesizability window），该框架实现了从亚稳态多晶型的经验性发现向基于第一性原理的理性设计（first-principles-informed rational design）的转变。

Abstract: Vapor deposition allows for the synthesis of metastable polymorphs with novel properties, yet phase selection remains largely empirical due to a lack of predictive guidelines bridging thermodynamics and process kinetics. Here, we present a nucleation-based framework that quantifies phase accessibility by integrating first-principles-based reaction energetics and substrate interactions into classical nucleation theory. Using Ga2O3 as a prototypical system, we identify the reaction driving force as a critical kinetic handle governing polymorph nucleation and growth. Our analysis reveals that precursors with a large reaction driving force kinetically stabilize the metastable α-phase, whereas low-driving-force precursors permit thermodynamic relaxation to the stable \b{eta}-phase. Furthermore, we demonstrate that precursor flow rates amplify supersaturation, widening the kinetic window to stabilize the elusive \k{appa}-phase. This framework is further validated in the TiO2 system, where it correctly predicts the competitive nucleation between rutile and anatase. By establishing a quantitative synthesizability window during vapor deposition, this framework enables a shift from empirical discovery to rational, first-principles-informed design of metastable phases.

Consequently, differences in predictive performance may arise not only from data or network design, but also from the underlying theoretical assumptions. By isolating the role of thermodynamic structure, we assess how restrictions such as duality, normality, operator-based evolution, and convexity influence learnability, expressiveness, stability, and generalization.

Abstract: The accumulation and growth of vacancy clusters under irradiation is a pivotal degradation mode for structural materials in extreme environments. Even tungsten undergoes rapid defect coarsening compromising its integrity. Here we show a tungsten multicomponent alloy that effectively fragments the vacancy diffusion network, kinetically trapping defects within localized domains. This effect originates from a broad spectrum of migration barriers and substantial vacancy-jump heterogeneity, which drives the interconnectivity of diffusion paths below the percolation threshold. To understand the role of nonmagnetic element Sn, we have investigated magnetic, transport, and electronic structure of the isostructural compound Co3SnInS2, where all the Sn (divalent) atoms in the Co3Sn Kagome layer are replaced by In (trivalent) atoms. We find long-range ferromagnetic order is nearly quenched in Co3SnInS2. The system exhibits predominantly antiferromagnetic correlations with only a very small net magnetic moment and turns ferromagnetic in the presence of an external magnetic field. Transport measurements show a semiconducting behaviour at low temperatures. Magnetoresistance shows a nonmonotonic field dependence, changing from negative to positive with increasing magnetic field. An anomalous Hall effect is observed, but its magnitude is significantly reduced compared to Co3Sn2S2 where the topological character of the Fermi surface plays a dominant role. These results indicate that substitution of Sn by In in the Co3Sn plane not only suppresses the topological electronic features of the transport electrons but drives the system away from the ferromagnetic Half-metallicity to an almost nonmagnetic semiconducting state with unusual paramagnetic response. Electronic structure calculations are consistent with some of these observations.

</details>


### [41] [Manipulating Charge Distribution in Moiré Superlattices by Light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02693)
*Ruiping Guo,Haowei Chen,Wenhui Duan,Yong Xu,Chong Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种针对莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattices）中二阶直流电荷响应的空间分辨理论，揭示了均匀光照射可驱动超晶胞内静态、空间非均匀的电荷重分布，这一效应普遍存在且不受晶体对称性限制。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固体中非线性光学响应通常基于晶胞平均研究，而莫尔超晶格因其大尺度特征，释放了常被忽视的自由度：局域可观测量在超晶胞内的空间变化。这为探索更丰富的非线性光学响应提供了新机遇。

Method: 研究者以空间分辨方式构建了二阶直流（direct current, DC）电荷响应理论，识别出发散解析响应系数的主导贡献，并将该理论应用于扭曲双层MoTe₂体系进行验证。

Result: 研究发现均匀光照射可驱动超晶胞内静态、空间非均匀的电荷重分布，该效应普遍存在且不受任何晶体对称性禁止。在无弛豫情况下，重分布呈现随时间线性增长的特征，由局域直流光电流的收敛或发散驱动。在扭曲双层MoTe₂中，该理论展示了由光强和频率控制的高度可调电荷调制。

Conclusion: 该工作强调了超晶胞内自由度的重要性，这些自由度使得莫尔超晶格中能够实现定性上更丰富的一类非线性光学响应，为原位全光学控制莫尔周期静电势开辟了新途径。

Abstract: In ordinary solids, nonlinear optical responses are typically studied in terms of unit-cell averages due to the angström-scale lattice constants. In contrast, moiré superlattices, characterized by a large length scale, unlock an often-overlooked degree of freedom: intra-supercell spatial variations of local observables. Here, we formulate the second-order direct current (DC) charge response in a spatially resolved manner, showing that even uniform optical illumination can drive a static, spatially non-uniform charge redistribution within a supercell. This effect is ubiquitous and cannot be forbidden by any crystalline symmetries. Furthermore, we identify a dominant contribution arising from diverging analytical response coefficients, which leads to linear-in-time growth of the redistribution in the absence of relaxation. This growth is driven by the convergence or divergence of local DC photocurrents. Applying our theory to twisted bilayer MoTe$_2$, we demonstrate strong, highly tunable charge modulation controlled by light intensity and frequency, opening a route to in situ, all-optical control of moiré-periodic electrostatic potentials. Our work underscores the importance of intra-cell degrees of freedom, which enable a qualitatively richer class of nonlinear optical responses in moiré superlattices.

Abstract: Rational design of interface passivators for perovskite solar cells is hindered by the entanglement of intrinsic molecular efficacy with extrinsic platform-dependent performance - a confounding factor that obscures true chemical advances. Trained on a curated dataset of 240 experimental entries, our model identifies hydrogen bond acceptor strength and electrostatic potential difference as key descriptors. Guided by these insights, we screened >121 million PubChem compounds using a hierarchical strategy integrating diversity clustering and uncertainty quantification. Here, we made a first step in the exploration by applying the Williamson-Hall (WH) analysis to X-ray diffraction data (XRD) measured in magnesium subjected to fast ramp compression at four pressures. In the result, we report the first microstructural evolution insights of magnesium under fast ramp compression.

Abstract: Reliable simultaneous optical sensing of pressure and temperature under extreme and dynamically fluctuating conditions remains a major challenge due to intrinsic cross-sensitivity between these two thermodynamic parameters. Multimodal systems enabling simultaneous yet fully decoupled monitoring of both parameters are therefore highly sought after. Here, we demonstrate that the synergistic interplay between Cr3+ and Ni2+ luminescence provides a platform for bifunctional temperature-pressure sensing with independent readout channels. Two complementary detection strategies were systematically investigated: ratiometric approach based on luminescence intensity ratio and kinetic approaches exploiting emission decay dynamics. Among the kinetic strategies, a time-gated dual-ion lifetime concept - introduced here for the first time for luminescence manometry - enables pressure readout with record-high relative sensitivity reaching 148.33% GPa-1 while exhibiting complete immunity to temperature fluctuations. Conversely, temperature sensing is achieved via time-gated single-ion Ni2+ luminescence, ensuring high thermometric performance with negligible pressure-induced interference. Importantly, this work study, for the first time, the potential of Ni2+ ions for application in near-infrared luminescence manometry. Abstract: Altermagnetism (AM) is an emerging magnetic order unifying essential characteristics of ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic states. Despite zero net magnetization, altermagnets (AMs) exhibit spin-split electronic bands and lifted altermagnon spin degeneracy. The altermagnet CrSb has attracted significant interest owing to its large spin-splitting energy. In this paper, we present the growth details of high-quality single crystals of CrSb using the self-flux method. We obtained large (001) oriented hexagonal crystals, up to 2 $\times$ 2.5 $\times$ 1 mm$^3$ in size. We investigated physical properties of the CrSb single crystals through measurements of electrical resistivity, magnetic susceptibility, and specific heat. The residual resistivity ratio (RRR) around 11 indicating the higher crystal quality than previous reports. A pronounced positive magnetoresistance of up to 80\% is observed at 3.5 K. The room temperature specific heat exceeds the Dulong-Petit limit due to a broad magnon contribution from the altermagnetic order. The charge accumulation in the diamond sectors can be neutralized by additional sub-threshold illumination, which generates charge carriers through internal photoeffect. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）研究Ti₃C₂和V₂C MXenes，评估了四种二维片层堆叠构型（four stacking configurations）和两种不同离子配位位点（ion coordination sites），以分析它们对离子嵌入和迁移的影响。

Result: 八面体堆叠（octahedral stacking）的O-端接层（O-terminated layers）表现出优异的结构稳定性，离子嵌入时层间距膨胀极小（V₂C中Al嵌入仅膨胀0.1埃）。虽然八面体堆叠能量上更有利，但相比棱柱堆叠（prismatic stacking）会降低离子迁移率。O-端接MXenes的理论比容量（theoretical specific capacities）超过270 mAh/g，而F-端接MXenes（F-terminated MXenes）在嵌入后极不稳定且容量显著降低。

Conclusion: 堆叠构型、端接基团（termination）和嵌入化学（intercalant chemistry）对MXenes在电池应用中的性能具有决定性影响。O-端接MXenes在八面体堆叠下展现出优异的稳定性和高容量特性，为设计高性能铝离子电池阴极材料提供了重要指导。

Abstract: As the energy storage ecosystem evolves beyond lithium, MXenes, a versatile family of 2D materials derived from MAX phases, have emerged as promising candidates for next-generation energy storage electrodes due to their tunable surface chemistry, large interlayer spacing, and excellent electronic conductivity. In this work, we use density functional theory to investigate Ti$_3$C$_2$ and V$_2$C MXenes as cathodes in Al-ion batteries. Four stacking configurations of the two-dimensional sheets and two different ion coordination sites are evaluated to understand their influence on ion intercalation and mobility. We find that the stacking configuration and surface chemistry critically impact interlayer spacing and electrochemical performance. O-terminated layers in an octahedral stacking exhibit remarkable structural stability with minimal interlayer expansion upon ion intercalation, particularly for Al intercalation in V$_2$C which exhibits an interlayer expansion of 0.1 angstrom, consistent with experimental findings. While octahedral stacking is observed to be energetically more favourable, it reduces ion mobility compared to prismatic stacking. Furthermore, O-terminated MXenes exhibit high theoretical specific capacities, reaching more than 270 mAh/g. F-terminated MXenes are considerably more unstable after intercalation and as a result exhibit much lower Al capacities. These findings highlight the importance of stacking configurations, termination and intercalant chemistry in MXenes for battery applications.

</details>


### [49] [Dynamical magnetic susceptibility of non-collinear magnets: A novel KKR-based ab initio scheme and its application](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03220)
*David Eilmsteiner,Arthur Ernst,Paweł A. Buczek*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker格林函数方法的线性响应含时密度泛函理论新实现，用于研究非共线磁体中的自旋激发，并应用于kagome非共线反铁磁体的磁振子研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种新的计算框架，用于处理非共线磁体中的自旋激发问题。传统方法在处理这类复杂磁结构时存在局限性，需要发展基于Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker格林函数方法的线性响应含时密度泛函理论实现。

Method: 方法基于线性响应含时密度泛函理论（linear response time-dependent density functional theory），采用Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker格林函数方法（Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker Green's function method）。理论框架基于绝热局域自旋密度近似（adiabatic local spin density approximation）的交换关联核，并推广到非共线情况。

Result: 该方法成功研究了kagome非共线反铁磁体代表性成员的磁振子性质，包括色散关系、朗道阻尼（Landau damping）和空间形状。同时从形式理论和数值收敛角度详细阐述了非共线磁化率计算中Goldstone模的形成。

Conclusion: 本文提出的计算方案为研究非共线磁体中的自旋激发提供了有效的理论框架和数值实现，特别适用于kagome晶格等复杂磁结构的磁振子性质分析。

Abstract: A novel implementation of the linear response time-dependent density functional theory addressing spin excitations in non-collinear magnets based on the Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker Green's function method is presented. Following the exposition of the formalism based on the adiabatic local spin density approximation to the exchange-correlation kernel generalized to the non-collinear case, the computational scheme is discussed in detail. The formation of the Goldstone modes in non-collinear susceptibility calculations is elaborated on formally and from the numerical convergence point of view. The scheme is deployed to study the dispersion, Landau damping, and spatial shapes of magnons for the representative members of the kagome non-collinear antiferromagnets.
