However, we lack the experimental tools to directly access the electric field of light in the sample plane of an optical microscope. Here, we introduce an all-optical imaging modality that resolves the electric field of light in the plane of a traditional widefield transmission optical microscope with 100-attosecond temporal and 200-nanometer spatial resolution. With this we demonstrate the delayed buildup of scattering contrast and pulse broadening through and around a thick MoTe2 flake - dynamics inaccessible via standard simulations. We showcase our technique's versatility by additionally resolving the full in-plane vector electric field lines during photoexcitation as the optical pulse propagates through and around the MoTe2 flake.

### [51] [High-Stress Si3N4 Reflective Membranes Monolithically Integrated with Cavity Bragg Mirrors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02490)
*Megha Khokhar,Lucas Norder,Paolo M. Sberna,Richard A. Norte*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用单片式晶圆级集成策略，通过无缺陷非晶硅牺牲层和无粘附等离子体刻蚀，将高应力Si3N4光子晶体薄膜直接悬浮在热兼容的SiN/SiO2分布式布拉格反射镜（DBRs）上方，形成亚微米间距的自对准谐振腔。

Yet their integration into high-finesse optical cavities has remained difficult, typically requiring bonding or alignment-sensitive assembly that limits scalability and long-term stability. Here, we introduce a monolithic, wafer-level integration strategy that directly suspends high-stress Si3N4 photonic-crystal membranes above thermally compatible SiN/SiO2 distributed Bragg reflectors (DBRs) capable of withstanding the high temperatures required for stoichiometric Si3N4 growth. A defect-free amorphous-silicon sacrificial layer and stiction-free plasma undercut yield vertically coupled cavities with sub-micron spacing-forming self-aligned resonators within seconds of release. Owing to the intrinsic tensile stress, the suspended membranes exhibit atomic-scale sagging, ensuring near-ideal cavity parallelism and long-term stability. Optical reflectivity measurements reveal cavity finesse exceeding 800 with nanoscale gaps between mirrors. Mechanical ringdown measurements show Q > 10^5, indicating that DBR integration preserves the low-dissipation character of high-stress Si3N4. This demonstrates that the integration process preserves the material's exceptional dissipation dilution, supporting straightforward extension to high-Q nanomechanical architectures reported in the literature. The resulting Si3N4-DBR platform unites optical and mechanical coherence with high fabrication yield and design flexibility, enabling scalable optomechanical devices for precision sensing and quantum photonics.

### [52] [One-point energy correlator for deep inelastic scattering at small $x$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02300)

TL;DR: 本文推导了深度非弹性散射中单点能量关联函数（OPEC）在色玻璃凝聚体框架下的高能极限表达式，该函数作为能量流与靶质子/核之间夹角的函数，能够系统探索散射过程中的不同动量尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过单点能量关联函数（one-point energy correlator, OPEC）提供对小x区域胶子饱和动力学（gluon saturation dynamics）的干净直接探测，特别是在未来电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider）相关运动学配置下。

Method: 方法基于色玻璃凝聚体（Color Glass Condensate, CGC）框架，在深度非弹性散射的高能（小x）极限下推导OPEC表达式。利用动量求和规则（momentum sum rule）消除了碎裂函数（fragmentation functions）的依赖，仅保留偶极振幅（dipole amplitude）作为非微扰输入。

Result: 数值结果显示，在未来电子-离子对撞机相关的代表性运动学配置下，存在显著的核抑制效应（nuclear suppression effects），并且该可观测量对饱和现象（saturation phenomena）表现出高度敏感性。

Conclusion: 结论表明，单点能量关联函数（OPEC）为小x区域胶子饱和动力学提供了干净直接的研究探针，其作为能量流与靶粒子夹角函数的特性，能够系统探索散射过程中的不同动量尺度。

Abstract: We derive the expressions for the one-point energy correlator (OPEC) in deep inelastic scattering in the high-energy (small-$x$) limit within the Color Glass Condensate framework. The OPEC is computed as a function of the angle between the energy flow and the target proton or nucleus, enabling a systematic exploration of different momentum scales in the scattering process. Owing to the momentum sum rule, the dependence on fragmentation functions cancels, leaving the dipole amplitude as the only nonperturbative input. As a result, the OPEC provides a clean and direct probe of gluon saturation dynamics at small $x$. We present numerical results for representative kinematic configurations relevant to the future Electron--Ion Collider, demonstrating sizable nuclear suppression effects and highlighting the sensitivity of this observable to saturation phenomena.

Method: 采用开放量子系统（open quantum systems）框架重新表述中微子-标量动力学。通过建立完整模型与唯象退相干方法之间的映射，分析超轻标量场导致的中微子质量矩阵时空依赖偏移如何引起退相干效应。

Abstract: We examine decoherence in neutrino oscillations induced by an ultralight scalar field coupled to neutrinos. Neutrinos sample different field configurations throughout an experimental data-taking period, which leads to damping effects in the oscillation pattern in the form of decoherence. By recasting the neutrino-scalar dynamics within the open quantum systems framework, we establish a mapping between a complete model and phenomenological decoherence approaches. We find that the parameter driving decoherence scales as $L^2/E^2$, where $L$ is the baseline and $E$ is the neutrino energy, as opposed to $L/E$ typically assumed in phenomenological studies of open system approaches to neutrino oscillations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LHC上三重极化WWW事件的产生特性，特别是三重纵向极化（triply-longitudinal, LLL）分额的精确计算，这对于检验标准模型（Standard Model）和探索新物理具有重要意义。

Method: 采用领头阶（leading order）计算，考虑完全轻子衰变（fully leptonic decays），使用标准模型理论框架，并开发了新的三玻色子过程壳上映射（on-shell mapping）方法用于极化截面计算。

Result: 对于W-W+W+过程，三重横向极化（triply-transverse）分额约为51%，而三重纵向极化（LLL）分额最小仅为1.4%；不同极化振幅间的干涉效应为+1.8%。W+W-W-过程结果类似。基于双玻色子过程的高阶结果，辐射修正不会显著提高LLL分额。

Conclusion: 三重纵向极化（LLL）分额极低（约1.4%），且辐射修正不会使其提升至百分之几十的水平，因此在LHC上测量LLL截面将极具挑战性。新开发的壳上映射方法为三玻色子极化截面计算提供了关键工具。

Abstract: We present first results for triply polarized $WWW$ events at the LHC. The calculation is performed at leading order for fully leptonic decays using the Standard Model. Employing an inclusive kinematic cut setup, we found that the triply-transverse polarization fraction is about $51\%$, while the triply-longitudinal (LLL) fraction is smallest with $1.4\%$ for the $W^-W^+W^+$ process. The interference between different polarization amplitudes amounts to $+1.8\%$. Results for the $W^+W^-W^-$ case are similar. Based on known higher-order results for the diboson processes, radiative corrections are not expected to increase the LLL fraction to the level of tens of percent. This means that measuring the LLL cross section at the LHC will be very challenging. A new on-shell mapping for triboson processes, being a crucial element of polarized cross-section calculation, is also presented.

### [57] [Radiative Corrections in Supergravity Models of Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02389)
*John Ellis,Tony Gherghetta,Kunio Kaneta,Wenqi Ke,Keith A. Olive*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文分析了超引力（supergravity）框架下类Starobinsky暴胀模型的辐射修正效应，发现部分模型在暴胀场较大时辐射修正会主导动力学，但识别出一类模型（包括Cecotti模型）在暴胀场值小于8普朗克单位时辐射修正很小，保持了与CMB观测数据的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超引力为早期宇宙宇宙学提供了自然的超对称框架，许多无标度超引力（no-scale supergravity）暴胀模型在树层级给出了与Starobinsky模型相似的宇宙微波背景（CMB）观测预言。然而，需要分析辐射修正对这些模型预测可靠性的影响。

Method: 利用全局超对称（global supersymmetry）和超引力的结果，分析了具有规范和非规范动能项的模型的辐射修正，特别关注类Starobinsky无标度超引力模型。推导了保持引力微子质量（gravitino mass）在暴胀期间有限的条件，并确保卡勒势（Kähler potential）的圈图修正相对于树层级势能保持有限或次要。

Result: 研究发现，在某些模型中（特别是具有Wess-Zumino超势的原始无标度超引力模型），辐射修正在大暴胀场值时增长并可能主导暴胀动力学，使模型对CMB数据的预测不可靠。然而，识别出一类无标度类Starobinsky模型（包括Cecotti模型），在暴胀场值小于8普朗克单位时辐射修正非常小。

Conclusion: 在暴胀场值小于8普朗克单位的条件下，特定类Starobinsky无标度超引力模型（如Cecotti模型）的辐射修正保持很小，从而保持了树层级预测与Planck CMB数据的一致性，确保了这些模型预测的可靠性。

Abstract: Supergravity provides the natural supersymmetric framework for early universe cosmology. A broad class of inflationary models in no-scale supergravity yields tree-level predictions for cosmic microwave background (CMB) observables that closely resemble those of the Starobinsky $R + R^2$ model. Using results from global supersymmetry and supergravity, we analyze radiative corrections in models with canonical and non-canonical kinetic terms, focusing particularly on Starobinsky-like no-scale supergravity models. We derive conditions on the superpotential that keep the gravitino mass finite during inflation and ensure that loop-induced corrections to the Kähler potential remain either finite or subdominant relative to the tree-level potential. We show that in some models, most notably the original no-scale supergravity model with a Wess-Zumino superpotential, radiative corrections grow at large inflaton field values and can dominate the inflationary dynamics, rendering unreliable the model predictions for CMB data. However, we identify a class of no-scale Starobinsky-like models, including the Cecotti model, in which radiative corrections remain very small for inflaton field values $\lesssim 8$ (in Planck units), preserving the agreement of the tree-level predictions with Planck CMB data.

</details>


### [58] [Probing Planck-Scale Physics with High-Frequency Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02493)
*Stefano Profumo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出通过蒸发近普朗克质量原初黑洞产生的随机引力波背景测试量子引力理论的新框架。由于引力子自由传播而不发生再散射，它们保留了黑洞温度-质量关系T(M)的直接光谱记录，而其他霍金辐射粒子则因快速热化而丢失该信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种测试量子引力理论的新方法。传统方法难以直接探测普朗克尺度物理，而蒸发中的近普朗克质量原初黑洞产生的随机引力波背景可能提供独特的观测窗口，因为引力子能够保留黑洞温度-质量关系的原始光谱信息。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）建立理论框架，将六个代表性量子引力理论（广义不确定性原理、圈量子引力、非对易几何、渐近安全、弦/哈格多恩物理、隧穿反作用）转化为不同的T(M)参数化形式；2）数值计算相应的引力波光谱；3）分析不同后暴胀时期早期宇宙条件的影响。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）抑制T(M)的修正模型可将光谱峰值频率移动多达十个数量级，部分情况下进入下一代干涉仪或共振腔探测器的敏感频段；2）施加硬蒸发截断的模型产生独特的光谱峰值形态，可用于区分不同量子引力方案；3）标准霍金预测与修正模型之间的相对光谱位移与宇宙学无关。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，随机引力波背景的光谱形状而非绝对峰值频率提供了探测普朗克尺度物理的最清晰探针。该方法为区分不同量子引力理论提供了新的观测途径，且结果具有宇宙学独立性，增强了其作为量子引力测试工具的可靠性。

Abstract: We develop a framework for testing quantum gravity through the stochastic gravitational-wave background produced by evaporating near-Planck-mass primordial black holes. Because gravitons free-stream from the emission region without rescattering, they preserve a direct spectral record of the black-hole temperature--mass relation $T(M)$, a relation that is erased for all other Hawking-radiated species by rapid thermalization. We translate six representative phenomenological beyond-semiclassical frameworks (the generalized uncertainty principle, loop quantum gravity, noncommutative geometry, asymptotic safety, string/Hagedorn physics, and tunneling backreaction) into distinct $T(M)$ parametrizations and compute the resulting gravitational wave spectra numerically. Modifications that suppress $T(M)$ shift the spectral peak by up to ten decades in frequency, in some cases into the sensitivity bands of next-generation interferometers or resonant-cavity detectors, while models imposing a hard evaporation cutoff produce distinctive peak morphologies that discriminate between quantum-gravity scenarios. We further discuss the impact of different choices for post-inflationary conditions in the very early universe. We find that the relative spectral displacement between the standard Hawking prediction and any modified model is cosmology-independent, hence spectral shape rather than absolute peak frequency provides the cleanest probe of Planck-scale physics.

</details>


### [59] [Nonlinear physics of axion inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02570)
*Oleksandr Sobol,Richard von Eckardstein,Elias Koch,Svetlana Gurevich,Uwe Thiele,Kai Schmitz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过梯度展开形式（gradient-expansion formalism）对轴子-规范场耦合系统进行参数扫描，发现了在强反作用（backreaction）下Anber-Sorbo解保持稳定的新参数区域，并识别出超临界Hopf分岔（supercritical Hopf bifurcation）和非平凡极限环（limit cycle）等非线性动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子类场（axion-like field）与阿贝尔规范场（Abelian gauge field）耦合提供了最简单的暴胀模型之一，该模型避免了eta问题并具有高效的重加热机制。对于足够大的耦合，系统进入强规范场反作用（strong gauge-field backreaction）区域，展现出丰富而复杂的动力学行为。

Method: 采用半解析方法——梯度展开形式（gradient-expansion formalism）进行全面的参数扫描，确定反作用（backreaction）发生的精确条件。研究局限于均匀轴子场和仅依赖时间的扰动，但在玩具模型（de Sitter时空、恒定势能斜率、无轴子梯度）中进一步研究了反作用区域解的非线性行为。

Result: 在扩展参数空间中发现了一个新区域，其中Anber-Sorbo解在强反作用（backreaction）下保持稳定，这代表了稳定反作用（stable backreaction）这一独特类型。在玩具模型中识别出不稳定起始点的超临界Hopf分岔（supercritical Hopf bifurcation）、不稳定区域中的非平凡极限环（nontrivial limit cycle）以及爆发式振荡动力学（burst-like oscillatory dynamics）。

Conclusion: 基于跨越不稳定阈值，提出了更严格的（不稳定）反作用起始判据，并将该判据应用于两个基准暴胀模型。尽管分析限于均匀场和仅时间依赖的扰动，但预期这种稳定性性质可外推至一般时空依赖扰动。

Abstract: An axion-like field coupled to an Abelian gauge field provides one of the simplest inflationary models that is free from the eta problem and possesses an efficient reheating mechanism. For sufficiently large coupling, this system enters a regime of strong gauge-field backreaction, exhibiting rich and intricate dynamics. In this work, we employ a semi-analytical method, the gradient-expansion formalism, to perform a comprehensive parameter scan and determine the precise conditions under which backreaction sets in. Previous studies have shown that the Anber-Sorbo solution, in which the potential-gradient force acting on the axion is balanced by Hubble friction and gauge-field backreaction, is unstable. Here, we broaden the parameter space and identify a new region in which the Anber-Sorbo solution remains stable despite strong backreaction. Although our analysis is restricted to a homogeneous axion field and to perturbations that depend only on time, we expect that this stability property can be extrapolated to generic time- and space-dependent perturbations. This newly identified region therefore represents a distinct type of backreaction - stable backreaction - which may not be accompanied by the rapid growth of perturbations. We further investigate the nonlinear behavior of solutions in the backreaction regime in a toy model (de Sitter, constant potential slope, no axion gradients), identifying a supercritical Hopf bifurcation at the onset of instability, a nontrivial limit cycle in the unstable regime, and burst-like oscillatory dynamics. Finally, we present a more stringent criterion for the onset of (unstable) backreaction, based on crossing the instability threshold, and apply this criterion to two benchmark inflationary models.

</details>


### [60] [Magnetic monopoles and high frequency gravitational waves from quasi-stable strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02996)
*Rinku Maji,Qaisar Shafi*

Main category: hep-ph

Method: 通过分析SO(10)对称性破缺路径：一条通过翻转SU(5)到标准模型，另一条通过SU(4)_c×SU(2)_L×SU(2)_R子群，研究磁单极子-反磁单极子对被弦束缚合并形成拓扑稳定磁单极子的机制，并计算其宇宙学演化。

Abstract: The spontaneous breaking of $SO(10)$ via flipped $SU(5)$ to the Standard Model yields a novel scenario in which the superheavy topologically stable GUT monopole carrying a single unit ($2π/e$) of Dirac magnetic charge emerges from the merger of a confined but topologically distinct monopole-antimonopole pair that are pulled together by a string. The $SO(10)$ breaking via the subgroup $SU(4)_c\times SU(2)_L\times SU(2)_R$, following a similar reasoning, produces a topologically stable monopole that carries two units ($4π/e$) of Dirac charge. We explore the cosmological consequences of this scenario by assuming that the monopoles and strings experience a limited number of inflationary $e$-foldings, before re-entering the horizon and ultimately forming a network of quasi-stable strings bounded by monopole-antimonopole pairs. We identify regions of the parameter space that yield an observable number density of the GUT monopole from the collapse of the appropriate string segments. The gravitational waves emitted by these quasi-stable cosmic strings lie in the Hz to kHz range, which can be tested in a number of proposed and ongoing experiments.

### [61] [Radius-Flow Entanglement in Hadron States and Gravitational Form Factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03064)
*Kiminad A. Mamo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种适用于格点QCD（lattice QCD）强子的纠缠观测量：真空减除的球Rényi熵半径流（vacuum-subtracted radius flow of the ball Rényi entropy），并基于此构建了边界主导性（boundary dominance）的格点稳定性测试框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为QCD强子开发一种可直接在格点上计算的纠缠观测量，以探究强子内部纠缠结构及其与引力形状因子（gravitational form factors）的联系，从而测试边界主导性假设。

Method: 方法核心是定义真空减除的球Rényi熵半径流 $\mathfrak{s}_n(R;h)$，该量通过欧几里得副本切割-粘合构造（Euclidean replica cut-and-glue construction）在静止系动量投影的单强子态中定义。通过将测量流在局部半径窗口上拟合到低曲率余项（low-curvature remainder）加上由强子引力形状因子构建的小模板基（template basis），来测试边界主导性。

Result: 对于典型的核子偶极子输入，纯端点模板预测了不同的单极值尺度：$R_{\rm EE}^{(0)}\sim0.84~\mathrm{fm}$ 和 $R_{\rm EE}^{(2)}\sim0.43~\mathrm{fm}$。这允许通过转折点位置、跨越转折点的斜率符号变化以及拟合的模板权重比，来区分标量控制、自旋-2控制和真正的混合情况。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的纠缠观测量和测试框架为在格点QCD中研究强子纠缠结构提供了新工具，能够有效区分不同引力形状因子对纠缠结构的贡献模式，并通过与软壁AdS/QCD（soft-wall AdS/QCD）模型的比较提供基准。

Abstract: We propose a lattice-ready entanglement observable for QCD hadrons: the vacuum-subtracted radius flow of the ball Rényi entropy, $\mathfrak{s}_n(R;h)\equiv R\,\partial_RΔS_n(B_R;h)$, defined via the Euclidean replica cut-and-glue construction in a rest-frame momentum-projected one-hadron state, with spin averaging performed at the level of the final flow. In the continuum, varying $R$ at fixed shape is equivalent to a Weyl rescaling, so the flow is trace selected and admits a surface-plus-remainder organization on the entangling sphere. We use this to formulate a lattice stability test of boundary dominance: fit the measured flow on local $R$ windows to a low-curvature remainder plus a small template basis built from hadronic gravitational form factors (GFFs). The two endpoint templates are the spin-0/trace shape $\mathfrak{t}_h^{(0)}(R)=R^3ρ_S(R)$ constructed from $A^S(t)$ and a spin-2/TT proxy $\mathfrak{t}_h^{(2)}(R)=R^3ρ_A(R)$ constructed from $A(t)$, together with the mixed family $\mathfrak{t}_h^{\rm mix}(R;c_0,c_2)=c_0\mathfrak{t}_h^{(0)}(R)+c_2\mathfrak{t}_h^{(2)}(R)$. A soft-wall AdS/QCD appendix shows that the pole-subtracted integrated trace--energy correlator closes on this same $\{A^S,A\}$ basis and supplies a model-dependent benchmark ratio for $c_0/c_2$; for lattice comparison the coefficients are left free and extracted from data. For representative nucleon dipole inputs, the pure endpoints predict distinct single-extremum scales, $R_{\rm EE}^{(0)}\sim0.84~\mathrm{fm}$ and $R_{\rm EE}^{(2)}\sim0.43~\mathrm{fm}$, enabling discrimination among scalar control, spin-2 control, and genuine mixing through the turning-point location, the sign change of the slope across it, and the fitted ratio of template weights.

### [62] [Absence of ballistic motion and presence of almost-ballistic motion for unitary operators with pure point spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03114)
*Christopher Cedzich,Jake Fillman,Luis Velázquez*

TL;DR: 该研究将Simon等人的两个结果推广到离散时间酉动力学（discrete-time unitary dynamics）框架，证明纯点谱（pure point spectrum）可排除弹道运动（ballistic motion），并通过扩展CMV矩阵（extended CMV matrices）的示例族表明该结论在该类系统中是尖锐的。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扩展Cantero-Moral-Velázquez（CMV）矩阵作为研究工具，在离散时间酉动力学框架下分析纯点谱与弹道运动之间的制约关系。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）证明纯点谱可排除弹道运动；2）构造扩展CMV矩阵的示例族，展示存在同时具有纯点谱且量子动力学可任意接近弹道运动的系统，表明该排除关系在扩展CMV矩阵类中是尖锐的。

Conclusion: 研究结论是纯点谱确实限制了弹道运动，但这种限制在扩展CMV矩阵框架下是尖锐的，即存在边界情况使系统可无限接近弹道运动。

Abstract: We adapt two results of Simon and collaborators to the setting of discrete-time unitary dynamics. We show that pure point spectrum precludes ballistic motion, and exhibit a family of examples showing that this is sharp within the class of extended Cantero--Moral-Velázquez (CMV) matrices: that is, there exist extended CMV matrices exhibiting pure point spectrum together with quantum dynamics as close to ballistic motion as one desires.

### [63] [Probing Axions with Relativistic Jet Polarimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03244)
*Dashon Michel Jones,Richard Anantua,Razieh Emami,Nate Lujan*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究利用事件视界望远镜（EHT）的偏振观测，首次探索了M87星系相对论性喷流作为轴子（axion）探测器的潜力，发现特定质量范围的轴子能产生可观测的偏振角旋转，并建立了区分轴子诱导双折射与等离子体法拉第旋转的形态学诊断框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子（axion）作为强CP问题的暗物质候选者，其与光子的耦合会在线性偏振辐射中产生频率无关的双折射（birefringence）。先前研究仅关注黑洞吸积盘附近的轴子信号，而M87的相对论性喷流（relativistic jet）提供了穿过暗物质分布的更长路径，却尚未被探索作为轴子探测器。

Method: 研究采用静止、轴对称、自相似的喷流模型，以及M87星系中心相干、均匀的孤子核（soliton core）作为轴子背景。在230 GHz频率下，针对代表性耦合范围$g_{aγ} \sim 5 \times 10^{-15} - 5 \times 10^{-14} GeV^{-1}$，分析轴子对相对论性喷流斯托克斯图（Stokes maps）的影响。

Result: 研究发现$10^{-21} eV$质量范围的轴子能产生度级到多度的电矢量位置角（EVPA）旋转，在某些情况下超过典型的EHT测量不确定度；而$10^{-22} eV$质量范围的轴子主要产生亚度级旋转。研究还建立了一套形态学诊断方法，用于区分轴子诱导的双折射与等离子体法拉第旋转（Faraday rotation）。

Conclusion: M87的相对论性喷流为探测轴子提供了新的观测窗口，特定质量范围的轴子能产生可被EHT观测到的偏振信号。建立的诊断框架为在分辨喷流偏振测量中区分轴子效应与等离子体效应提供了系统性方法。

Abstract: The prospect of identifying axion signals due to axion-photon coupling induced changes to the polarization has now become a reality in view of near-horizon polarimetric observations by the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT). Axion-like particles (ALPs), motivated as dark matter candidates by the strong CP problem, induce frequency-independent birefringence in linearly polarized radiation, producing observable rotations of the electric vector position angle. While previous studies have focused exclusively on axion signatures in near-horizon accretion disk emission, the relativistic jet of M87 -- extending from 10 gravitational radii to kiloparsec scales -- remains unexplored as an axion probe despite offering extended path lengths through the putative dark matter distribution. In this study, we investigate the effects of an axion cloud around the jet in M87 on the Stokes maps of relativistic jets using a stationary, axisymmetric, self-similar model for the jet and a coherent, homogeneous soliton core in M87's galactic center for the axion background. At 230 GHz, for representative couplings in range $g_{a γ} \sim 5 \times 10^{-15} - 5 \times 10^{-14} GeV^{-1}$, we find that axion masses in the $10^{-21} eV $ range produce degree-level to multi-degree EVPA rotations, in some cases exceeding typical EHT measurement uncertainties, whereas masses in the $10^{-22} eV$ range yield predominantly sub-degree rotations. We identify a suite of morphological diagnostics that together constitute a framework for distinguishing axion-induced birefringence from plasma Faraday rotation in resolved jet polarimetry.

### [64] [Flow Subgraphs and Flow Network Design under End-to-End Power Dissipation Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02336)
*Zhihao Qiu,Xinhan Liu,Rogier Noldus,Piet Van Mieghem*

TL;DR: 该研究探讨网络图如何支持源节点与目标节点间的流传输，提出计算随机图中参与传输的节点与链路期望数量的方法。研究进一步解决如何在给定端到端功耗约束下构建图的问题，提出一种称为"电阻间隙剪枝"的启发式算法，能生成稀疏图以近似满足需求有效电阻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解网络底层图如何支持节点间的流传输，并量化随机图中参与传输的节点与链路的期望数量。同时关注与传输相关的"成本"或"功耗耗散"问题，探索如何在预定端到端功耗约束下构建合适的网络图。

Method: 研究方法包括计算随机图中参与传输的节点与链路的期望数量，并将预定功耗约束下的图构建问题简化为"逆有效电阻问题"。提出启发式算法"电阻间隙剪枝"，该算法通过剪枝操作生成稀疏加权图，使其有效电阻矩阵近似等于预定需求矩阵。

Result: 研究结果表明，电阻间隙剪枝算法能够生成稀疏图，这些图能紧密近似需求有效电阻。该算法在不同需求场景下表现出稳定的性能，为解决逆有效电阻问题提供了有效工具。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了分析网络图支持流传输能力的框架，并提出了解决逆有效电阻问题的实用算法。电阻间隙剪枝算法在保持图稀疏性的同时，能够有效近似预定功耗约束，为网络设计与优化提供了新方法。

Abstract: We investigate how the underlying graph of a network supports a flow between a source node and a destination node and propose to compute the expected number of nodes and links that contribute to transferring items in random graphs. Since the transportation is associated with a \quotes{cost} or \quotes{power dissipation}, we further address how to construct a graph given predetermined end-to-end power dissipation, which can be reduced to the \quotes{inverse effective resistance problem} that asks for a weighted graph in which the effective resistance matrix equals a predetermined demand matrix. We propose a heuristic algorithm, \quotes{Resistor Gap Pruning} (RGP), which provides sparse graphs closely approximating the demand effective resistance and which shows stable performance across different demand scenarios.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立曲率线参数化曲面的新离散化方法，该方法推广了现有的圆形网（circular nets）、圆锥网（conical nets）和主接触元网（principal contact element nets）等离散化方案。

Result: 结果表明主双网构成离散可积系统（discrete integrable system），具有多维一致性，并能推广到高维方格晶格$\Z^N$。同时建立了与离散正交坐标系（discrete orthogonal coordinate systems）和离散共焦二次曲面（discrete confocal quadrics）概念的联系。

Conclusion: 主双网为曲率线参数化曲面提供了新的离散化框架，具有可积系统特性，并与现有离散几何结构存在理论联系，为离散微分几何研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: Principal binets are a discretization of curvature line parametrized surfaces defined on the vertices and faces of the square lattice $\Z^2$. They generalize the previously established discretizations given by circular nets, conical nets, and principal contact element nets. We show that principal binets constitute a discrete integrable system in the sense of multi-dimensional consistency. In particular, they generalize to higher-dimensional square lattices $\Z^N$. We also discuss relations to the notion of discrete orthogonal coordinate systems as previously established for discrete confocal quadrics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在回顾Manuele Filaci对非交换几何中标准模型描述的贡献，特别是基于他发现标准模型谱三元组存在多种最小扭曲方式这一成果，系统研究扭曲诱导的内积结构。

Method: 基于Manuele Filaci关于标准模型谱三元组最小扭曲的发现，系统研究扭曲诱导的内积结构，并在宽松假设下分析该内积的数学性质。

Conclusion: 通过系统研究扭曲诱导的内积结构，揭示了该内积将希尔伯特空间转化为克雷因空间的数学性质，并发现了标准模型中扭曲内积酉群与扭曲子对称群之间的包含关系。

Abstract: We review the contributions of Manuele Filaci - a PhD student from the university of Genova prematurely deceased a little more than a year ago - to the description of the Standard Model in noncommutative geometry. Building on Manuele's discovery that there exist various ways to minimally twist the spectral triple of the Standard Model, we study in a systematic way the inner product induced by the twist. Under loose assumptions, this product turns the Hilbert space of the spectral triple into a Krein space. For the Standard Model, the group of unitary with respect to the twisted product contains the symmetry group of twistors as a subgroup.

### [67] [Phase-field investigation of non-isothermal solidification coupled with melt flow dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02968)
*Timileyin David Oyedeji,Aaron Brunk,Yangyiwei Yang,Herbert Egger,Holger Marschall,Bai-Xiang Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个热力学一致的非等温相场模型，用于模拟凝固过程与熔体流动的耦合，特别包含了毛细应力（Korteweg应力）以准确捕捉热毛细效应驱动的流动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相场模型与Navier-Stokes方程耦合时，大多忽略了重要的热力学耦合项，特别是动量方程中的毛细应力（Korteweg应力）。这种忽略导致模型与非平衡热力学不一致，无法准确捕捉毛细效应驱动的熔体流动。

Method: 本文开发了一个热力学一致的非等温相场模型，用于凝固过程与熔体流动的耦合模拟。该模型包含了交叉耦合项，并在动量方程中明确引入了Korteweg应力。模型验证包括纯凝固情况，随后模拟了熔体流动下的枝晶生长。

Result: 结果表明，热毛细效应在界面附近诱导流动，影响枝晶尖端速度和形貌。强制对流下的模拟进一步显示了流动场导致的非对称枝晶生长。此外，数值分析还展示了粘度插值方案对在相场模型中实施无滑移边界条件的影响。

Conclusion: 本文提出的热力学一致相场模型成功捕捉了凝固过程中热毛细效应驱动的熔体流动，为准确模拟凝固-流动耦合过程提供了更完整的理论框架。

Abstract: Solidification, coupled with melt flow, plays a critical role in determining the microstructure and properties of materials in several manufacturing processes. Phase-field models coupled with the Navier-Stokes equations are widely used to model and simulate these dynamics. However, most existing models neglect essential thermodynamic couplings, particularly the capillary (Korteweg) stress in the momentum equation. This stress, which arises from the coupling between the phase field and the melt flow, accounts for thermal capillary effects during non-isothermal solidification. Neglecting it leads to models inconsistent with non-equilibrium thermodynamics and incapable of capturing capillarity-driven melt flow. In this work, we present a thermodynamically consistent, non-isothermal phase-field model for solidification coupled with melt flow, incorporating cross-coupling terms and explicitly including the Korteweg stress in the momentum equation. Model validation is performed for solidification-only cases, followed by simulations of dendritic growth under melt flow. The results show that thermal capillary effects induce flow near the interface, influencing dendrite tip velocity and morphology. Simulations under forced convection further demonstrate asymmetric dendrite growth due to the imposed flow field. Additionally, we numerically demonstrate the influence of viscosity interpolation schemes on enforcing the no-slip boundary condition in phase-field models with melt flow.

### [68] [Anisotropic skyrmion liquid phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02997)
*Daniel Schick,Tim Matthies,Thomas Mutschler,Levente Rózsa,Ulrich Nowak*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究通过准粒子动力学模拟，探讨了原子晶格诱导的斯格明子-斯格明子相互作用各向异性对二维系统熔化转变的影响。研究发现各向同性相互作用下存在六角相（hexatic phase），而各向异性相互作用则导致直接的固-液转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维系统熔化转变的本质自KTHNY理论提出以来备受关注，该理论预测的六角相（hexatic phase）最近在磁性斯格明子（magnetic skyrmions）系统中得到实验验证。本研究旨在探究原子晶格诱导的斯格明子-斯格明子相互作用各向异性如何影响熔化转变过程。

Method: 采用准粒子动力学模拟（quasiparticle dynamical simulations）方法，研究斯格明子-斯格明子相互作用各向异性对熔化转变的影响。通过比较各向同性和各向异性相互作用条件下的相变行为。

Result: 对于各向同性相互作用，观察到从固相通过一个狭窄温度范围内的稳定六角相（hexatic phase）向各向同性液相转变。然而，当原子晶格迫使斯格明子间相互作用呈现各向异性时，可直接观察到固-液转变，且取向有序（orientational order）在液相中可保持至30K的温度。

Conclusion: 原子晶格诱导的相互作用各向异性显著改变二维斯格明子系统的熔化转变路径，各向异性条件下六角相消失，转变为直接的固-液转变，同时液相中保持取向有序。

Abstract: The nature of the melting transition in two-dimensional systems of particles has attracted considerable research attention since the development of Kosterlitz-Thouless-Halperin-Nelson-Young (KTHNY) theory. The hexatic phase proposed by this theory has been recently identified experimentally in ensembles of magnetic skyrmions, quasiparticles formed in a magnetically ordered crystal. Here, we use quasiparticle dynamical simulations to study how the anisotropy of the skyrmion-skyrmion interactions induced by the atomic lattice influences the melting transition. For isotropic interactions, we find a transition from a solid phase through a hexatic phase stable in a narrow temperature range to an isotropic liquid phase. However, if the interactions between skyrmions are forced to be anisotropic by the atomic lattice, then a direct solid-liquid transition can be observed with orientational order persisting up to temperatures of 30 K in the liquid phase.

Magnetic fields were scanned in the range 5 microT < B < 109 microT. No evidence of anomalous neutron losses was found. Consequently, new limits for the n-n' oscillation time constant were set. ### [70] [Continual Learning via Ensemble-Based Depth-Wise Masked Autoencoders for Data Quality Monitoring in High-Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02369)
*Dale Julson,Eric Reinhardt,Andrii Krutsylo,Resham Sohal,Guillermo Fidalgo,Sergei Gleyzer,Emanuele Usai,The CMS HCAL Collaboration*

TL;DR: 该论文提出DepthViT，一种轻量级掩码自编码器架构，结合持续学习框架，用于高能物理（HEP）数据质量监控（DQM）中的自适应异常检测（AD），以应对数据流中的分布偏移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能物理（HEP）领域，探测器在长期恶劣环境中运行，基于静态数据集训练的机器学习（ML）模型用于数据质量监控（DQM）时，会因输入数据流中自然发生的分布偏移（distributional shifts）而导致性能下降，除非采用持续ML技术进行缓解。

Method: 提出DepthViT架构，采用独特的深度嵌入（depth-wise embeddings）和跨深度注意力（cross-depth attention）机制，实现计算高效的异常检测任务。开发持续学习框架，将基于最新数据流训练的DepthViT模型与旧模型集成，构建对数据流偏移更具鲁棒性的系统。

Result: 在紧凑μ子螺线管（CMS）强子量能器的占用图（occupancy maps）上进行评估，该方法在大小分布偏移下均能保持99%以上的精度，并维持正确的异常预测与异常数量之比的稳定性。

Conclusion: DepthViT结合基于集成的持续适应策略，为动态数据环境中可持续运行的自适应异常检测系统提供了一条可行路径。该策略可直接应用于工业监控环境，其中数据同样会随时间自然演化。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) techniques have been demonstrated to improve the accuracy and efficiency of anomaly detection (AD) when compared to conventional methods. This has led to the adoption of ML for data quality monitoring (DQM) use cases in order to monitor the operation of certain systems to ensure that they are free of undesirable or potentially deleterious anomalies. For applications in the field of High-Energy physics (HEP), where detectors must operate in long-running, harsh environments, ML models used in DQM that have been trained on static datasets are bound to experience degraded performance due to distributional shifts that naturally occur in the incoming data streams, unless directly mitigated via the inclusion of continual ML techniques. This work introduces DepthViT, a lightweight masked autoencoder architecture that employs unique depth-wise embeddings and cross-depth attention, to perform computationally efficient AD tasks. A continual learning framework is developed in which DepthViT models trained on the most recent data streams are ensembled with older models to create a robust overall system which is more resilient to shifts in incoming data streams. When evaluated on occupancy maps from the Compact Muon Solenoid (CMS) hadron calorimeter across multiple data-taking campaigns, the proposed method maintains precision above 99\% and stable ratio of correct anomaly predictions to number of anomalies both under small and large distributional shifts. Beyond HEP, the same ensembling-based continual adaptation strategy can be directly applied to industrial monitoring environments where data also naturally evolve over time. This work therefore presents a path toward adaptive anomaly detection systems capable of sustained operation in dynamic data environments.

### [71] [Two-stage Convolutional Neural Network for six-dimensional phase space reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02733)
*Sayantan Mukherjee,Masao Kuriki,Zachary John Liptak,Hitoshi Hayano,Masakazu Kurata,Nobuhiro Terunuma,Toshiyuki Okugi,Yasuchika Yamamoto*

TL;DR: 开发了一种基于卷积神经网络（CNN）的两阶段方法，仅需16张横向x-y屏幕图像即可重建粒子加速器中难以测量的六维（6D）束流相空间分布，相比传统层析成像技术显著减少了测量时间和计算资源需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在粒子加速器中，完整获取六维（6D）束流相空间信息至关重要，但传统束流诊断技术难以实现。现有6D束流成像测量技术如层析成像（tomography）需要较长的测量时间和大量计算资源。

Method: 开发了两阶段卷积神经网络（CNN）模型，仅利用16张在不同相空间旋转角度下采集的横向x-y屏幕图像重建6D相空间。模型使用KEK加速器测试装置（ATF）注入器的ASTRA模拟数据进行训练，并通过改变射频电子枪的RF相位和螺线管磁场获取真实空间图像。

Conclusion: 相比现有6D束流成像测量技术如层析成像，该方法显著减少了测量时间和所需计算资源，为实现更实用的6D相空间测量方法提供了可能。

Abstract: In particle accelerators, full knowledge of the six-dimensional (6D) beam phase space is crucial but difficult to obtain with conventional beam diagnostics. We develop a two-stage convolutional neural network (CNN) that reconstructs the 6D phase space from only sixteen transverse $x-y$ screen images taken at a place with dispersion by different phase space rotation angles. The model is trained with simulation data of KEK-Accelerator Test Facility (ATF) injector with ASTRA. The real-space images in the chicane orbit at the KEK-ATF injector were acquired by varying the RF phase of the RF electron gun and the solenoid magnetic field. From these data, we reconstructed the 6D phase space distribution at the cathode surface and visualized it as 15 two-dimensional images covering all pairwise coordinate combinations. The time width and spatial spread of the electron beam at the cathode showed values consistent with the measured values at KEK-ATF. Compared to existing 6D beam imaging measurement techniques such as tomography, it significantly reduces measurement time and required computational resources, enabling the provision of a more practical 6D phase space measurement method.

Method: 通过模拟相当于5.4 Mt·年曝光量的大气中微子事件，结合超束流中微子（super-beam neutrinos）数据，分析两者对δ_CP测量的协同效应。

Result: 研究发现，结合大气中微子数据后，δ_CP的分辨率从7.5°（6.7°）提升至7.1°（6.5°）（在1σ置信水平下，分别对应δ_CP = -90°和+90°），同时解决了中微子质量顺序引起的简并问题。

Conclusion: ESSnuSB实验中超束流中微子与大气中微子之间存在显著的协同效应，这种结合能够显著提升轻子CP相位δ_CP的测量精度并解决相关简并问题。

Abstract: The ESSnuSB experiment aims to measure the leptonic CP phase $δ_{CP}$ with an unprecedented resolution by probing neutrino oscillations at the second oscillation maximum. In the present work, the complementarity between the long-baseline neutrino program and atmospheric neutrinos is investigated for ESSnuSB. By simulating atmospheric neutrino events equivalent of 5.4 Mt$\cdot$year exposure, the resolution for $δ_{\rm CP}^{}$ is found to improve from $7.5^\circ$ ($6.7^\circ$) to $7.1^\circ$ ($6.5^\circ$) at $1σ$~CL for $δ_{\rm CP}^{} = -90^\circ$ ($+90^\circ$) with respect to super-beam neutrinos, resolving also the degeneracies arising from neutrino mass ordering. These findings highlight the synergies that exist between super-beam neutrinos and atmospheric neutrinos in ESSnuSB.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII合作组利用$(1.0087 \pm 0.0044)\times 10^{10}$个$J/ψ$事例，首次在$Ξ^{0}\toΛ+\text{不可见粒子}$衰变中寻找超出标准模型的无质量粒子，未发现显著信号，并在90%置信水平下给出分支比上限$2.3 \times 10^{-4}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过$Ξ^{0}\toΛ+\text{不可见粒子}$衰变过程寻找超出标准模型的无质量粒子（massless beyond-standard-model particle）。这是首次在$Ξ^0$衰变中研究涉及能量缺失（missing energy）的味改变中性流（flavor-changing neutral current）过程。

Method: 实验使用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的$(1.0087 \pm 0.0044)\times 10^{10}$个$J/ψ$事例，分析$Ξ^{0}\toΛ+\text{不可见粒子}$衰变过程。研究中始终隐含考虑电荷共轭过程（charge-conjugate processes）。

Result: 未观测到显著信号，在90%置信水平下给出分支比$\mathcal{B}(Ξ^{0}\toΛ+\text{不可见粒子})$的上限为$2.3 \times 10^{-4}$。

Conclusion: 这是首次在$Ξ^0$衰变中对涉及能量缺失的味改变中性流过程进行实验搜索，结果为超出标准模型的无质量粒子存在性设定了严格的约束条件。

Abstract: A search for a massless beyond-standard-model particle is performed in the decay $Ξ^{0}\toΛ+\text{invisible}$ using $(1.0087 \pm 0.0044)\times 10^{10}$ $J/ψ$ events collected with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider. No significant signal is observed and the upper limit on the branching fraction $\mathcal{B}(Ξ^{0}\toΛ+\text{invisible})$ is set to be $2.3 \times 10^{-4}$ at the $90\%$ confidence level. This is the first search for a flavor-changing neutral current process with missing energy in $Ξ^0$ decays. Throughout this paper, charge-conjugate processes are always implied.

</details>


### [74] [Search for a narrow resonance with a mass between 10 and 70 GeV decaying to a pair of photons in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03250)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用CMS实验数据，在10-70 GeV质量范围内搜索通过胶子融合产生并衰变为双光子的窄共振态，未发现显著超出背景的信号，并给出了轴子类粒子有效场论框架下的上限限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多个理论模型预测存在质量低于电弱能标（electroweak scale）的新自旋为零粒子，LHC上双光子共振产生过程的搜索能够检验这些模型。

Method: 研究使用CMS实验在质心能量13 TeV下记录的质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度54.4 fb⁻¹，采用新引入的双光子触发（diphoton trigger）探索低质量双光子谱，搜索通过胶子融合（gluon fusion）产生并衰变为不变质量在10-70 GeV范围内的双光子窄共振。

Result: 未观察到显著超出预期背景的过量信号，为窄共振的胶子融合产生截面与双光子衰变分支比的乘积设定了上限，并在轴子类粒子（axion-like particles）的有效场论（effective field theory）框架下对这些限制进行了解释。

Conclusion: 在10-70 GeV质量范围内未发现新的自旋为零粒子证据，研究结果为轴子类粒子等理论模型提供了重要的实验约束。

Abstract: The existence of a new spin-zero particle with a mass below the electroweak scale is predicted by several theoretical models. Searches for resonant production of photon pairs at the LHC are able to probe these models. We present a search for a narrow resonance produced through gluon fusion that decays into a pair of photons with an invariant mass between 10 and 70 GeV, using a proton-proton collision data set from the CMS experiment. This data set, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 54.4 fb$^{-1}$, was recorded in 2018 at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV using a newly introduced diphoton trigger that enabled exploration of the low-mass diphoton spectrum. No significant excess above the expected background is observed. Upper limits are set on the product of the gluon fusion production cross section and the branching fraction of the diphoton decay of a narrow resonance. An interpretation of these limits within an effective field theory framework for axion-like particles is also provided.

</details>

# cond-mat.soft [[Back]](#toc)

### [75] [Dynamic Instabilities and Pattern Formation in Chemotactic Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02595)
*Hongbo Zhao,Qiwei Yu,Andrej Košmrlj,Sujit S. Datta*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了集体趋化（collective chemotaxis）如何影响运动诱导相分离（MIPS），发现趋化作用可以抑制MIPS或引发新的动态不稳定性，如行波和螺旋模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 运动诱导相分离（motility-induced phase separation, MIPS）在无方向偏好的随机运动粒子中已被深入研究，但许多活性系统表现出集体趋化行为——粒子通过自身产生或消耗化学物质形成梯度并沿其定向运动。研究旨在探索集体趋化如何影响MIPS这一基本物理过程。

Method: 采用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）、振幅方程（amplitude equations）和数值模拟（numerical simulations）相结合的方法，研究MIPS在集体趋化影响下的行为。模型可推广到产生或消耗化学引诱剂（chemoattractant）或化学排斥剂（chemorepellent）的粒子，以及具有不同趋化行为的粒子混合物。

Result: 研究发现趋化作用可以抑制或完全阻止MIPS，或引发新的动态不稳定性，如行波（traveling waves）和螺旋（spirals）。预测了稳态和振荡模式的稳定性区域，识别了四种分岔类型：叉形（pitchfork）、鞍结（saddle-node）、无限周期（infinite period）和超临界Hopf（supercritical Hopf）。推导了模式振幅和行波速度的解析表达式，与模拟结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 通过建立描述MIPS与趋化竞争关系的定量原理，该研究深化了对化学响应活性物质系统（chemically-responsive active matter systems）丰富物理基础的理解，为理解复杂活性系统的模式形成提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Collectives of actively-moving particles can spontaneously segregate into dilute and dense phases through a process known as motility-induced phase separation (MIPS). This captivating phenomenon is well-studied for randomly-moving particles with no directional bias. However, many active systems perform collective chemotaxis -- directed motion along a chemical gradient collectively generated by the particles themselves through consumption or production. Here, we use linear stability analysis, amplitude equations, and numerical simulations to study how MIPS is influenced by collective chemotaxis. We find that chemotaxis can either arrest or entirely suppress MIPS, or give rise to novel dynamic instabilities such as traveling waves and spirals. We predict the stability region of the stationary and oscillatory patterns and identify four types of bifurcation that can arise: pitchfork, saddle-node, infinite period, and supercritical Hopf. We also derive analytical expressions for the amplitude of the pattern and traveling wave velocity, yielding excellent quantitative agreement with simulations. Furthermore, we generalize our model to study particles that either consume or produce chemoattractant or chemorepellent, as well as mixtures of particles with different chemotactic behaviors. By establishing quantitative principles describing the competition between MIPS and chemotaxis, our study helps deepen understanding of the rich physics underlying chemically-responsive active matter systems.

</details>


### [76] [Disorder induced melting and glass formation in a one-component Lennard-Jones system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02624)
*Saumya Suvarna,Prabhat K. Jaiswal,Madhu Priya*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟探究了二维Lennard-Jones液体中钉扎（pinning）浓度对玻璃形成的影响。研究发现，适度的钉扎浓度能抑制结晶并促进粒子运动，而过高浓度则会降低系统整体动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解玻璃形成的条件对于揭示玻璃化转变机制至关重要。纯液体由于缺乏"挫折"（frustration）而倾向于结晶而非玻璃化，因此需要引入无序来研究玻璃形成条件。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟研究二维Lennard-Jones单组分液体，通过钉扎协议引入无序——即从平衡构型中选择固定比例的粒子进行固定。系统研究钉扎浓度对结构和动力学性质的影响。

Result: 结构性质（径向分布函数和六角序参数）随钉扎浓度增加而系统性降低。动力学性质（脆性指数和长时间均方位移）则呈现非单调趋势：适度钉扎浓度能防止结晶并促进粒子运动，但过高浓度会抑制粒子迁移率。

Conclusion: 钉扎在控制简单液体相行为中起关键作用，研究结果与玻璃盖片间受限胶体悬浮液的实验观察一致，验证了二维钉扎液体的独特动力学特征。

Abstract: Identifying the conditions under which glass formation occurs is crucial for a fundamental understanding of the glass transition mechanism. Pure liquids devoid of any frustration avoid glass transition and undergo crystallization. In this work, we investigate a one-component liquid interacting via the Lennard-Jones potential in two dimensions, where disorder is introduced through pinning, a protocol in which a fixed fraction of particles is immobilized at positions selected from an equilibrium configuration. By employing molecular dynamics simulation, we systematically study the influence of pinning concentration on both structural and dynamical properties. Structural properties quantified by radial distribution function and hexatic-order parameter display a systematic decrease with a rise in pinning concentration. However, the dynamical properties such as the fragility index and the late-time mean squared displacement exhibit a non-monotonic trend as the concentration of pinned particles increases. A moderate concentration of pinned particles helps prevent crystallization and facilitates particle motion. A further rise in the number of pinned particles suppresses particle mobility, leading to a reduction in the overall dynamics of the system. These simulation results are in good agreement with experimental observations on colloidal suspensions confined between glass coverslips, where particles are immobilized. Our findings demonstrate the pivotal role of pinning in controlling the phase behavior of simple liquids and validate the unique dynamical features of two-dimensional liquids with pinned particles.

</details>


### [77] [Riding the Wave: Polymers in Time-dependent Nonequilibrium Baths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02777)
*Bhavesh Valecha,Jens-Uwe Sommer,Abhinav Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过粗粒化分析发现，聚合物系统对时间依赖信号（time-dependent signals）的稳态响应取决于其长度和拓扑结构：长链、环形和星形拓扑结构会"骑乘"波场正向漂移，而短链和全连接结构则逆波场方向漂移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 定向输运（directed transport）是生物系统响应营养和化学梯度等信号的典型特征，这些信号由于系统相互作用的高度复杂性通常具有时间依赖性。研究旨在探索聚合物系统对此类时间依赖信号的稳态响应行为。

Method: 采用理想Rouse聚合物模型浸没在非平衡浴（nonequilibrium bath）中，该浴由空间和时间变化的自推进波场（self-propulsion wave field）描述。通过粗粒化分析（coarse-graining analysis）结合稳健的数值模拟验证理论预测。

Result: 聚合物对时间刺激的响应随长度和拓扑结构呈现丰富涌现行为：长聚合物以及环形和星形拓扑结构会"骑乘"波场，在波传播方向上显示正向漂移；而短聚合物和全连接结构则逆波信号方向漂移。

Conclusion: 聚合物系统对时间刺激的响应可以通过聚合物拓扑结构或长度进行调控，这为理解复杂生物系统中的定向输运机制提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Directed transport is a characteristic feature of numerous biological systems in response to signals such as nutrient and chemical gradients. These signals often depend on time owing to the high complexity of interactions in these systems. In this study, we focus on the steady-state behavior of polymeric systems responding to such time-dependent signals. We model them as ideal Rouse polymers submerged in a nonequilibrium bath, which is described by a spatially and temporally varying self-propulsion wave field. Through a coarse-graining analysis, we show that these polymers display rich emergent response to the temporal stimuli as a function of their length and topology. In particular, long polymers and structures with ring and star topologies ride the wave, displaying a positive drift in the direction of the wave. Whereas, shorter polymers and fully connected structures drift against the wave signal. We confirm these analytical predictions with robust numerical simulations, showing that the response of polymeric systems to temporal stimuli can be controlled by the topology or the length of the polymer.

</details>


### [78] [Nature of granular drag in microgravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03006)
*Tivadar Pongo,Tianhui Liao,Jinchen Zhao,Valentin Dichtl,Simeon Voelkel,Raul Cruz Hidalgo,Kai Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和数值模拟探究重力对弹丸撞击颗粒介质时阻力（drag force）的影响。研究发现微重力（microgravity）下惯性阻力主导，导致不同的标度律（scaling laws）和空腔动力学（cavity dynamics），并定义了无量纲颗粒阻力系数 $C_{\rm gd}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究重力对弹丸撞击颗粒介质时阻力特性的影响，特别是在微重力条件下的行为。这有助于理解颗粒阻力（granular drag）在空间环境中的本质，为未来太空任务提供理论基础。

Method: 采用实验和数值模拟相结合的方法：实验方面使用嵌入式惯性测量单元（IMU）传感器；数值模拟方面采用离散元方法（DEM）进行仿真分析。

Result: 微重力下惯性阻力主导，产生不同的标度律和空腔动力学。定义的无量纲颗粒阻力系数 $C_{\rm gd}$ 在微重力下保持恒定约1.2，而有重力时会出现与撞击速度成反比的附加项。初始阻力峰值也存在类似差异。

Conclusion: 研究通过类比流体动力学，为理解微重力下颗粒阻力的本质提供了新见解。恒定项源于穿透方向的动量传递，附加项则反映了重力引起的内部应力累积的影响，这对未来太空任务具有启示意义。

Abstract: The influence of gravity on the drag force acting on a projectile impacting granular media is investigated experimentally via embedded inertial measurement unit (IMU) sensor and numerically through discrete element method (DEM) simulations. As gravity approaches zero, inertial drag dominates, yielding qualitatively different scaling laws and cavity dynamics. Analogous to fluid dynamics, we define a dimensionless granular drag coefficient $C_{\rm gd}$, which is found to stay largely at a constant $\sim 1.2$ in microgravity while an additional term inversely proportional to impact velocity arises in the presence of gravity. The constant term can be understood from momentum transfer along the penetration direction while the additional term suggests the influence of internal stress built-up due to gravity. Similar discrepancy is also found for the initial peak of the drag force. This analogy provides novel insights into the nature of granular drag in microgravity and sheds light on future space missions.

</details>


### [79] [Guiding isotropic active fluids with anisotropic friction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03232)
*Cody D. Schimming,Brian A. Camley*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了各向异性摩擦（anisotropic friction）对二维可压缩活性流体（active fluid）的影响，发现拓扑缺陷（topological defects）模式可驱动流体聚集，而初始对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）可导致聚集团簇的圆周运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于近期细胞在各向异性基底上积累的实验观察，旨在探索各向异性摩擦对活性流体动力学行为的影响。

Method: 采用二维可压缩各向同性活性流体模型，引入各向异性摩擦条件，并开发近似解析模型（approximate analytical model）进行定性分析。

Result: 研究发现，正拓扑缺陷模式的各向异性摩擦区域可驱动活性流体聚集形成团簇（clump），但该行为的稳健性取决于初始构型。当初始方位角对称性（azimuthal symmetry）充分破缺时，模式不对称性可导致聚集团簇的圆周运动（circular motion）。

Conclusion: 基于简化模型设计了能够引导聚集团簇沿特定路径定向运动（directed motion）的基底模式，为控制活性物质的空间分布提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Inspired by recent experiments of cells accumulating on anisotropic substrates, we study a two-dimensional, compressible, isotropic, active fluid in the presence of anisotropic friction. We find that regions of anisotropic friction that are patterned as positive topological defects may drive accumulation of an active fluid into a clump, but the robustness of this behavior depends on the initial configuration. If the initial azimuthal symmetry is sufficiently broken, we find that patterning asymmetry can instead lead to circular motion of accumulated clumps. We develop an approximate analytical model to qualitatively explain the motion. Finally, we use our simplified model to design a substrate pattern that creates directed motion of accumulated clusters along a given path.

### [80] [Nonclassical Turing instabilities induced by superdiffusive transport in FitzHugh-Nagumo dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03254)
*Rossella Rizzo,Gaetana Gambino,Vincenzo Sciacca,Marco Sammartino*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有超扩散（superdiffusive）传输的FitzHugh-Nagumo反应扩散系统中的扩散驱动不稳定性，通过分数拉普拉斯算子建模。分析表明超扩散改变了不稳定模式带和图案空间尺度，并揭示了与传统激活-抑制框架不同的不稳定性机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索超扩散传输对反应扩散系统中图案形成的影响，特别是当激活剂（activator）和抑制剂（inhibitor）具有不同扩散阶数时，系统可能表现出与传统扩散驱动不稳定性不同的行为。

Method: 采用分数拉普拉斯算子（fractional Laplacian operators）建模超扩散传输，对激活剂和抑制剂分别赋予不同扩散阶数。通过线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）获得不稳定性阈值和临界波数的显式表达式，并在阈值附近进行弱非线性分析（weakly nonlinear analysis）推导振幅方程。

Result: 结果显示不稳定性阈值仅取决于分数指数比和动力学参数，而空间尺度由扩散阶数和域大小控制。当扩散阶数不同时，即使激活剂扩散快于抑制剂，空间不稳定性仍可能发生。超扩散促进了亚临界行为（subcritical behavior），并在Turing-Hopf余维二点附近分析了静态与振荡不稳定性的相互作用。

Conclusion: 超扩散显著改变了反应扩散系统的图案形成机制，导致不稳定性阈值和空间尺度依赖于扩散阶数比和系统尺寸。这些发现扩展了经典的激活-抑制框架，揭示了异常扩散（anomalous diffusion）在图案形成中的重要作用。

Abstract: We investigate diffusion-driven instabilities in a FitzHugh-Nagumo reaction-diffusion system with superdiffusive transport, modeled by fractional Laplacian operators with different diffusion orders for the activator and the inhibitor.
  A linear stability analysis yields explicit expressions for the instability threshold and the critical wavenumber and shows that superdiffusion modifies the band of unstable modes and the characteristic spatial scale of emerging patterns. We show that the threshold depends only on the ratio of the fractional exponents and on the kinetic parameters, while the spatial scale is controlled by the diffusion orders and the domain size.
  When the diffusion orders differ, spatial instabilities may occur even in regimes where the activator diffuses faster than the inhibitor, due to the combined effect of diffusion rates, anomalous scaling and system size. This leads to instability mechanisms that depart from the classical activator-inhibitor framework.
  A weakly nonlinear analysis near threshold provides the amplitude equation governing nonlinear saturation and reveals that superdiffusion promotes subcritical behavior. We also analyze the interaction between stationary and oscillatory instabilities near Turing-Hopf codimension-two points. All analytical results are supported by numerical simulations.

</details>

### [81] [Invariant Curves and the Variational Structure in Tubular Origami Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02410)
*Ryutaro Ichikawa,Mitsuru Shibayama*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文通过将管状折纸镶嵌（tubular origami tessellations）的逆模数$N^{-1}$作为Kolmogorov-Arnold-Moser（KAM）理论中的扰动参数，进行了严格的动力系统分析。在大模数极限下，保守动力学收敛于具有变分结构的可积映射，其生成函数对应离散平均曲率。系统可转化为非扭转映射，产生零频率共振，形成新的可折叠区域，并通过引入虚拟辅助折叠作为漂移控制机制，证实了稳定准周期吸引子的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在对管状折纸镶嵌进行严格的动力系统分析，通过识别逆模数$N^{-1}$作为Kolmogorov-Arnold-Moser（KAM）理论中的扰动参数，建立系统的理论框架。研究试图理解折纸结构在可积极限下的几何特性及其在扰动下的行为变化。

Method: 采用Kolmogorov-Arnold-Moser（KAM）理论框架，将逆模数$N^{-1}$作为扰动参数进行分析。在大模数极限（$N \to \infty$）下，证明保守动力学收敛于具有变分结构的可积映射。通过调整山-谷折叠分配和折叠长度，将系统转化为非扭转映射（nontwist map），并引入虚拟辅助折叠作为漂移控制机制。

Result: 在大模数极限下，生成函数对应总离散平均曲率（total discrete mean curvature），其几何解释在可积极限下清晰明了。数值结果支持KAM理论预测的不变曲线持续性，相空间密集分布着此类曲线。零频率共振导致相空间中出现新的稳定可折叠区域，表现为椭圆岛（elliptic islands）。通过虚拟辅助折叠机制，数值证实了稳定准周期吸引子（stable quasi-periodic attractors）的存在。

Conclusion: 该研究为管状折纸镶嵌提供了基于KAM理论的严格动力系统分析框架。可积极限下的生成函数具有清晰的几何解释，而非扭转映射中的零频率共振创造了标准扭转机制无法实现的可折叠配置。漂移控制机制证实了稳定准周期吸引子的存在，为折纸结构设计提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We present a rigorous dynamical systems analysis of tubular origami tessellations by identifying the inverse module number, $N^{-1}$, as a perturbation parameter within the framework of Kolmogorov-Arnold-Moser (KAM) theory. In the large-module limit ($N \to \infty$), we prove that the conservative dynamics converges to an integrable map with a variational structure, whose generating function corresponds to the total discrete mean curvature. Although the geometric interpretation of the generating function becomes more complex under perturbations, it is straightforward in the integrable limit, where its structure can be clearly understood. This limit also provides a fundamental framework for characterizing the global behavior of the system. The KAM-predicted persistence of invariant curves is supported by numerical results showing a phase space densely populated with such curves. By adjusting mountain-valley fold assignments and fold lengths, the system can be transformed into a nontwist map that exhibits multiple zero frequencies. The resonance associated with these zero frequencies leads to the emergence of new stable foldable regions in phase space, appearing as elliptic islands. These regions enable the design of foldable configurations that are inaccessible within standard twist regimes. Finally, we analyze the expanding and contracting dynamics of the origami structure within the framework of conformally symplectic systems. By introducing a virtual auxiliary fold as a drift control mechanism, we numerically confirm the existence of stable quasi-periodic attractors.

Abstract: We derive an upper bound for the annealed return probability for the simple random walk on supercritical Bienaymé-Galton-Watson trees. It is valid for all offspring distributions with a finite first moment and is optimal whenever the offspring distribution does not exclude leaves or linear pieces in the tree. This solves completely the case left open by Piau [Ann. Probab. 26, 1016-1040 (1998)]. In the special case of a Poissonian offspring distribution we apply this upper bound to deduce a Lifshits tail for the empirical eigenvalue distribution of the graph Laplacian on supercritical Erdős-Rényi random graphs with finite mean degree.

### [84] [$P$--$V$ criticality, Joule--Thomson expansion, and holographic heat engine of charged Hayward-AdS black holes with a cloud of strings and perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02276)
*Ahmad Al-Badawi,Faizuddin Ahmed,İzzet Sakallı*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括：1）构建带有弦云（CS）和完美流体暗物质（PFDM）的带电Hayward-AdS黑洞解；2）将宇宙学常数视为压力，推导热力学量并验证Smarr关系；3）分析P-V临界性和相变；4）研究Joule-Thomson（JT）膨胀效应；5）设计矩形循环的全息热机并计算其效率。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）发现类范德瓦尔斯（vdW）的小-大黑洞相变，具有平均场临界指数；2）Joule-Thomson（JT）膨胀的最小反转温度与临界温度比值约为0.247；3）参数g和Q收缩冷却区域，β扩展冷却区域，a非单调地重塑该区域；4）全息热机效率在0.362-0.396范围内，Carnot基准比值为0.625-0.791。

Conclusion: 结论表明：弦云参数通过降低固定热力学体积下的焓值来提高热机效率，而完美流体暗物质参数则通过增加不贡献机械功的引力焓来降低效率。该研究为包含天体物理相关物质成分的黑洞热力学提供了系统的相结构分析。

Abstract: We construct the charged Hayward-anti-de Sitter (AdS) black hole (BH) with a cloud of strings (CS) and perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM), and analyze its extended thermodynamic phase structure. The Hayward parameter $g$ replaces the central singularity with a de Sitter (dS) core, while the CS parameter $a$ and the PFDM parameter $β$ encode astrophysically motivated matter content. Treating the cosmological constant as pressure, we derive the thermodynamic quantities, verify the Smarr relation, and establish $P$--$V$ criticality with a van der Waals (vdW)-like small-large BH phase transition and mean-field critical exponents. The Gibbs free energy (GFE) exhibits the characteristic swallowtail below the critical pressure. The Joule-Thomson (JT) expansion yields $T_i^{\rm min}/T_c \approx 0.247$, roughly half the Reissner--Nordström-AdS value. The parameters $g$ and $Q$ contract the cooling region, $β$ expands it, and $a$ reshapes it non-monotonically. A holographic heat engine with a rectangular cycle gives efficiencies $η= 0.362$--$0.396$ and Carnot benchmarking ratios $η/η_C = 0.625$--$0.791$ across six configurations. The CS parameter improves the engine efficiency by reducing the enthalpy at fixed thermodynamic volume, while the PFDM parameter degrades it by adding gravitational enthalpy without contributing to the mechanical work.

</details>


### [85] [Zero-point length as a topological protection of black hole regularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02295)
*Ankit Anand,Kimet Jusufi,Cosimo Bambi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过扩展热力学第一定律，分析了具有零点长度（zero-point length）的规则黑洞的热力学拓扑结构。研究发现零点长度提供了拓扑保护，防止黑洞向裸奇点（naked singularity）转变，并为弱宇宙监督猜想（weak cosmic censorship conjecture）提供了拓扑表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有零点长度的规则黑洞的热力学拓扑性质，特别是分析零点长度如何影响黑洞的热力学结构和奇点形成。通过将正则化尺度 $l_0$ 作为热力学变量，可以更深入地理解黑洞的拓扑保护机制。

Method: 采用扩展的热力学第一定律（extended first law），将零点长度作为几何存储量纳入考虑。通过将正则化尺度 $l_0$ 视为热力学变量，分析热力学流形（thermodynamic manifold）的Hessian几何（Hessian geometry）。研究向量场 $\vecφ = (T, Ψ)$ 的性质，其中 $T$ 是温度，$Ψ$ 是 $l_0$ 的共轭量。

Result: 当 $l_0 > 0$ 时，向量场 $\vecφ$ 在物理参数空间中永不消失，这意味着不存在Morse临界点（Morse critical points）且绕数（winding number）为零（$W = 0$）。在奇点极限 $l_0 \to 0$ 时，出现非零绕数（$W = 1$），将史瓦西奇点（Schwarzschild singularity）表征为拓扑缺陷（topological defect）。

Conclusion: 零点长度的存在不仅正则化了时空背景，还提供了对抗奇点形成的拓扑保护，防止黑洞向裸奇点转变。拓扑不变量在平滑演化下的守恒为弱宇宙监督猜想提供了严格的拓扑表述，表明零点长度在维持时空完整性方面起着关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic topology of regular black holes with zero-point length using an extended first law that includes the zero-point length stored in the geometry. By treating the regularization scale $l_0$ as a thermodynamic variable, we analyze the Hessian geometry of the thermodynamic manifold and demonstrate that the vector field $\vecφ = (T, Ψ)$, where $T$ is the temperature and $Ψ$ is the conjugate to $l_0$, never vanishes in the physical parameter space for $l_0 > 0$. This implies the absence of Morse critical points and a vanishing winding number ($W = 0$), indicating topological protection against the formation of naked singularities. Crucially, we show that in the singular limit $l_0 \to 0$, a non-zero winding number ($W = 1$) emerges, characterizing the Schwarzschild singularity as a topological defect. The conservation of this topological invariant under smooth evolution provides a rigorous topological formulation of the weak cosmic censorship conjecture: the presence of zero-point length not only regularizes the spacetime background but also enforces topological protection against the formation of singularities, preventing black hole-to-naked singularity transitions.

</details>


### [86] [Global existence for a Fritz John equation in expanding FLRW spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02307)
*João L. Costa,Jesús Oliver,Flavio Rossetti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在具有幂律膨胀的FLRW时空上的一类半线性波动方程，证明了在时空膨胀（0<p≤1）条件下，即使缺乏逆尺度因子的可积性，足够小的光滑紧支初始数据也能产生全局解，抑制了Minkowski时空中的有限时间爆破机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究Fritz John型"爆破"方程在非平稳膨胀时空背景下的行为。该方程在Minkowski时空（p=0）中已知会产生有限时间爆破解，研究其在FLRW膨胀时空（0<p≤1）中的行为可以揭示时空膨胀对非线性波方程解的正则化效应。

Method: 采用向量场方法（vector field method）结合色散估计与时空膨胀效应来控制解的行为。通过将Laplace-Beltrami算子与Poincaré代数中不含boost的子集进行交换，并运用Klainerman-Sideris类型的不等式来抑制非线性爆破机制。

Result: 证明了在具有幂律膨胀的FLRW时空（0<p≤1）上，对于足够小的光滑紧支初始数据，Fritz John型方程存在全局时间解。这一结果与Minkowski时空（p=0）中的有限时间爆破行为形成鲜明对比，表明时空膨胀具有正则化效应。

Conclusion: 研究提供了时空膨胀对非线性波方程正则化效应的严格证明，所发展的方法具有一般性，能够处理FLRW时空的非平稳特性，并可推广应用于更广泛的非线性问题和应用场景。

Abstract: We study the family of semilinear wave equations $\square_{\mathbf{g}_p}φ=(\partial_tφ)^2$, on fixed expanding FLRW spacetimes, having $\mathbb{R}^3$ spatial slices and undergoing a power law expansion, with scale factor $a(t)=t^p$, $0< p \le 1$. This is a natural generalization to a non-stationary background of a famous Fritz John ''blow-up'' equation in $\mathbb{R}^{1+3}$ (corresponding to $p=0$, i.e. the case in which $\mathbf{g}_0$ is the Minkowski metric). While, in Minkowski spacetime ($p=0$), non-trivial solutions to this equation are known to diverge in finite time, here we prove that, on the referred FLRW backgrounds ($0<p\leq 1$), sufficiently small, smooth, and compactly supported initial data yield global-in-time solutions to the future. Previous work, co-authored by the first two authors, considered accelerated expanding spacetimes ($p>1$) and relied on the integrability of the inverse of the scale factor to establish future global well-posedness. In the current work, where such an integrability condition is lacking, we rely on a vector field method that captures and combines dispersive estimates with the spacetime expansion to control the solution and suppress the nonlinear blow-up mechanism. To achieve this, we commute the Laplace-Beltrami operator with a boosts-free subset of the Poincaré algebra and employ Klainerman-Sideris types of inequalities. Our strategy is general and is developed to handle the non-stationary nature of FLRW spacetimes. While we focus solely on this Fritz John type of equation, which serves as a prototype to study blow-up of non-linear waves, our approach provides a rigorous proof of the regularizing effects of spacetime expansion and can be exploited for a wider range of applications and nonlinearities.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两种互补方法：经典物理方法中的准均匀基本方程（quasi-homogeneous fundamental equation）和几何热力学（geometrothermodynamics, GTD）的几何框架。在扩展相空间（extended phase space）中分析系统的临界结构与相行为。

Abstract: We investigate the optical and thermodynamic properties of a deformed Schwarzschild Anti-de Sitter (AdS) black hole coupled to a cloud of strings and embedded in perfect fluid dark matter. We analyze the photon sphere and the corresponding black hole shadow, determining how these observables are affected by the string cloud, dark matter distribution, and geometric deformation. The thermodynamic behavior is studied through both the quasi-homogeneous fundamental equation within the classical physical approach and the geometric framework of geometrothermodynamics (GTD), showing full consistency between the two descriptions. In the extended phase space, we examine the critical structure and phase behavior of the system. Our analysis reveals that neither the geometric deformation nor the dark matter parameter generates new phase transitions; criticality emerges only in the vicinity of the Reissner--Nordström--AdS solution (RN--AdS), where the deformation parameter effectively plays the role of an electric charge squared. These results clarify the interplay between matter distributions, geometric deformations, and the phase structure of AdS black holes.

Abstract: In this work, we generalize Ernst potentials to the Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton case and explicitly write the corresponding potential space metric. Since this metric is five-dimensional in potential space, we generalize the corresponding Newman-Penrose coefficients for this metric and compare this formalism with previous approaches to show that this formulation is very convenient for analyzing these spacetimes and finding new exact solutions. We show how to obtain old exact solutions and some new ones with very interesting properties.

### [89] [Orbital Dynamics and Gravitational Wave Signatures of Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals in Galactic Dark Matter Halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02414)
*Guo-He Li,Chen-Kai Qiao,Jun Tao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了暗物质晕对极端质量比旋进（EMRI）系统轨道动力学和引力波信号的影响，通过对比NFW和Beta两种暗物质模型，揭示了暗物质环境对轨道演化、引力波波形和相位的显著改变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在天体物理学中，极端质量比旋进（extreme mass ratio inspiral, EMRI）系统通常嵌入星系暗物质（dark matter, DM）晕中。暗物质环境不可避免地影响致密天体的轨道动力学和系统发射的引力波（gravitational wave, GW）信号，因此需要系统研究不同暗物质模型的具体影响。

Method: 研究选取了两种典型的暗物质晕轮廓模型——纳瓦罗-弗伦克-怀特（Navarro-Frenk-White, NFW）模型和Beta模型，并纳入了三种耗散机制：动力学摩擦（dynamical friction）、吸积（accretion）和引力辐射反作用（gravitational radiation reaction），以系统研究它们对致密天体长期轨道演化的具体影响。

Result: 与纯真空介质相比，暗物质晕的存在显著改变了进动轨道轨迹、轨道参数的动力学演化以及发射引力波的波形和相位。在NFW模型中，由于强烈的吸积效应，能流呈现出独特的"尖峰"特征，在特定半正焦弦处出现从净能量损失到增益的反转，这一现象在Beta模型中不存在。虽然短期观测可能不足以区分NFW和Beta模型，但它们在长期轨道演化中的差异变得明显。

Conclusion: 使用NFW和Beta模型计算的引力波波形表现出相位偏移，在高密度暗物质环境中可能被探测到。对于更高偏心率的轨道和更长的观测时间，这种相位偏移变得更加显著。这些结果为利用未来空间引力波天文台探测不同暗物质模型对EMRI的环境效应提供了理论框架。

Abstract: In astrophysics, extreme mass ratio inspiral (EMRI) systems, which consist of a central supermassive black hole and a stellar-mass compact object (SCO), are typically embedded in galactic dark matter (DM) halos. This dark matter environment inevitably affects the orbital dynamics of the SCO and the gravitational wave (GW) signals emitted by the system. In this work, we select two typical dark matter halo profiles -- the Navarro-Frenk-White (NFW) and Beta models -- to systematically investigate their specific impacts on the long-term orbital evolution of the SCO. By incorporating three dissipative mechanisms -- dynamical friction, accretion, and gravitational radiation reaction -- our results demonstrate that, compared to a pure vacuum medium, the presence of a dark matter halo significantly alters the trajectories of precessing orbits, the dynamical evolution of orbital parameters, and the waveforms and phases of the emitted gravitational waves. Due to the strong accretion effect within the NFW model, the energy flux exhibits a distinctive "cusp" feature, marking a reversal from net energy loss to gain at a specific semi-latus rectum, which is a phenomenon absent in the Beta model. Although short-term observations may not be sufficient to distinguish between the NFW and Beta models, their differences become evident over long-term orbital evolution. The gravitational waveforms computed using the NFW and Beta models exhibit a phase shift, which could be detectable in high-density DM environments. This phase shift becomes even more pronounced for higher eccentric orbits and longer observation times. These results offer a theoretical framework for probing environmental effects on EMRIs across different dark matter models using future space-based gravitational wave observatories.

### [90] [The Cost of Circularity: Quantifying Eccentricity-Induced Biases in Binary Black Hole Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02453)
*Tamal RoyChowdhury,V. Gayathri,Rossella Gamba,Shubhagata Bhaumik,Imre Bartos,Jolien Creighton*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过注入使用TEOBResumS-Dali生成的偏心信号，并利用准圆形进动波形模型IMRPhenomXPHM进行恢复分析。研究覆盖了20-80太阳质量范围以及高达e=0.5的偏心率。

Result: 研究发现，准圆形波形模型仅在非常小的偏心率下保持可靠。当偏心率在10 Hz频率下超过e~0.2时，恢复的质量、自旋、倾角和距离开始显示出显著的系统性偏移。准圆形进动模板通过引入人工进动来模拟偏心振幅和相位调制，突显了这些效应之间的主要简并性（degeneracy）。

Conclusion: 对于高质量、中等偏心率的并合事件，准圆形模型对参数的误估程度足以偏置天体物理解释和群体研究。研究结果确立了偏心波形模型在当前和下一代探测器中对于精确推断变得必不可少的参数空间边界。

Abstract: Dynamically assembled binary black holes are expected to retain measurable orbital eccentricity in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA band, but most parameter estimation analyses still assume quasi-circular inspirals. This raises a critical question: how strongly does unmodeled eccentricity bias the inferred properties of BBH mergers? We address this by injecting eccentric signals generated with TEOBResumS-Dali and recovering them using the circular, precessing IMRPhenomXPHM waveform model. Across $20$-$80 \, M_\odot$ and eccentricities up to $e=0.5$, we find that circular waveform models remain reliable only for very small eccentricities. Above $e\sim0.2$ at 10 Hz, recovered masses, spins, inclination, and distances begin to show significant systematic offsets. Circular precessing templates mimic eccentric amplitude and phase modulations by introducing artificial precession, highlighting a major degeneracy between these effects. For high-mass, moderately eccentric mergers, circular models misestimate parameters at a level that would bias astrophysical interpretation and population studies. Our results establish the parameter-space boundaries where eccentric waveform models become essential for accurate inference in current and next-generation detectors.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在澄清黑洞背景下两点卡罗尔关联子与无质量散射之间的关系。研究动机源于理解每个渐近平坦时空零边界上存在的两种卡罗尔关联子的物理意义及其与散射振幅的对应关系。

Method: 通过分析从$\mathscr I^-$到$\mathscr I^+$以及从$\mathscr I^-$到未来视界$\mathcal H^+$的两种卡罗尔关联子，研究采用正则化方法（减去平直时空类比项）处理关联子，并探讨其极点与零测地线的关系。

Result: 研究发现：从$\mathscr I^-$到$\mathscr I^+$的关联子是反射振幅的位置空间版本，需要正则化处理；而从$\mathscr I^-$到$\mathcal H^+$的关联子则是透射振幅的位置空间版本，在平直时空中不存在。关联子的极点由零测地线决定，并定义了卡罗尔空间中的两类经典方程。

Conclusion: 卡罗尔关联子建立了夏皮罗时间延迟（Shapiro time delay）与光线偏转角之间的关系，应理解为准正规模（QNMs）和格林函数分支切割的对偶描述。时间延迟在小偏转角下呈现对数/二次行为，在大偏转角下则呈线性增长。

Abstract: In this note, we clarify the relationship between the two-point Carrollian correlator and massless scattering in black hole background. It turns out that there are two kinds of Carrollian correlators at the null boundaries of each asymptotically flat spacetime. The correlator from $\mathscr I^-$ to $\mathscr I^+$ should be regularized by subtracting the flat space analog, and it is the position space version of the reflection amplitude of massless scattering. On the other hand, the correlator from $\mathscr I^-$ to the future horizon $\mathcal H^+$ is absent in flat space, and it is the position space version of the transmission amplitude. The poles of the Carrollian correlators are governed by the null geodesics from $\mathscr I^-$ to $\mathscr I^+$ or $\mathcal H^+$, and they define two kinds of classical equations in Carrollian space. These equations establish the relationship between the Shapiro time delay and the deflection angle for light rays and should be understood as the dual descriptions of the quasinormal modes (QNMs) and the branch cut of the Green's function. We find that the time delay contains a logarithmic/quadratic behavior for the correlator from $\mathscr I^-$ to $\mathscr I^+/\mathcal H^+$ for small deflection angles. On the other hand, the time delay is always increasing linearly for both correlators when the deflection angle is large.

</details>


### [93] [Emergent $Λ$CDM cosmology from a fractional extension of Newtonian gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03113)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种牛顿引力（Newtonian gravity）的最小单参数扩展，通过引入含时分数阶核（time-dependent fractional kernel）来修改引力理论。该理论能够自洽地再现辐射主导时期、物质主导时期和当前加速膨胀相，且无需手动引入宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索牛顿引力的分数阶变形（fractional deformation）如何能够产生类似ΛCDM的宇宙学动力学。通过引入单参数变形，试图在不手动引入宇宙学常数的情况下，自洽地再现宇宙演化的各个阶段。

Method: 方法是通过引入一个由变形参数α表征的含时分数阶核，对牛顿引力进行最小单参数扩展。该修改在动力学中诱导出有效的分数阶部分，并通过将标准势能（standard potential）一致地推广到依赖于α的有效势能（effective potential）来推导宇宙学方程。

Result: 结果显示，尽管运动方程中出现类摩擦项（friction-like term），但存在包含类记忆分数阶动能贡献的守恒量。该理论产生的背景动力学与相对论性宇宙学（relativistic cosmology）在动力学上等价，能够同时自洽地再现辐射主导时期、物质主导时期和当前加速膨胀相。

Conclusion: 结论表明，类似ΛCDM的宇宙学动力学可以从牛顿引力的单参数分数阶变形中涌现（emerge）。理论约束要求|α-1|≪1，且在α→1的极限下，理论平滑地约化为标准牛顿引力。这为从分数阶引力框架理解宇宙加速膨胀提供了新视角。

Abstract: We propose a minimal single-parameter extension of Newtonian gravity obtained by introducing a time-dependent fractional kernel characterized by a deformation parameter $α$. This modification induces an effective fractional sector in the dynamics. Despite the appearance of a friction-like term in the equations of motion, we demonstrate the existence of a conserved quantity that contains a memory-like fractional kinetic contribution. By consistently generalizing the standard potential to an effective potential that depends on $α$, the resulting cosmological equations exhibit background dynamics that are dynamically equivalent to relativistic cosmology. Remarkably, with a single unified potential and without introducing a cosmological constant by hand, the radiation-dominated era, the matter-dominated era, and the present accelerated phase are simultaneously and self-consistently reproduced. The structural presence of $α$ in all physical observables allows theoretical and observational constraints to be imposed, indicating that compatibility with the data requires $|α- 1| \ll 1$. In the limit $α\to 1$, the theory smoothly reduces to standard Newtonian gravity. These results show that an emergent $Λ$CDM-like cosmological dynamics can arise from a single-parameter fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity.

### [94] [Quasinormal modes of four-dimensional regular black holes in quasi-topological gravity: Overtones' outburst via WKB method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03189)
*R. A. Konoplya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了非多项式准拓扑引力（non-polynomial quasi-topological gravity）中四维正则黑洞（regular black holes）的标量、电磁和狄拉克微扰的准正则模（quasinormal modes）。研究发现，虽然基模（fundamental mode）随正则化参数平滑变化，但高阶泛音（higher overtones）对近视界修正表现出显著增强的敏感性，导致特征性的泛音爆发（outburst of overtones）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索几何正则黑洞（geometrically regular black holes）的谱特性，特别是高阶泛音对近视界修正的敏感性。这为理解正则黑洞的动力学特性提供了新的探测手段。

Method: 研究方法包括：从非多项式准拓扑引力框架中构建更一般的度规函数类，并选取两个代表性案例进行详细分析；使用高阶WKB近似（WKB approximation）配合Pade重求和（Pade resummation）；采用时域分析（time-domain analysis）和Leaver方法进行验证。

Conclusion: 结论指出，泛音动力学为几何正则黑洞提供了敏感的探测手段，高阶WKB方法能够有效捕捉超越基模的非平凡谱特征。这为研究正则黑洞的微观结构和动力学特性提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We study quasinormal modes of scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of four-dimensional regular black holes arising in non-polynomial quasi-topological gravity. Starting from a more general class of metric functions constructed within the same framework, from which two representative cases are selected for detailed analysis, we examine their spectral properties. While the fundamental mode changes smoothly with the regularization parameter, higher overtones display a markedly enhanced sensitivity to near-horizon modifications, leading to the characteristic outburst of overtones. Remarkably, pushing the WKB approximation to sufficiently high orders with Pade resummation already allows one to detect the onset of this effect. Time-domain analysis and the Leaver method confirm that the relative error of the higher-order WKB approach is much smaller than the observed effect. Our results indicate that overtone dynamics provides a sensitive probe of geometrically regular black holes and that high-order WKB methods remain capable of capturing nontrivial spectral features beyond the fundamental mode.

### [95] [Geodesic flows on a black-hole background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03222)
*Kaushlendra Kumar,Shahn Majid*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究详细分析了基于非交换几何（noncommutative geometry）的新型测地流（geodesic flow）概念在史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中的应用，探讨了密度演化与波函数演化在黑洞（black-hole）环境下的不同行为，并重新审视了克莱因-戈登流（Klein-Gordon flow）在黑洞附近的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于非交换几何中提出的新型测地流概念，该概念在经典情况下也具有新颖性。研究旨在详细分析这一框架在史瓦西时空中的应用，特别是探讨测地速度场作为独立概念如何定义时空密度或波函数的演化。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）将测地速度场作为独立概念，定义密度ρ或波函数ψ的演化；2）使用Kruskal-Szekeres坐标处理穿越视界（horizon）的问题；3）通过密度演化模拟大量测地线的插值；4）重新分析黑洞附近的克莱因-戈登流或伪量子力学（pseudo-quantum mechanics）。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）使用Kruskal-Szekeres坐标时，穿越视界没有问题；2）两个碰撞的高斯密度峰会合并为单个峰，而相反相位的波函数峰会合并为偶极子（dipole），密度剖面不同；3）先前在视界处发现的黑洞原子态（black-hole atom states）和模式也以反射方式存在于黑洞内部；4）视界模式的跨视界行为以及原子谱的离散化取决于视界处的量子引力修正（quantum gravity corrections）。

Conclusion: 该研究为基于非交换几何的新型测地流概念提供了详细分析，展示了密度演化与波函数演化在黑洞环境中的不同行为特征。波函数碰撞实验为验证波函数假设提供了潜在测试，而视界模式的跨视界行为和谱离散化则指向了量子引力修正的重要性。

Abstract: A recent notion of geodesic flows which comes out of noncommutative geometry but which is also novel in the classical case is studied in detail for a Schwarzschild spacetime. In this framework, the geodesic velocity field is an independent concept which then defines the flow of a density $ρ$ on spacetime or possibly that of an amplitude wave function $ψ$ with $ρ= |ψ|^2$. The proper time flow parameter $s$ is generated collectively by the flow of matter. We show carefully how the $ρ$ evolution can be justified as modelling a large number of geodesics interpolated as a local density. Using Kruskal-Szekeres coordinates, we show that there are no issues crossing the horizon. A novel feature is that whereas two colliding Gaussian bumps in density $ρ$ merge into a single bump, two colliding wave function $ψ$ bumps of opposite phase merge into a dipole with a different density $|ψ|^2$ profile, providing a potential test of our wave-function hypothesis. We also revisit the Klein-Gordon flow or pseudo-quantum mechanics around a black-hole and find that previously found black-hole atom states and modes generated at the horizon when an area of disturbance approaches it are also present inside the black-hole in a reflected fashion. We argue that the behaviour of the horizon modes across the horizon as well as discretisation of the atomic spectrum depend on quantum gravity corrections at the horizon.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当代机器学习系统日益依赖序列推理，从语言理解到多模态生成，通常基于类似关联记忆模型的原型模式字典进行操作。理解关联记忆模型中的检索和序列性为洞察机器学习推理提供了重要桥梁，但目前对序列检索和多记忆整合的理论基础仍有限，现有研究主要依赖数值证据。

Method: 研究采用输入驱动可塑性（input-driven plasticity, IDP）Hopfield网络，分析了一个双时间尺度架构，该架构将快速关联检索与慢速推理动力学耦合。通过建立序列推理的动力学理论，推导出记忆转换的明确条件。

Result: 研究得出了自维持记忆转换的明确条件，包括增益阈值（gain thresholds）、逃逸时间（escape times）和崩溃机制（collapse regimes）。这些结果为关联记忆模型中的序列性提供了原则性的数学解释。

Abstract: Reasoning is the ability to integrate internal states and external inputs in a meaningful and semantically consistent flow. Contemporary machine learning (ML) systems increasingly rely on such sequential reasoning, from language understanding to multi-modal generation, often operating over dictionaries of prototypical patterns reminiscent of associative memory models. Understanding retrieval and sequentiality in associative memory models provides a powerful bridge to gain insight into ML reasoning. While the static retrieval properties of associative memory models are well understood, the theoretical foundations of sequential retrieval and multi-memory integration remain limited, with existing studies largely relying on numerical evidence. This work develops a dynamical theory of sequential reasoning in Hopfield networks. We consider the recently proposed input-driven plasticity (IDP) Hopfield network and analyze a two-timescale architecture coupling fast associative retrieval with slow reasoning dynamics. We derive explicit conditions for self-sustained memory transitions, including gain thresholds, escape times, and collapse regimes. Together, these results provide a principled mathematical account of sequentiality in associative memory models, bridging classical Hopfield dynamics and modern reasoning architectures.
