### [98] [From Reachability to Learnability: Geometric Design Principles for Quantum Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03071)
*Vishal S. Ngairangbam,Michael Spannowsky*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出量子神经网络（QNN）中几何特征学习的新框架，通过引入经典到李代数映射和几乎完全局部选择性准则，证明数据与可训练参数的联合依赖对几何灵活性至关重要，且参数化纠缠方向是实现高维形变的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典深度网络通过深度实现数据表示的自适应几何形变，但在量子神经网络中，仅凭深度或状态可达性无法保证这种特征学习能力。研究旨在探索量子神经网络中几何特征学习的理论基础。

Method: 在纯态设置下，将编码数据视为$\mathbb{C}P^{2^n-1}$中的嵌入流形，通过李代数方向分析无穷小幺正作用。引入经典到李代数映射和几乎完全局部选择性准则，该准则结合了方向完备性和数据依赖的局部选择性。

Result: 研究表明：数据无关的可训练幺正算符具有完备性但缺乏选择性，即可学习的刚性重定向；纯数据编码具有选择性但不可调谐，即固定形变。几何灵活性需要数据与可训练权重的非平凡联合依赖。参数化纠缠方向对访问多量子比特状态流形的高维形变至关重要。

Conclusion: 该框架将量子神经网络设计从状态可达性重新定义为隐藏量子表示的可控几何学。数值验证显示，满足CLS准则的数据重上传模型在仅需四分之一门操作的情况下优于不可调谐方案。

Abstract: Classical deep networks are effective because depth enables adaptive geometric deformation of data representations. In quantum neural networks (QNNs), however, depth or state reachability alone does not guarantee this feature-learning capability. We study this question in the pure-state setting by viewing encoded data as an embedded manifold in $\mathbb{C}P^{2^n-1}$ and analysing infinitesimal unitary actions through Lie-algebra directions. We introduce Classical-to-Lie-algebra (CLA) maps and the criterion of almost Complete Local Selectivity (aCLS), which combines directional completeness with data-dependent local selectivity. Within this framework, we show that data-independent trainable unitaries are complete but non-selective, i.e. learnable rigid reorientations, whereas pure data encodings are selective but non-tunable, i.e. fixed deformations. Hence, geometric flexibility requires a non-trivial joint dependence on data and trainable weights. We further show that accessing high-dimensional deformations of many-qubit state manifolds requires parametrised entangling directions; fixed entanglers such as CNOT alone do not provide adaptive geometric control. Numerical examples validate that CLS-satisfying data re-uploading models outperform non-tunable schemes while requiring only a quarter of the gate operations. Thus, the resulting picture reframes QNN design from state reachability to controllable geometry of hidden quantum representations.

</details>


### [99] [Multiparty Quantum Key Agreement: Architectures, State-of-the-art, and Open Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03225)
*Malik Mouaji,Saif Al-Kuwari*

Main category: quant-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多方量子密钥协商（multiparty quantum key agreement, MQKA）使三个或更多互不信任的用户能够通过协作量子协议建立共享密钥。本文旨在提供一个全面的综述，认为MQKA最好被理解为一个由三个正交但紧密耦合的轴组成的设计空间。

Method: 本文采用三轴视角框架：网络架构（network architecture）决定量子态在参与者间的流动方式；量子资源（quantum resources）编码实现所需的物理自由度；安全模型（security model）定义关于设备和基础设施的信任假设。作者将MQKA协议分类为结构性家族，并将其映射到基础量子资源。

Result: 通过三轴框架揭示了重复出现的模式、尖锐的权衡和未探索的设计空间。分析了不同安全模型如何塑造公平性（fairness）和抗合谋性（collusion resistance），识别了MQKA协议中的结构性家族。

Conclusion: 本文提出了面向后NISQ时代量子互联网部署的研究路线图，包括可组合安全框架（composable security frameworks）、网络原生集成、设备无关实现（device-independent implementations），以及适用于混合资源、玻色子编码和公平性感知的MQKA发展方向。

Abstract: Multiparty quantum key agreement (MQKA) enables $n \geq 3$ mutually distrustful users to establish a shared secret key through collaborative quantum protocols. In this paper, we provide a comprehensive review where we argue that MQKA is best understood as a design space organized along three orthogonal but tightly coupled axes: (1) network architecture, which determines how quantum states flow between participants; (2) quantum resources, which encode the physical degrees of freedom used for implementation; and (3) security model, which defines trust assumptions about devices and infrastructure. Rather than treating MQKA as a linear sequence of isolated protocols, we develop this three-axis perspective to reveal recurrent patterns, sharp trade-offs, and unexplored design spaces. We classify MQKA protocols into structural families, map them to underlying quantum resources, and analyze how different security models shape fairness and collusion resistance. We further identify open challenges in composable security frameworks, network native integration, device-independent implementations, and propose a research roadmap toward hybrid-resource, bosonic-code-encoded, and fairness-aware MQKA suitable for the future quantum internet deployments in the post-NISQ era.

### [100] [Quantum regression theorem in the Unruh-DeWitt battery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02287)
*Manjari Dutta,Arnab Mukherjee,Sunandan Gangopadhyay*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用量子回归定理（quantum regression theorem）解析研究匀加速Unruh-DeWitt探测器（作为相对论量子电池）的关联函数，分析加速度如何增强自发辐射（spontaneous emission）耗散，并推导出长时极限下的洛伦兹线型（Lorentzian line shape）自发辐射谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究匀加速两能级量子系统（Unruh-DeWitt探测器）作为相对论量子电池（relativistic quantum battery）的关联函数特性，特别关注加速度对自发辐射耗散的增强效应，以及其在玻色-爱因斯坦统计（Bose-Einstein statistics）中光子聚束（photon bunching）背景下的二阶关联函数。

Method: 采用量子回归定理（quantum regression theorem）和Born-Markov近似，推导出Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad主方程（master equation）描述系统约化密度矩阵演化；通过Wightman函数的傅里叶变换（Fourier transformation）和指数正则化（exponential regularisation）计算主方程中的函数形式；求解单时期望值演化方程并确定一阶和二阶双时关联函数（two-time correlation functions）。

Result: 解析求解了系统的单时平均值和双时关联函数，详细分析了自发辐射现象，证明加速度能够增强相关耗散；研究了与玻色-爱因斯坦统计中光子聚束相关的特殊二阶关联函数；推导出自发辐射谱在长时极限下高频区域呈现明确定义的洛伦兹线型（Lorentzian line shape）。

Conclusion: 通过量子回归定理成功解析研究了匀加速Unruh-DeWitt探测器（作为相对论量子电池）的关联函数特性，揭示了加速度对自发辐射耗散的增强机制，并获得了长时极限下具有洛伦兹线型的自发辐射谱，为理解相对论量子系统中的能量耗散提供了理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we employ the quantum regression theorem, a powerful tool in the study of open quantum systems, to analytically study the correlation functions of an Unruh-DeWitt detector, which is an uniformly accelerated two-level quantum system, absorbing charges from an external classical coherent pulse. The system can thus be viewed as a relativistic quantum battery that interacts with the environment of its perceived particles, namely, the quanta of a massless scalar field. By considering the relativistic battery moving in Rindler spacetime, under Born-Markov approximation, we derive the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad master equation governing the evolution of the system's reduced density matrix. Moreover, we perform the Fourier transformation of the Wightman functions and use exponential regularisation to compute the functional forms appearing in the master equation. Next, we derive the evolution equations for the the single-time expectation values of the system's operators. We not only solve these equations to find out the single time averages, but also employ the quantum regression theorem to determine the two-time correlation functions of first and second order. We analyse them in details to explain the phenomenon of spontaneous emission and show analytically how the acceleration can enhance the associated dissipation. Furthermore, we address a special form of second order correlation function relevant to the context of photon bunching arising in Bose-Einstein statistics. Finally, we derive the spontaneous emission spectrum of the battery detector analytically, which in the long-time limit displays a well-defined Lorentzian line shape in the high frequency regime.

</details>


### [101] [Collapse and transition of a superposition of states under a delta-function pulse in a two-level system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02407)
*Ariel Edery*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了量子两能级系统在δ函数脉冲作用下，从本征态的线性叠加态到特定本征态的跃迁概率。通过求解一阶耦合方程，获得了跃迁概率的精确解析表达式，揭示了δ脉冲可实现波函数"坍缩"到确定本征态的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子跃迁理论主要关注本征态间的跃迁概率计算。本研究旨在探索从本征态的线性叠加态（linear superposition of eigenstates）到特定本征态的跃迁过程，特别是在δ函数脉冲作用下的动力学行为。

Method: 研究采用两能级系统（two-level system）模型，能量分别为E₁和E₂。通过求解含时薛定谔方程的一阶耦合方程组，获得了δ脉冲作用后系数c₁(t>0)和c₂(t>0)的精确解析解。初始叠加态系数α₁和α₂为自由参数，仅受归一化条件约束。

Result: 获得了从初始叠加态到第二本征态的跃迁概率P_{α₁,α₂→2}的通用解析表达式。研究发现δ脉冲导致的跃迁是瞬时性的，且与能隙E₂-E₁无关。特定相互作用强度β的多重值可使系统以单位概率坍缩到确定本征态，实现波函数坍缩（collapse of the wavefunction）。

Conclusion: δ函数脉冲可在薛定谔方程框架内实现波函数从叠加态到确定本征态的瞬时坍缩，这一过程与测量导致的坍缩机制不同。该研究为量子态操控提供了新的理论可能性。

Abstract: Under a time-dependent perturbation it is common to calculate the transition probability in going from from one eigenstate to another eigenstate of a quantum system. In this work we study the transition in going from a \textit{linear superposition of eigenstates} to an eigenstate under a delta-function pulse (which acts at $t=0$). We consider a two-level system with energy levels $E_1$ and $E_2$ and solve the coupled set of first order equations to obtain exact analytical expressions for the coefficients $c_1(t>0)$ and $c_2(t>0)$ of the final state. The expressions for the final coefficients are general in the sense that they are functions of the interaction strength $β$ and the coefficients $α_1$ and $α_2$ of the initial superposition state which are free parameters constrained only by $|α_1|^2+ |α_2|^2=1$. This opens up new possibilities and in particular, allows for a ``collapse" scenario. We obtain a general analytical expression for the transition probability $P_{α_1,α_2 \to 2}$ in going from an initial superposition state to the second eigenstate. Armed with this general expression we study some interesting special cases. With a delta-function pulse, the transitions are abrupt/instantaneous and we show that they do not depend on the energy gap $E_2-E_1$ and hence on the relative phase between the two eigenstates. For specific multiple values of the interaction strength $β$, we show that the system ends up in a definite eigenstate i.e. probability of unity. Such a transition can be viewed as a ``collapse" since a superposition of states transitions abruptly to a definite eigenstate. The collapse of the wavefunction is familiar in the context of a measurement. Here it occurs via a delta-function pulse in Schrödinger's equation. We discuss how this differs from a collapse due to a measurement.

</details>


### [102] [Local decoder for the toric code with a high pseudo-threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02328)
*Louis Paletta*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于Kitaev环面码（toric code）的新型局部解码器——2D信号规则（2D signal-rule），该解码器通过缺陷吸引和二进制信号交换机制，在分布式架构下实现了接近最优的阈值和缩放性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局部解码器（local decoder）通过完全分布式架构替代集中式经典处理，为实时量子纠错提供了有前景的解决方案。然而现有局部解码器存在阈值（threshold）不理想和缩放（scaling）性能欠佳的问题，需要改进以接近最优解码器的性能。

Method: 提出2D信号规则解码器，将奇宇称稳定子测量（odd parity stabilizer measurements）解释为缺陷（defects），这些缺陷通过交换二进制信号（binary signals）相互吸引。该方法在现象学噪声模型（phenomenological noise model）下进行数值评估，考虑了每次迭代中的数据错误和测量错误。

Result: 数值证据显示，在临界错误率以下，系统尺寸增大时逻辑错误呈指数抑制（exponential logical error suppression）。与已知局部解码器相比，该构造将阈值差距（threshold gap）减半（对数尺度），并在实验相关系统尺寸下实现最优缩放（optimal scaling）。

Conclusion: 该2D信号规则解码器显著提升了局部解码器的性能，使其接近最先进解码器的阈值，并实现最优缩放，为二维局部量子存储器（two-dimensional local quantum memory）的实际实现提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Local decoders provide a promising approach to real-time quantum error-correction by replacing centralized classical processing, with significant hardware constraints, by a fully distributed architecture based on a simple, local update rule. We propose a new local decoder for Kitaev's toric code: the 2D signal-rule, that interprets odd parity stabilizer measurements as defects, attracted to each other via the exchange of binary signals. We present numerical evidence of exponential logical error suppression with system size below some critical error rate, under a phenomenological noise model, with data and measurement errors between each iteration. Compared to previously known local decoders, which exhibit suboptimal thresholds and scaling, our construction halves (in log scale) the threshold gap with state-of-the-art decoders, and achieves optimal scaling for experimentally relevant system sizes, enabling the practical realization of a two-dimensional local quantum memory.

</details>


### [103] [Charging power enhancement at the phase transition of a non-integrable quantum battery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02819)
*D. Farina,M. Sassetti,V. Cataudella,D. Ferraro,N. Traverso Ziani*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了非可积量子电池中量子相变对充电性能的影响，发现在轴向次近邻伊辛模型中，临界性能够显著增强充电功率，为多量子比特系统的量子电池设计提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用多体相互作用和临界现象提升量子电池性能是新兴研究方向，但量子相变能否增强充电能量或功率，特别是在非可积系统中的表征仍有限，这源于苛刻的数值计算要求。

Method: 研究采用一维轴向次近邻伊辛模型（Axial Next-Nearest-Neighbor Ising model）作为非可积量子电池示例，通过量子淬火协议进行充电，对比可积系统的情况。

Result: 与可积情况不同，在该非可积设置中，临界性能够导致充电功率的显著增强，这一发现为多量子比特系统的量子电池设计提供了重要信息。

Conclusion: 研究结果不仅指导多量子比特系统的量子电池设计，而且可在当前量子模拟平台（包括中性原子阵列）上进行实验验证，为非可积系统中量子相变对电池性能的影响提供了新见解。

Abstract: Exploiting many-body interaction and critical phenomena to improve the performance of quantum batteries is an emerging and promising line of research. A central question in this direction is whether quantum phase transitions can enhance the charging energy or the power. While preliminary works have addressed this problem in fine-tuned integrable models, its characterization in non-integrable systems remains limited due to the demanding numerical requirements. Here, we investigate a one-dimensional Axial Next-Nearest-Neighbor Ising model as an example of non-integrable quantum battery charged via a quantum-quench protocol. In contrast to integrable cases, we find that criticality in this setting can lead to a pronounced enhancement of the charging power. Our findings inform quantum-battery design of many-qubit systems and are amenable to experimental verification on current quantum-simulation platforms, including neutral-atom arrays.

### [104] [Spin hydrodynamics on a hyperbolic expanding background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02296)
*Rajeev Singh,Alexander Soloviev*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了Grozdanov最近发现的κ=-1双曲流背景上的相对论自旋流体动力学，推导了完美流体自旋流体动力学框架下自旋势所有分量的精确演化方程，发现与Gubser流相比，κ=-1流具有更强的自旋动力学局域化和独特的振荡衰减行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索Grozdanov最近发现的κ=-1双曲流背景上的相对论自旋流体动力学（relativistic spin hydrodynamics）。该背景对应于SO(2,1)不变、横向膨胀且具有有限时空支撑的闵可夫斯基空间解，与具有SO(3)对称性和无限横向范围的著名Gubser流（κ=+1）形成对比。

Method: 研究方法基于完美流体自旋流体动力学（perfect-fluid spin hydrodynamics）的表述，在κ=-1背景上推导了自旋势（spin potential）所有分量的精确演化方程。

Result: 研究发现，与Gubser流相比，增强的早期膨胀速率和因果边缘（causal edge）的存在导致自旋动力学具有更强的局域化。值得注意的是，自旋势的方位角分量在前向光锥（forward lightcone）内衰减时发生振荡，这与Gubser流形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，κ=-1流作为一个独特且具有物理意义的基准，可用于研究具有有限时空支撑的膨胀相对论流体中的自旋动力学。

Abstract: We study relativistic spin hydrodynamics on the hyperbolic $κ=-1$ flow background recently identified by Grozdanov. This background corresponds to an $SO(2,1)$-invariant, transversely expanding solution with finite spacetime support in Minkowski space, in contrast to the well-known Gubser flow $(κ=+1)$ which possesses $SO(3)$ symmetry and infinite transverse extent. Working within the formulation of perfect-fluid spin hydrodynamics, we derive the exact evolution equations for all spin components of the spin potential on the $κ=-1$ background. We find that the enhanced early-time expansion rate and the presence of a causal edge lead to a stronger localization of spin dynamics compared to the Gubser case. Remarkably, the azimuthal component of the spin potential oscillates as it decays in the forward lightcone, in stark contrast to the Gubser flow. Thus, our results establish the $κ=-1$ flow as a distinct and physically meaningful benchmark for studying spin dynamics in expanding relativistic fluids with finite spacetime support.

</details>

### [105] [Transformer Neural-Network Quantum States for lattice models of spins and fermions: Application to the Ancilla Layer Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02316)
*Riccardo Rende,Alexander Nikolaenko,Luciano Loris Viteritti,Subir Sachdev,Ya-Hui Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Transformer架构的变分波函数方法，用于研究包含自旋和费米子自由度的晶格系统。该方法在一维Ancilla Layer Model中取得了与DMRG高度一致的结果，识别了多种量子相，并展示了在周期性边界条件下的计算优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发能够处理复合局部希尔伯特空间（composite local Hilbert space）的变分波函数方法。传统方法在处理同时包含自旋和费米子自由度的晶格系统时面临挑战，特别是在周期性边界条件和高维模型中。

Method: 方法基于神经网络量子态（Neural-Network Quantum States, NQS）框架，采用Transformer架构处理复合局部希尔伯特空间。通过受自然语言处理启发的标记化（tokenization）过程，神经网络以前流（backflow）方式预测依赖于自旋构型的费米子轨道。

Result: 在一维Ancilla Layer Model中，该方法在开边界条件下与密度矩阵重整化群（Density Matrix Renormalization Group, DMRG）结果在全参数范围内达到优异定量一致。识别了多种量子相：有效解耦的Luttinger液体（LL）、具有不同费米波矢的LL*相（其中移动费米子被梯子的一条腿Kondo屏蔽），以及Luther-Emery（LE）相。在周期性边界条件下，Transformer Ansatz保持了相当的精度。

Conclusion: 结论表明基于Transformer的NQS为具有复合局部希尔伯特空间的相关晶格系统提供了精确且可扩展的变分框架。该方法在处理边界效应和异质局部结构方面具有潜力，特别适用于高维模型研究，其中张量网络方法计算成本更高。

Abstract: We introduce a variational wave function based on Neural-Network Quantum States (NQS) to study lattice systems whose local Hilbert space contains both spin and fermionic degrees of freedom. Our approach is based on the use of the Transformer architecture, which can naturally handle composite local Hilbert spaces through a tokenization procedure closely inspired by techniques from natural language processing. The neural network predicts a set of fermionic orbitals that depend on the spin configuration in a backflow-inspired manner. We apply the method to the one-dimensional Ancilla Layer Model, consisting of a chain of mobile spin-$1/2$ fermions coupled to a two-leg spin-$1/2$ ladder. For open boundary conditions, we achieve excellent quantitative agreement with Density Matrix Renormalization Group (DMRG) results across the full range of parameters considered. We find a phase in which the chain forms an effectively decoupled Luttinger liquid (LL), and a LL* phase with a distinct Fermi wavevector in which the mobile fermions are Kondo screened by one leg of the ladder, while the other leg forms the critical Bethe spin liquid. The LL* is the analog of the phase describing the pseudogap in two dimensions. We also find a Luther-Emery (LE) phase, where the LL* state becomes unstable toward the formation of a spin gap. The Transformer Ansatz maintains comparable accuracy for periodic boundary conditions, where tensor-network methods are computationally more demanding. Together, these findings establish Transformer-based NQS as an accurate and scalable variational framework for correlated lattice systems with composite local Hilbert spaces and highlight their potential for studying higher-dimensional models where boundary effects and heterogeneous local structures pose significant challenges.

</details>


### [106] [Trion liquid and its photoemission signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02323)
*Noam Ophir,Anna Keselman*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索掺杂低维半导体中强电子-空穴相互作用下三子液体的形成机制，并通过角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）识别其特征，以理解在正常带绝缘体与激子绝缘体相边界附近掺杂时形成的强关联物态。

Method: 研究方法采用一维微观模型，并运用基于矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）的精确无偏计算。通过分析光电子能谱，研究部分占据的三子带在ARPES谱中产生的带隙内特征。

Result: 研究结果表明，部分占据的三子带在角分辨光电子能谱中产生带隙内特征，且在费米能级处谱权重消失。这证实了三子液体在掺杂低维半导体中的形成，特别是在正常带绝缘体与激子绝缘体相边界附近。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在强电子-空穴相互作用的掺杂低维半导体中，特别是在正常带绝缘体与激子绝缘体相边界附近，会自然形成三子液体这一强关联物态。该物态在角分辨光电子能谱中表现为带隙内特征且费米能级处谱权重消失，为实验探测提供了明确特征。

Abstract: We study the formation of a trion liquid in doped low-dimensional semiconductors with strong electron-hole interactions and analyze its signatures in angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES). We show that this strongly correlated state of matter forms naturally in the vicinity of the phase boundary between a normal band insulator and an excitonic insulator upon doping. By studying the photoemission spectrum, we show that a partially occupied trion band gives rise to an in-gap feature in the ARPES spectrum with vanishing spectral weight at the Fermi energy. We demonstrate our findings using a 1D microscopic model employing exact, unbiased, matrix product state (MPS)-based calculations.

### [107] [Large Electron Model: A Universal Ground State Predictor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02346)
*Timothy Zaklama,Max Geier,Liang Fu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了大型电子模型（Large Electron Model），这是一种能够生成整个哈密顿参数流形上相互作用电子变分波函数的单一神经网络模型。该模型基于费米集架构（Fermi Sets architecture），通过条件化处理哈密顿参数和粒子数，在二维谐振势中准确预测基态波函数，并泛化到未见过的耦合强度和粒子数区域。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用费米集架构作为多体费米子波函数的通用表示，该架构进一步以哈密顿参数和粒子数为条件。构建的大型电子模型是单一神经网络模型，能够生成整个哈密顿参数流形上相互作用电子的变分波函数。

Result: 在二维谐振势中的相互作用电子系统中，单个训练模型准确预测基态波函数，并泛化到未见过的耦合强度和粒子数区域。模型生成准确的真实空间电荷密度和基态能量，处理能力可达50个粒子。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了基于变分原理的材料发现基础模型方法，能够准确处理超出密度泛函理论能力的强电子关联效应。大型电子模型为量子多体系统的通用表示和计算提供了新范式。

Abstract: We introduce Large Electron Model, a single neural network model that produces variational wavefunctions of interacting electrons over the entire Hamiltonian parameter manifold. Our model employs the Fermi Sets architecture, a universal representation of many-body fermionic wavefunctions, which is further conditioned on Hamiltonian parameter and particle number. On interacting electrons in a two-dimensional harmonic potential, a single trained model accurately predicts the ground state wavefunction while generalizing across unseen coupling strengths and particle-number sectors, producing both accurate real-space charge densities and ground state energies, even up to $50$ particles. Our results establish a foundation model method for material discovery that is grounded in the variational principle, while accurately treating strong electron correlation beyond the capacity of density functional theory.

### [108] [Quantitative Determination of Quantum Fluctuations in Clean Magnets I: Neutron Spin Echo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02431)
*Fanjun Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究从中子散射的磁总矩求和规则出发，建立了有序磁矩减小与中间散射函数长时间极限之间的直接联系，为测量体量子磁体中的量子涨落强度提供了模型无关的实验方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立一种直接且实验可测量的方法来量化体量子磁体（bulk quantum magnets）中的量子涨落强度，特别是针对多晶样品（polycrystalline samples）。当前需要一种模型无关（model-independent）的方法来评估量子涨落水平。

Method: 从中子散射的磁总矩求和规则（magnetic total-moment sum rule）出发，推导出有序磁矩减小（ordered-moment reduction）与中间散射函数（intermediate scattering function）长时间极限之间的显式联系。通过线性自旋波计算（linear spin-wave calculations）对方形和三角形海森堡反铁磁体（Heisenberg antiferromagnets）进行验证。

Result: 建立了时间域公式：长时间极化率（long-time polarization）等于有序磁矩与总磁矩的比值，即 \(P(t\rightarrow\infty)=\frac{\langle μ\rangle^{2}}{\langle μ^{2} \rangle}\)。计算表明，量子自旋减小（quantum spin reduction）和几何阻挫（geometric frustration）都会抑制平台值，且与磁矩减小定量一致。

Conclusion: 该框架通过中子自旋回波光谱学（neutron spin-echo spectroscopy）为测量体量子磁体中的量子涨落水平提供了直接且模型无关的方法，特别适用于多晶样品，建立了长时间极化率与有序/总磁矩比值的直接联系。

Abstract: Starting from the magnetic total-moment sum rule of neutron scattering, we derive an explicit connection between ordered-moment reduction and the long-time limit of the intermediate scattering function. We show that this time-domain formulation establishes a direct and experimentally accessible measure of quantum fluctuation strength through neutron spin-echo spectroscopy, with \[P(t\rightarrow\infty)=\frac{I(Q,t\rightarrow\infty)}{I(Q,t=0)}=\frac{\langle μ\rangle^{2}}{\langle μ^{2} \rangle}\] This identity links the long-time polarization to the ratio between ordered and total magnetic moments. Linear spin-wave calculations for square and triangular Heisenberg antiferromagnets demonstrate that both quantum spin reduction and geometric frustration suppress the plateau value in quantitative agreement with moment reduction. The resulting framework establishes a direct and model-independent measure of the level of quantum fluctuations in bulk quantum magnets, particularly for polycrystalline samples.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究确立了关联交变磁体的有限温度相图，阐明了强电子相互作用在该相中的关键作用，特别是几何阻挫对稳定关联磁性金属相和增强磁相变尺度的贡献。

Abstract: We present the first finite-temperature study of a strongly correlated $d$-wave altermagnet across the Mott insulator-metal transition using a non-perturbative numerical approach. We map out the thermal phase diagram and provide quantitative estimates of the transition scales in an interacting altermagnet. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering, INS）探测CeNiSn的磁激发，结合电子结构计算和动力学平均场理论（dynamical-mean field theory）分析重正化能带结构。

Conclusion: CeNiSn被确认为拓扑近藤绝缘体，解决了其电子性质的长久谜团，并展示了强关联窄带材料中拓扑多体相干态在光谱测量中的表现。

Abstract: In Kondo insulators the many-body Kondo lattice effect drives the formation of bands containing heavy charge carriers with a hybridization gap, leading to insulating properties. These renormalized bands can host non-trivial topologies driven by strong electron-electron interactions, but probing narrow heavy bands at low temperatures is challenging. We use inelastic neutron scattering (INS) to probe the Kondo lattice CeNiSn, which hosts both semimetallic transport properties and a hybridization gap. The INS response exhibits momentum-dependent magnetic excitations and a spin-gap in the low-temperature Kondo coherent state, which electronic structure calculations corroborate as arising from the renormalized heavy band structure. Dynamical-mean field theory demonstrates that this renormalized band structure corresponds to a topological Kondo insulating state, and hence the INS probes bulk excitations of heavy topological bands. This identification of a Kondo insulator addresses the long-standing mystery of the electronic properties of CeNiSn, and demonstrates the manifestation of a topological many-body coherent state in spectroscopic measurements of strongly correlated narrow band materials.

### [111] [Emergent quantum phenomena in two-dimensional 1T-TaS2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02815)
*Haiyang Chen,Zhiqiang Sun,Peng Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

Method: 综述主要基于角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）和扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）的实验结果，分析二维1T-TaS2的电子结构。同时讨论了超越中子散射等传统探测手段的实验方法，以及近藤效应（Kondo effect）在探测自旋子激发中的作用。

Result: 总结了1T-TaS2中电荷密度波、超导性和量子自旋液体态之间复杂的竞争与共存关系。在二维极限下，量子涨落增强可以稳定量子自旋液体态，该态的特征可以在电子谱中观察到。外部刺激如压力、离子门控和光激发提供了调控这些量子态的有效途径。

Conclusion: 综述提出了未来的实验方向，强调外部扰动如门控和光激发为控制和利用这些相互交织的量子态提供了多功能途径。通过结合多种实验手段，可以更深入地理解二维1T-TaS2中复杂的量子现象。

Abstract: Strong electron correlation drives 1T-TaS2 from a half-filled metallic state into a Mott insulating phase, coexisting with a charge density wave at low temperatures. Under external stimuli such as pressure or ionic gating, superconductivity emerges in 1T-TaS2, exhibiting an intricate relationship of competition and coexistence with the charge density wave order. In the two-dimensional (2D) limit, enhanced quantum fluctuations can stabilize a quantum spin liquid (QSL) state in the Mott insulator. This review summarizes recent advances in understanding these quantum states in 2D 1T-TaS2 from the perspective of angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) and scanning tunneling microscopy (STM), with a focus on the dimensionality effect on its electronic structure. We outline the signatures of QSL state in electronic spectra and discuss how this state can be revealed in the family of this material through experimental approaches beyond conventional probes such as neutron scattering. The role of Kondo effect in detecting spinon excitations is further discussed. Finally, we suggest future experimental directions and highlight how external perturbations such as gating and light excitation offer versatile pathways to control and exploit these intertwined quantum states.

### [112] [Kitaev model in a magnetic field: stable emergent structure, degenerate classical ground states, and reentrant topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02992)
*Sheikh Moonsun Pervez*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了蜂窝晶格上反铁磁Kitaev模型在塞曼场下的行为。通过Majorana平均场分析发现，在特定磁场方向下，系统存在方向依赖的稳定化现象；对于锥形磁场，中间区域存在两个不同相：无序相和经典高度简并相。研究还扩展到各向异性耦合极限，发现拓扑性质存在重入行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究蜂窝晶格上反铁磁Kitaev模型在塞曼场下的行为，特别关注磁场方向对系统稳定性的影响，以及锥形磁场下中间区域相的特性。同时探索各向异性耦合极限下拓扑性质的变化。

Method: 采用广泛的Majorana平均场分析（Majorana mean-field analysis）研究系统行为，并通过精确对角化计算（exact diagonalization calculations）对平均场结果进行定性验证。研究扩展到Kitaev耦合参数的各向异性极限。

Result: 当磁场沿特定笛卡尔轴方向时，涌现场（emergent fields）表现出方向依赖的稳定化，直至外部场达到临界强度。对于锥形磁场，中间区域存在两个相：无序相（涌现场密度收敛于随机值，陈数无定义）和经典高度简并相（涌现场密度极小，磁化矢量大小为1）。各向异性耦合极限下，拓扑性质在锥形磁场中间强度时表现出重入行为（reentrant behavior）。

Conclusion: 反铁磁Kitaev模型在塞曼场下展现出丰富的相行为，包括方向依赖的稳定化、中间区域的两个不同相（无序相和经典高度简并相），以及各向异性极限下拓扑性质的重入现象。精确对角化计算定性支持了平均场分析的部分结果。

Abstract: We have studied the anti-ferromagnetic Kitaev model on a honeycomb lattice under the Zeeman field, using an extensive Majorana mean-field analysis. When the magnetic field is along a specific Cartesian axis, we find that the emergent fields exhibit direction-dependent stabilization up to a certain critical strength of the external field. For a conical magnetic field, the characteristics of the emergent intermediate state are elusive. Our mean-field analysis reveals the existence of two distinct phases in the intermediate region. First, the system enters a disordered phase, where emergent-field densities converge to random values, and the Chern number is ill-defined. The magnitude of magnetization also fluctuates and remains less than unity, indicating a strong quantum effect. In the second phase, emergent-field densities attain vanishingly small values. In this phase, the magnetization components fluctuate heavily, but the magnitude of the magnetization vectors becomes unity, indicating highly degenerate classical ground states. We perform exact diagonalization calculations that qualitatively support some of the mean-field results. We extend our study to the anisotropic limit of the Kitaev coupling parameters. When the couplings are beyond the triangular inequality, the pure Kitaev model is known to host a topologically trivial gapped quantum spin liquid. We find that, for intermediate strengths of a conical magnetic field, topology shows a reentrant behavior.

### [113] [A composite electron-lattice order: electronic nematicity of 2DEG and polarization density waves at a near-ferroelectric interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03057)
*Fei Yang,Zhi-Yang Wang,Long-Qing Chen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用自洽微观多体计算（self-consistent microscopic many-body calculation）方法，研究二维电子气与极性声子强耦合系统。通过平均场理论估计了这种涌现有序态的转变温度，并分析了其随多个调控参数的演化。

Result: 计算表明耦合系统稳定形成了复合电子-晶格有序态，其中晶格极化自发形成极化密度波，同时二维电子气中出现电子条纹序。这种交织序部分重构了电子谱，产生了二重准粒子各向异性，在单粒子层面产生电子向列性。在强外电场作用下，向列响应转变为由复合序的集体滑动动力学主导。

Conclusion: 该理论为KTaO₃(111)界面的异常输运和各向异性响应提供了自然解释。提出的复合序以及场诱导的从准粒子驱动到滑动主导的向列性转变，为临界电子-玻色子系统中由多体效应和集体动力学产生的向列性提供了独特机制，其适用性超越了铁电平台。

Abstract: We consider a two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG) formed at a near-ferroelectric interface and strongly coupled to polar phonons. Through a self-consistent microscopic many-body calculation, we show that the coupled system stabilizes a composite electron-lattice ordered state in which the lattice polarization spontaneously forms a polarization density wave (PDW), accompanied by an electronic stripe order in the 2DEG. This intertwined order partially reconstructs the electronic spectrum and generates a twofold quasiparticle anisotropy, giving rise to electronic nematicity at the single-particle level. However, under strong external electric fields, the nematic response becomes dominated by the collective sliding dynamics of the composite order: the sliding motion overwhelms the quasiparticle anisotropy and produces a strongly enhanced nematic signal with higher-order angular harmonics. The theory offers a natural explanation for several anomalous transport and anisotropic responses recently observed at the KTaO$_3$ (111) interface. We also estimate the mean-field transition temperature of this emergent ordered state, obtaining good agreement with experiments, and analyze its evolution with several tuning parameters. The proposed composite order, along with the field-induced crossover from quasiparticle-driven to sliding-dominated nematicity, provides a distinct mechanism of nematicity arising from many-body effects and collective dynamics in critical electron-boson systems, with applicability beyond ferroelectric platforms.

*Prashanta K. Mukharjee,Sebastian Erdmann,Lichen Wang,Julian Kaiser,Anton Jesche,Pascal Puphal,Masahiko Isobe,Matthias Hepting,Bernhard Keimer,Philipp Gegenwart,Alexander A. Tsirlin*

Our data for in-plane magnetic fields show a strongly anisotropic $c^{*}$-axis lattice response, which is dominated by the variation of Co--O--Co bond angles according to \textit{ab initio} calculations. At $T = 0.4$~K, the magnetization $M(B)$ exhibits step-like features that are also highly anisotropic. In the case of $B \parallel b$, a small hysteresis observed around the second field-induced magnetic transition ($B_{c2}$) indicates its first-order character, whereas divergence of the magnetic Grüneisen parameter at $B_{c2}$ is suppressed upon cooling and signals the absence of quantum critical behavior upon entering the field-polarized state. None of our thermodynamic measurements provide evidence for a field-induced quantum spin liquid state near or above $B_{c2}$.

### [115] [Characterization of Feshbach resonances in $^6\mathrm{Li}{-}^7\mathrm{Li}$ using improved interaction potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02361)
*Jing-Chen Zhang,Paul Julienne,Yu Liu*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过改进锂二聚体（Li₂）的相互作用势，表征了所有同位素变体中的Feshbach共振（Feshbach resonances），并预测了异核⁶Li-⁷Li系统中的s波Feshbach共振特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在改进锂二聚体（Li₂）系统的相互作用势，以更精确地描述所有同位素变体（isotopologues）中的Feshbach共振现象，为制备超冷Li₂分子提供理论基础。

Method: 基于光谱学精确的Morse/长程（MLR）势能曲线，对单重态（X¹Σ⁺）和三重态（a³Σ⁺）电子态应用内壁调整，通过拟合阈值测量数据优化势能，并采用耦合通道散射计算（coupled-channels scattering calculations）预测共振特性。

Result: 成功预测了⁶Li-⁷Li同位素变体中的s波Feshbach共振，发现其最低能量超精细通道（hyperfine channel）中的共振均为窄共振（~0.01-0.1 G），强闭合通道主导，且主要呈现三重态电子自旋特征，与同核系统形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 优化的势能为设计拉曼光学转移路径（Raman optical-transfer pathways）提供了基础，可用于在所有三种同位素变体中制备处于X¹Σ⁺和a³Σ⁺势能深束缚振转能级的超冷Li₂分子。

Abstract: We characterize Feshbach resonances in all isotopologues of the $\mathrm{Li}{-}\mathrm{Li}$ system with improved interaction potentials. Starting from spectroscopically accurate Morse/long-range (MLR) potential-energy curves for the singlet ($X^{1}Σ^{+}$) and triplet ($a^{3}Σ^{+}$) electronic states of $\mathrm{Li}_2$, we apply small phenomenological inner-wall adjustments (following Julienne and Hutson, Phys. Rev. A 89, 052715 (2014), arXiv:1404.2623v3) and fit the resulting potentials to threshold measurements for the $^{6}\mathrm{Li}{-}^{6}\mathrm{Li}$ and $^{7}\mathrm{Li}{-}^{7}\mathrm{Li}$ isotopologues, including binding energies, scattering lengths, and Feshbach resonance positions. Using the optimized potentials in coupled-channels scattering calculations, we predict and characterize s-wave Feshbach resonances in the $^{6}\mathrm{Li}{-}^{7}\mathrm{Li}$ isotopologue. In its lowest-energy hyperfine channel, all resonances are narrow ($\sim 0.01{-}0.1$ G), strongly closed-channel dominated, and predominantly triplet in electronic spin character, in marked contrast to the homonuclear systems. These results provide a foundation for designing Raman optical-transfer pathways to produce ultracold $\mathrm{Li}_2$ molecules in deeply bound rovibrational levels of both the $X^1Σ^{+}$ and $a^3Σ^{+}$ potentials across all three isotopologues.

### [116] [Tensor renormalization group approach to the $O(2)$ models via symmetry-twisted partition functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02739)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种基于对称性扭曲配分函数的高效方法，用于探测O(2)模型中的各种临界现象。该方法旨在通过张量重整化群框架实现高效计算，并能够检测连续对称性的自发破缺和BKT相变等复杂物理过程。

Method: 研究方法采用对称性扭曲配分函数结合张量重整化群（tensor renormalization group）框架。该方法通过计算有限扭曲角下的螺旋度模量（helicity modulus）来探测相变，并应用于三维和二维O(2)模型以及二维广义O(2)模型的分析。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）在三维O(2)模型中，对称性扭曲配分函数能够有效检测全局连续对称性的自发破缺；2）在二维O(2)模型中，该方法通过直接提供有限扭曲角下的螺旋度模量，成功确定了BKT相变点；3）在二维广义O(2)模型中，该方法成功识别了铁磁相-向列相（ferromagnetic-nematic）以及向列相-顺磁相（nematic-paramagnetic）之间的相变。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了对称性扭曲配分函数结合张量重整化群方法在分析O(2)模型临界现象中的有效性。该方法不仅能够检测连续对称性的自发破缺和BKT相变，还能成功识别广义O(2)模型中的复杂相变行为，为研究类似系统的相变提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We investigate critical phenomena in the $O(2)$ models using symmetry-twisted partition functions that can be efficiently computed within the tensor renormalization group framework. We first demonstrate, taking the three-dimensional model as an example, that symmetry-twisted partition functions detect the spontaneous breaking of global continuous symmetry. We then consider the same model in two dimensions, where the Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless (BKT) transition occurs. Since symmetry-twisted partition functions directly provide the helicity modulus at a finite twist angle, we determine the BKT transition point. These results are presented based on Ref.~\cite{Akiyama:2026dzg}. Finally, in addition to the original paper~\cite{Akiyama:2026dzg}, we apply this approach to the two-dimensional generalized $O(2)$ model and confirm that it successfully identifies the phase transitions between the ferromagnetic and nematic phases, as well as between the nematic and paramagnetic phases.

</details>


### [117] [Solving sign problems with physics-informed kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03159)
*Friederike Ihssen,Renzo Kapust,Jan M. Pawlowski*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于物理信息核（physics-informed kernels）的新型生成架构，用于处理具有复杂概率分布的系统采样任务，同时解决符号问题（sign problems）和高效采样两大挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂概率分布系统的采样任务面临两大挑战：符号问题（sign problems）的解决和高效采样。现有方法难以同时应对这两个问题，需要新的架构设计。

Method: 该架构基于物理信息核（physics-informed kernels, PIKs），其核心特性是概率权重保持性质（probability-weight preserving property）。通过这一性质，可以将采样任务映射到无符号问题（sign-problem free）的流形上，该流形具有简单分布和高效采样特性。

Result: 该架构的潜力在零维复耦合场论（zero-dimensional field theories with complex couplings）和量子力学谐振子（quantum-mechanical harmonic oscillator）的实时演化（real-time evolution）应用中得到了验证。

Conclusion: 基于物理信息核的新型生成架构能够同时解决复杂概率分布系统中的符号问题和高效采样挑战，为相关物理系统的模拟提供了有效工具。

Abstract: In the present work we construct a novel generative architecture for systems with complex probability distributions. In general, these sampling tasks come with two challenges: resolving sign problems and efficient sampling. The architecture is based on physics-informed kernels (PIKs) introduced in arXiv:2510.26678, and aims at resolving both challenges. Key to the complex PIK-architecture is its probability-weight preserving property, which allows us to map the sampling task to one on a sign-problem free manifold with a simple distribution and efficient sampling. The potential of this novel architecture is demonstrated within applications to zero-dimensional field theories with complex couplings, as well as the real-time evolution of the quantum-mechanical harmonic oscillator.

### [118] [Kosterlitz-Thouless transition in uniformly confined $^4$He](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02388)
*Filip Novotný,Marek Talíř,Balázs Szalai,Emil Varga*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过纳米通道限制的超流体氦-4，揭示了二维转子激发（2D rotons）而非关联长度标度（correlation length scaling）主导了Kosterlitz-Thouless（KT）转变的有限尺寸行为，实现了对绝对转变温度的准确预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管超流体密度（superfluid density）的普适跃变（universal jump）是已知现象，但基于薄膜几何预测绝对转变温度（absolute transition temperature）一直存在挑战，通常依赖经验拟合。本研究旨在解决这一长期难题。

Method: 使用片上纳米流体亥姆霍兹谐振器（on-chip nanofluidic Helmholtz resonators），通道高度分别为10、15和20纳米，通过第四声共振模式（4th sound resonant modes）探测转变。将二维转子激发（2D rotons）纳入静态KT理论（static KT theory）。

Result: 实验观察到相对于体相λ点（bulk lambda point）的转变温度偏移可由二维热激发（two-dimensional thermal excitations）准确解释。包含转子激发的KT理论能够预测与实验测量和历史数据一致的绝对转变温度，无需传统关联长度标度论证（coherence length scaling arguments）。KT理论的动力学扩展（AHNS）完全描述了转变附近观察到的耗散峰（dissipation peaks）。

Conclusion: 研究提供了有力证据，表明转子激发（roton excitations）而非关联长度标度（correlation length scaling）主导了受限超流体氦-4的有限尺寸行为（finite-size behaviour），解决了长期存在的转变温度预测难题。

Abstract: This study investigates the Kosterlitz-Thouless (KT) transition in superfluid $^4$He confined within uniform nanochannels. While the universal jump in superfluid density is a well-established phenomenon, predicting the absolute transition temperature ($T_{KT}$) based on film geometry has remained a long-standing challenge, often relying on empirical fits. Using on-chip nanofluidic Helmholtz resonators with channel heights of 10, 15, and 20 nm, we probe the transition using 4th sound resonant modes.We demonstrate that the observed shift in the transition temperature relative to the bulk lambda point ($T_λ$) is accurately accounted for by including two-dimensional thermal excitations, specifically 2D rotons. By incorporating these roton-like excitations into the static KT theory, we can predict absolute transition temperatures that align with our experimental measurements and historical data without invoking traditional coherence length scaling arguments. Furthermore, we show that the dynamical extension of the KT theory (AHNS) fully describes the dissipation peaks observed near the transition without requiring ad-hoc free vortex contributions. These results provide compelling evidence that roton excitations, rather than correlation length scaling, govern the finite-size behaviour of confined superfluid $^4$He

</details>


### [119] [Geometry-Driven Thermodynamics: Shape Effects and Anisotropy in Quantum-Confined Ideal Fermi and Bose Gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02634)
*Rivo Herivola Manjakamanana Ravelonjato,Ravo Tokiniaina Ranaivoson,Raoelina Andriambololona,Naivo Rabesiranana,Charles Oyverné Randriamaholisoa,Wilfrid Chrysante Solofoarisina*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究基于量子相空间（QPS）形式体系，提出了纳米尺度约束下理想量子气体热力学的统一描述。该框架同时处理费米-狄拉克和玻色-爱因斯坦统计，揭示了纳米热力学固有的各向异性特性，并展示了纯几何形状效应如何调控相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立纳米尺度约束下理想量子气体热力学的统一理论框架。通过量子相空间（Quantum Phase Space, QPS）形式体系，将费米-狄拉克和玻色-爱因斯坦统计纳入单一描述，以理解纳米系统中量子效应的影响。

Method: 采用量子相空间（QPS）形式体系，其中统计动量方差B_ll捕捉量子简并性：对于费米子包含费米能（Fermi energy），对于玻色子包含凝聚能标。该方法从统一框架推导出内能、各向异性压力张量和热容等关键性质的精确解析表达式。

Result: 研究揭示了纳米热力学固有的各向异性：压力变为方向依赖，在极端约束下分数各向异性可达单位值。纯形状效应（通过B_ll中的几何参数控制）可在不改变系统尺寸、温度或密度的情况下调控相变。对约束电子和氦-4气体的数值模拟显示，在5-50 nm约束尺度和mK至K温度范围内存在显著量子效应。

Conclusion: 该工作为纳米系统提供了理论工具包，对纳米流体器件和量子传感器具有直接应用价值。量子相空间形式体系成功统一描述了从经典到量子区域的转变，为纳米尺度热力学研究建立了普适框架。

Abstract: This study presents a unified description of the thermodynamics of ideal quantum gases under nanoscale confinement using a Quantum Phase Space (QPS) formalism. We show that the statistical momentum variances B_ll capture quantum degeneracy: for fermions, they incorporate the Fermi energy, and for bosons, the condensate energy scale. This bridges our formalism with established results and allows both Fermi-Dirac and Bose-Einstein statistics to be treated within a single framework. From this, we derive exact analytical expressions for key properties - internal energy, anisotropic pressure tensor, and heat capacity - seamlessly describing the transition from classical to quantum regimes. Our results reveal that nanoscale thermodynamics is intrinsically anisotropic: pressure becomes direction-dependent, with fractional anisotropy reaching unity under extreme confinement. Notably, pure shape effects, controlled via geometric parameters in B_ll, enable manipulation of phase transitions without altering system size, temperature, or density. Numerical simulations for confined electron and helium-4 gases show significant quantum effects at accessible temperatures (mK to K) for confinement scales of 5-50 nm. This work provides a theoretical toolkit for nanosystems, with direct implications for nanofluidic devices and quantum sensors.

</details>


### [120] [First-order transition into a topological superfluid state in an atom-cavity system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03034)
*Hannah Kleine-Pollmann,Ludwig Mathey*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种结合高布洛赫带玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation）和驱动-耗散腔-BEC系统的混合光-物质平台，用于实现拓扑超流态（topological superfluid state）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种新型量子光学多体系统平台，用于工程化非平凡轨道序（orbital order）和拓扑超流相（topological superfluid phases）。通过结合高布洛赫带凝聚和腔-BEC系统，旨在实现可控的拓扑态制备。

Method: 方法包括将凝聚体囚禁在具有可调能量偏移的双分格s-p_x-p_y晶格中，实现从s轨道到近简并p_x和p_y轨道的受控布居转移。采用截断Wigner模拟（truncated Wigner simulations）和互补的平均场分析（mean-field analysis）来确定相变性质。

Result: 系统形成了具有p_x ± i p_y对称性的手性基态（chiral ground state），并产生交错轨道电流（staggered orbital currents）。通过增加横向泵浦强度，系统被驱动进入超辐射相（superradiant phase），形成自组织的密度棋盘结构，将交错手性序整流为拓扑超流态。相变被确定为一级相变（first order phase transition）。

Conclusion: 结论表明，耦合到腔的高带凝聚体为在量子光学多体系统中工程化非平凡轨道序和拓扑超流相提供了一个有前景的平台。该混合光-物质系统能够实现可控的拓扑态制备和相变调控。

Abstract: We propose to combine Bose-Einstein condensation in higher Bloch bands and a driven-dissipative cavity-BEC system into a hybrid light-matter platform. Specifically, the condensate is trapped in a bipartite $s$-$p_x$-$p_y$-lattice, with a tunable energy offset. This enables a controlled population transfer from the $s$-orbital to the nearly degenerate $p_x$ and $p_y$ orbitals. The system forms a chiral ground state with $p_x \pm i p_y$ symmetry, with staggered orbital currents. By increasing the transverse pump strength, we drive the system into the superradiant phase, resulting in a self-organized, density checkerboard, which rectifies the staggered chiral order into a topological superfluid state. Using truncated Wigner simulations and complementary mean-field analysis, we determine the phase transition into this state as first order. Our results show that higher-band condensates coupled to a cavity provide a promising platform for engineering non-trivial orbital order and topological superfluid phases in quantum optical many-body systems.

### [121] [Hamilton Revised: The Action Principle for Initial Value Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02350)
*W. A. Horowitz,A. Rothkopf*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过取量子力学中Schwinger-Keldysh表达式的经典极限，提出了经典保守力点粒子力学初值问题的变分作用量原理，澄清了Keldysh路径中正负路径的物理意义及其在经典极限归一化中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立经典保守力点粒子力学初值问题的变分作用量原理（variational action principle），并通过严谨推导澄清Hamilton原理在推导Euler-Lagrange方程时位置变分与速度变分的关系。研究动机源于对Schwinger-Keldysh形式经典极限的深入理解需求。

Method: 通过取量子力学中算符期望值时间依赖性的Schwinger-Keldysh表达式的经典极限（classical limit），严格推导出经典变分作用量原理。该方法特别关注正负Keldysh路径（plus and minus Keldysh paths）在经典极限中的行为。

Result: 研究发现正负Keldysh路径均具有经典路径和涨落，而非传统认知中仅正路径提供经典解而负路径提供涨落。负路径的经典解恒为零且时间反演传播，因此在Schwinger-Keldysh形式主义的经典极限中无需手动设负路径为零。该结果对经典极限的正确归一化至关重要。

Conclusion: 本文建立的变分作用量原理为经典力学初值问题提供了新视角，澄清了Schwinger-Keldysh形式经典极限中路径的物理行为。研究结果对非完整约束（non-holonomic constraints）的经典与量子力学以及场导数依赖规范（gauges dependent on the derivatives of the fields）的量子场论具有重要启示。

Abstract: We present the variational action principle for initial value problems in classical, conservative-force point particle mechanics. We rigorously derive this formulation by taking the classical limit of the Schwinger-Keldysh expression for the time dependence of the expectation value for operators in quantum mechanics. We clarify the connection between the variation of the position and the variation of the velocity of a particle when implementing Hamilton's Principle in deriving the Euler-Lagrange Equations. We show that both the plus and minus Keldysh paths (of the average and difference of the forward/backward paths) have classical paths and fluctuations -- unlike the common perception that the minus path provides the fluctuations around the single classical solution given by the plus path -- and that the fluctuations of both paths are crucial for the correct normalization of the classical limit. The classical limit yields "initial conditions" and equations of motion for the minus paths such that the unique classical solution for the minus paths is that they are identically zero, and, fascinatingly, that the minus paths' solution propagates backwards in time; thus one does not need to set the minus paths to zero by hand when taking the classical limit of the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism. We note implications for the classical and quantum mechanics of non-holonomic constraints and quantum field theories with gauges dependent on the derivatives of the fields.

</details>

### [122] [Fluctuating environments are sufficient to drive substantial variability in species abundance across locations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02403)
*James F. D. Henderson,Andreas Tiffeau-Mayer*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 该研究通过最小化模型量化了时空变化环境中物种丰度的非平衡分布，揭示了环境波动与迁移平衡如何影响物种丰度空间异质性，并发现了噪声诱导的双峰不平等转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于量化物种在时空变化环境中丰度分布的非平衡效应，即使在没有持久位置偏好的情况下，环境波动也会导致物种在不同位置的丰度差异。

Method: 采用最小化模型方法，研究具有时间平均中性竞争但位置依赖环境波动的空间分隔群落，通过解析推导两点不平等分布，并分析迁移松弛与波动强度的平衡关系。

Result: 研究结果包括：推导了两点不平等分布，表征了迁移松弛与波动强度平衡如何决定分布的整体和极值统计特性；发现了噪声诱导的双峰不平等转变，该转变依赖于环境波动的相关时间尺度。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在具有时间相关性的环境中，有限迁移率具有进化优势，这为理解物种在变化环境中的空间分布模式提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Species growing in environments that change in time and space will vary in their abundance across locations, even in the absence of persistent location preferences. Here we quantify this non-equilibrium effect by studying a minimal model of a spatially compartmentalised community with time-averaged-neutral competition but location-dependent environmental fluctuations. We analytically derive distributions of two-point inequality, defined as the log-ratio of a species' abundance across a pair of locations. We characterise how the balance of relaxation via migration and fluctuation strength determine the bulk and extreme value statistics of these distributions in the two-patch and infinite-patch cases. We demonstrate the existence of a noise-induced transition to bimodal inequality, which depends on the correlation timescale of the environmental fluctuations. Finally, we discuss the evolutionary benefit of finite migration rates in environments with temporal correlations.

### [123] [Selecting Optimal Variable Order in Autoregressive Ising Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20394)
*Shiba Biswal,Marc Vuffray,Andrey Y. Lokhov*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 该论文提出通过推断底层数据的马尔可夫随机场结构来构建优化的变量排序，以改进自回归模型的采样性能。在二维类图像模型上的实验表明，基于图结构的排序能减少条件集复杂度并提高生成样本的保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归模型（autoregressive models）的性能严重依赖于变量排序（variable ordering），因为排序决定了条件分布（conditional distributions）的复杂度。现有方法缺乏对底层数据结构的利用，导致次优的变量排序选择。

Method: 该方法首先学习描述底层数据的马尔可夫随机场（Markov random field），然后利用推断出的图模型结构（graphical model structure）构建优化的变量排序。特别针对二维类图像模型（two-dimensional image-like models），通过结构感知的排序实现受限的条件集（restricted conditioning sets）。

Result: 在离散数据的伊辛模型（Ising models）上的数值实验表明，基于图信息的排序（graph-informed orderings）相比朴素变量排序（naive variable orderings）能产生更高保真度的生成样本（higher-fidelity generated samples）。

Conclusion: 利用底层图结构信息来指导变量排序是提升自回归模型采样性能的有效策略，特别是在具有空间结构的二维数据上，结构感知的排序能显著降低模型复杂度并改善生成质量。

Abstract: Autoregressive models enable tractable sampling from learned probability distributions, but their performance critically depends on the variable ordering used in the factorization via complexities of the resulting conditional distributions. We propose to learn the Markov random field describing the underlying data, and use the inferred graphical model structure to construct optimized variable orderings. We illustrate our approach on two-dimensional image-like models where a structure-aware ordering leads to restricted conditioning sets, thereby reducing model complexity. Numerical experiments on Ising models with discrete data demonstrate that graph-informed orderings yield higher-fidelity generated samples compared to naive variable orderings.

### [124] [Data Unfolding: From Problem Formulation to Result Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03168)
*Nikolay D. Gagunashvili*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 该论文讨论了在粒子物理、核物理等实验数据反卷积（unfolding）过程中，如何独立于外部信息，使用内部标准评估反演结果质量的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验测量的概率密度函数（PDFs）由于分辨率、偏差和效率效应而偏离真实PDFs。可靠的PDF估计对于检验理论模型、比较不同实验结果以及整合各类研究至关重要，但缺乏外部标准时难以评估反卷积质量。

Method: 论文探讨了多种内部标准（internal criteria）来独立评估反卷积结果质量，同时分析了影响反演分布质量的各种因素。这些方法不依赖于外部信息，适用于缺乏先验测量的情况。

Result: 论文系统讨论了在缺乏外部评估标准时，如何通过内部标准独立评估反卷积质量的方法框架。这些内部标准能够为反卷积过程提供质量评估依据，特别是在先前未进行过类似测量的情况下。

Conclusion: 内部质量评估标准为反卷积过程提供了独立的质量判断依据，特别是在缺乏外部参考的情况下。理解影响反演分布质量的因素对于获得可靠的PDF估计至关重要。

Abstract: Experimental data in particle and nuclear physics, particle astrophysics, and radiation protection dosimetry are collected using experimental facilities that consist of a complex system of sensors, electronics, and software. Measured spectra or cross sections are considered as Probability Density Functions (PDFs) that deviate from true PDFs due to resolution, bias, and efficiency effects. Unfolding is viewed as a procedure for estimating an unknown true PDF. Reliable estimates of the true PDF are necessary for testing theoretical models, comparing results from different experiments, and combining results from various research endeavors. Both external and internal quality assessment methods can be applied for this purpose. In some cases, external criteria exist to evaluate deconvolution quality. A typical example is the deconvolution of a blurred image, where the sharpness of the restored image serves as an indicator of quality. However, defining such external criteria can be challenging, particularly when a measurement has not been performed previously. This paper discusses various internal criteria for assessing the quality of the results independently of external information, as well as factors that influence the quality of the unfolded distribution.

</details>


<div id='cs.CC'></div>

# cs.CC [[Back]](#toc)

### [125] [Computational Complexity of Physical Counting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.15571)
*Tristan Simas*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 该论文研究了因子化状态空间中决定最优动作的坐标特征，提出了决策商（decision quotient）作为最小抽象，并建立了决策复杂度度量与多种数学物理概念的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解因子化状态空间 $\mathcal{D}=(A,S,U)$ 中哪些坐标决定最优动作，其中 $S=X_1\times\cdots\times X_n$。目标是识别充分坐标集（sufficient coordinate set）并构建最小抽象来保持最优动作信息。

Method: 方法包括：定义充分坐标集 $I$ 和决策商 $Q=S/{\sim}$ 作为最小抽象；从纯数学角度证明十四个基本原理定理；分析计算复杂度问题，包括 SUFFICIENCY-CHECK 和 MINIMUM-SUFFICIENT-SET 的 coNP-完全性等。

Result: 结果表明：决策商 $Q$ 是保持最优动作的最小抽象；Fisher信息、熵、最优输运、率失真和热力学均独立恢复 $\mathrm{srank}$ 作为决策复杂度度量；贝叶斯更新唯一最小化期望对数损失；多个复杂度问题被证明为完全问题。

Conclusion: 论文建立了决策理论与多种数学物理框架的深刻联系，证明决策复杂度 $\mathrm{srank}$ 可从多个独立途径推导得出。在经验条件下，决策精度受熵产生限制，最小 $\sigma$ 与 $\mathrm{srank}$ 成比例。

Abstract: We characterize which coordinates of a factored state space determine optimal actions. For $\mathcal{D}=(A,S,U)$ with $S=X_1\times\cdots\times X_n$, coordinate set $I$ is sufficient if $s_I=s'_I\Rightarrow\operatorname{Opt}(s)=\operatorname{Opt}(s')$. The decision quotient $Q=S/{\sim}$ ($s\sim s'\Leftrightarrow\operatorname{Opt}(s)=\operatorname{Opt}(s')$) is the minimal abstraction: any abstraction preserving optimal actions factors uniquely through $Q$.
  We prove fourteen first-principles theorems (thirteen from pure mathematics, one empirical). The chain from counting measure to probability to Bayes' theorem to $Q$ follows from finite set cardinality. Fisher information, entropy, optimal transport, rate-distortion, and thermodynamics each independently recover $\mathrm{srank}$ as decision complexity measure. From $\log x\leq x-1$ alone, Bayesian updating uniquely minimizes expected log loss.
  Complexity: SUFFICIENCY-CHECK and MINIMUM-SUFFICIENT-SET are coNP-complete; ANCHOR-SUFFICIENCY is $Σ_2^P$-complete; stochastic and sequential variants PP- and PSPACE-complete with strict separation. Six subcases admit polynomial algorithms. Under ETH, succinct encodings carry $2^{Ω(n)}$ lower bounds. Verification requires $\geq 2^{n-1}$ witness pairs.
  Two results carry empirical conditions. Conditional on Landauer's principle ($k_BT\ln 2$ per bit erasure; experimentally confirmed 2012), $dU\geqλ\,dC$ follows by composition with bit-operation bounds; rejecting it requires rejecting Landauer. Conditional on stochastic thermodynamics (Barato--Seifert 2015), $\mathrm{Var}(J)/\langle J\rangle^2\geq 2/σ$ bounds decision precision by entropy production, minimal $σ$ scaling with $\mathrm{srank}$.

</details>

### [126] [Unveiling Davydov-Split Excitons in a Template-Engineered Molecular-Graphene Heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02301)
*Jan Kunc,Bohdan Morzhuk,Veronika Stará,Devanshu Varshney,Mykhailo Shestopalov,Kryštof Matějka,Martin Rejhon,Jiří Novák,Jan Čechal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种纳米制造协议，恢复了SiC上外延石墨烯的原子级纯度，使其达到超高真空（UHV）水平。这一纯净界面使HMTP分子层中出现了宏观激子相干性，通过多种光谱技术解析了复杂的振动能级结构，揭示了暗态激子分支主导辐射通道的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机-无机量子模拟器的高保真实现常受限于器件制备过程中引入的界面缺陷。本研究旨在通过开发一种稳健的纳米制造协议，恢复外延石墨烯界面的原子级纯度，为研究激子动力学和开发固态分子量子存储器建立可扩展平台。

Method: 采用纳米制造协议恢复SiC上外延石墨烯的原子级纯度，通过低能电子衍射（Low-Energy Electron Diffraction）和显微技术验证其达到UHV水平。在纯净界面上沉积HMTP分子层，结合高灵敏度傅里叶变换光电流光谱（Fourier Transform Photo-current Spectroscopy）、光致发光和动态拉曼映射技术解析振动能级结构。使用基于ARPES推导的分子间耦合和分子动力学模拟验证的拉曼振动模式参数化的分析紧束缚模型（analytical tight-binding model）。

Result: HMTP分子层的P6₃/m晶体对称性解除了HOMO-LUMO跃迁的简并度，产生了离散的亮态和暗态激子分支。量化了极化能（polarization energy）、黄-里斯因子（Huang-Rhys factor）以及对Franck-Condon模型的Herzberg-Teller修正。研究发现暗态激子分支主导辐射通道，遵循与Kasha规则一致的极化子介导弛豫路径（polaron-mediated relaxation pathway）。

Conclusion: 该工作通过将宏观器件架构与UHV级表面科学相协调，建立了一个可扩展的研究平台，可用于研究暗态激子动力学（dark-exciton dynamics）和开发固态分子量子存储器（solid-state molecular quantum memories）。

Abstract: The realization of high-fidelity organic-inorganic quantum emulators is frequently hindered by the interfacial imperfections introduced during device fabrication. Here, we demonstrate a robust nanofabrication protocol that restores the atomic-scale purity of epitaxial graphene on SiC to UHV-equivalent levels, as confirmed by Low-Energy Electron Diffraction, and Microscopy. This pristine interface enables the emergence of macroscopic excitonic coherence in epitaxial overlayers of 2,3,6,7,10,11-hexamethoxytriphenylene (HMTP), a model molecular system characterized by intense electron-phonon coupling. Through a combination of high-sensitivity Fourier Transform Photo-current Spectroscopy, photoluminescence, and dynamic Raman mapping, we resolve a complex vibronic manifold governed by Davydov splitting. We show that the $P6_3/m$ crystalline symmetry of the HMTP overlayer lifts the degeneracy of the HOMO-LUMO transition, creating discrete bright and dark excitonic branches. Using an analytical tight-binding model parameterized by ARPES-derived intermolecular coupling and Raman vibrational modes validated by molecular dynamics simulations, we quantify the polarization energy, the Huang-Rhys factor, and Herzberg-Teller corrections to the Franck-Condon model. Our results reveal that the dark-state branch dominates the radiative channel, following a polaron-mediated relaxation pathway consistent with Kasha's rule. By reconciling macroscopic device architecture with UHV-level surface science, this work establishes a scalable platform for the study of dark-exciton dynamics and the development of solid-state molecular quantum memories.

### [127] [Graphene-capped bismuthene on SiC as a platform for correlated quantum spin Hall edge states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02397)
*Huu Thoai Ngo,Zamin Mamiyev,Niclas Tilgner,Andres David Pena Unigarro,Sibylle Gemming,Thomas Seyller,Christoph Tegenkamp*

TL;DR: 该研究通过在SiC(0001)衬底上插层铋并氢化处理，制备了石墨烯覆盖的铋烯（bismuthene）岛，实现了受对称性保护的拓扑边缘态，为高温量子自旋霍尔（QSH）输运提供了可调控平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外延铋烯在SiC(0001)上具有大带隙内的对称性保护金属边缘态，是高温量子自旋霍尔（quantum spin Hall, QSH）输运的潜在二维拓扑绝缘体。研究旨在实现可控边缘终止的铋烯结构，并探索其拓扑特性。

Method: 通过在SiC(0001)上的零层石墨烯下插层铋（intercalating Bi），随后进行氢化处理，制备了具有明确边缘终止的铋烯岛。利用光谱学测量表征边缘态特性，并分析石墨烯覆盖层与铋烯的相互作用。

Result: 光谱测量证实边缘态位于体带隙内且保持电荷中性。石墨烯覆盖层与铋烯仅发生弱相互作用，既保护了拓扑特性又提供了环境稳定性。一维边缘通道显示出比独立铋烯增强的电子关联特征。

Conclusion: 石墨烯覆盖的铋烯建立了稳健且可调控的相关量子自旋霍尔态平台，其边缘物理受到邻近效应修饰，为研究高温QSH输运提供了新途径。

Abstract: Epitaxial bismuthene on SiC(0001) hosts symmetry-protected metallic edge states within a large bulk band gap, establishing it as a promising two-dimensional topological insulator for hightemperature quantum spin Hall (QSH) transport. Here we realize bismuthene islands by intercalating Bi beneath zero-layer graphene on SiC(0001) followed by hydrogen treatment, yielding well-defined edges with controlled terminations. Spectroscopic measurements demonstrate that the edge states reside inside the bulk band gap and remain charge neutral. The graphene overlayer interacts only weakly with the bismuthene, preserving its topological character while providing environmental protection. Notably, the one-dimensional edge channels exhibit signatures of enhanced electronic correlations relative to freestanding bismuthene, suggesting proximity-induced modification of the QSH edge physics. These results establish graphene-capped bismuthene as a robust and tunable platform for correlated quantum spin Hall states.

### [128] [Modulating Surface Acoustic Wave Generation through Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02415)
*Andrew Christy,Yuzan Xiong,Rui Sun,Yi Li,Kenneth O. Chua,Andrew H. Comstock,Junming Wu,Sidong Lei,Frank Tsui,Megan N. Jackson,Dali Sun,Valentine Novosad,James F. Cahoon,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究开发了基于氮化铌（NbN）叉指换能器（IDTs）的表面声波（SAW）器件，在低温量子应用中克服了传统铝（Al）和金（Au）电极的局限性，实现了通过超导态转变精细控制声波传输的开关功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统表面声波（SAW）器件使用铝（Al）或金（Au）电极，但在量子应用所需的低温环境下存在缺陷：Al电极会形成双能级系统（two-level systems），而Au电极缺乏超导性导致欧姆损耗（Ohmic losses）。因此需要开发适用于低温量子应用的新型SAW器件材料。

Method: 采用氮化铌（NbN）作为叉指换能器（IDTs）和布拉格反射器（Bragg reflectors）材料，通过光刻（photolithography）和反应离子刻蚀（reactive ion etching, RIE）工艺制造声学器件，工作频率范围为高MHz至低GHz。

Result: NbN在超导态和正常态之间的尖锐转变对应SAW传输的显著变化，实现了器件"开"（超导）和"关"（正常）状态的精细控制，传输差异达到16倍。SAW传输行为与NbN在临界温度（Tc）处的电阻变化一致。

Conclusion: 该研究为将NbN SAW谐振器集成到现有的基于NbN的量子架构中提供了新途径，并开发了一种不依赖于外加电压即可调节传输特性的方法，为量子声学器件的发展开辟了新可能性。

Abstract: Surface acoustic waves (SAWs), with their five orders-of-magnitude slower propagation velocity, allow for considerably shorter wavelengths at the same frequency compared to electromagnetic waves. The short wavelengths allow for device miniaturization and on-chip integration. The generic design of these devices involve piezoelectric substrates with comblike arrays of Al or Au electrodes known as interdigitated transducers deposited on the surface. However, Al and Au both have shortcomings at the cryogenic temperatures required for quantum applications, namely the formation of two-level systems and the lack of superconductivity perpetuating Ohmic losses, respectively. In this work, SAWs are generated in the high-MHz to low-GHz range using niobium nitride (NbN) interdigitated transducers (IDTs) and Bragg reflectors. We demonstrate the fabrication of acoustic devices through photolithography and reactive ion etching (RIE). The sharp transition between superconducting and normal states and the corresponding change in SAW transmission allows for fine control of the 'on' (superconducting) and 'off' (normal) states of NbN, with a Δ_T = K separating the transmission minimum and maximum. We demonstrate a 16x difference in transmission between the 'on' and 'off' states of the device. The SAW transmission behavior mirrors the change in resistance of NbN at its Tc. These findings open up new possibilities for the integration of NbN SAW resonators into existing quantum architectures based on NbN and a method for adjusting transmission properties independent of applied voltage.

</details>


### [129] [Anomalous Klein tunnelling with magnetic barriers in strained graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03240)
*Edgardo Marin-Colli,Tonatiuh Gómez-Ramírez,O-Excell Gutierrez,Yonatan Betancur-Ocampo,Alfredo Raya,Erik Díaz-Bautista*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 研究应变石墨烯中电子在N个静电和磁势垒序列中的输运特性，发现应变与磁场的相互作用产生反常克莱因隧穿（anomalous Klein tunnelling），电导可通过应变和势垒配置有效调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究应变石墨烯（strained graphene）在静电和磁势垒序列中的电子输运行为，探索机械变形与外部磁场相互作用对电荷传输的影响，为调控二维材料电子特性提供理论基础。

Method: 采用改进的转移矩阵框架（modified and improved transfer-matrix framework），分析单轴应变（uniaxial strain）和势垒数量变化对透射系数（transmission coefficients）和反射系数（reflection coefficients）的影响。

Result: 发现机械变形与磁场的相互作用产生反常克莱因隧穿现象，电导（conductance）可通过应变和势垒配置有效调制，应变工程（strain engineering）和磁场调制成为调控电荷传输的有力工具。

Conclusion: 应变工程和磁场调制是调控二维材料电荷传输的有效手段，机械和电磁控制可用于设计具有可调电子特性的下一代固态器件（solid-state devices）。

Abstract: We study electron transport in a strained graphene sheet subjected to a sequence of $N$ electrostatic and magnetic barriers. Employing a modified and improved transfer-matrix framework, we examine how the transmission and reflection coefficients evolve with variations in uniaxial strain and in the number of barriers. The interplay of mechanical deformation and external magnetic fields is found to generate an anomalous Klein tunnelling, allowing the conductance to be effectively modulated through strain and barrier configurations. These findings highlight the role of strain engineering and magnetic field modulation as powerful tools for tailoring charge transport in two-dimensional materials. More broadly, they underscore how mechanical and electromagnetic control can be used to design next-generation solid-state devices with tunable electronic properties.

</details>


### [130] [Designing XY and Dzyaloshinskii--Moriya couplings in Majorana Cooper pair boxes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02713)
*Manato Teranishi,Shintaro Hoshino,Ai Yamakage*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该理论研究如何设计马约拉纳库珀对盒（MCB）网络中的自旋耦合，通过正常金属引线连接，利用传导电子介导的RKKY相互作用实现任意类型的耦合，特别是XY交换相互作用和DM相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索如何设计马约拉纳库珀对盒（Majorana Cooper pair boxes, MCBs）网络中的自旋耦合，以克服先前MCB方案中难以实现特定相互作用的限制，为工程化量子自旋系统提供更灵活的平台。

Method: 通过理论分析由多个正常金属引线（normal-metal leads）连接的马约拉纳库珀对盒网络，利用传导电子介导的Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida（RKKY）相互作用来生成盒间相互作用，并通过门控隧穿振幅（gate-controlled tunneling amplitudes）连续调节耦合的符号和大小。

Result: 研究结果表明，马约拉纳与引线的连接性使得能够实现任意类型的耦合，特别是成功展示了XY交换相互作用（XY exchange interaction）和Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya（DM）相互作用的实现，这些在先前提出的MCB方案中难以实现。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了马约拉纳库珀对盒作为工程化量子自旋系统的多功能平台，其耦合的符号和大小可通过门控隧穿振幅连续调节，为实现复杂的量子自旋相互作用提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: We theoretically study how to design spin couplings in networks of Majorana Cooper pair boxes (MCBs) connected by multiple normal-metal leads. The inter-box interaction is generated by the conduction-electron-mediated Ruderman--Kittel--Kasuya--Yosida (RKKY) interaction. We show that the connectivity of Majoranas to the leads enables arbitrary types of couplings. As concrete examples, we show the realization of the XY exchange interaction and the Dzyaloshinskii--Moriya (DM) interaction, which are difficult to implement in previously proposed MCB-based schemes. The sign and magnitude of the couplings can be tuned continuously via gate-controlled tunneling amplitudes. These results establish MCBs as a versatile platform for engineered quantum spin systems.

</details>


### [131] [Electrical driving of hole spin states in planar silicon MOS device by g-matrix modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02746)
*Aaquib Shamim,Scott D. Liles,Joe Hillier,Jonathan Y. Huang,Isaac Vorreiter,Pratik Chowdhury,Chris C. Escott,Fay E. Hudson,Wee Han Lim,Kok Wai Chan,Rajib Rahman,Andrew S. Dzurak,Alexander R. Hamilton*

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了平面硅空穴量子点中的自旋控制机制，通过g矩阵形式区分不同自旋驱动机制的贡献，并识别出自旋对电荷噪声较不敏感的区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IV族量子点中的空穴自旋因其固有的自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）而成为CMOS兼容自旋量子比特（spin qubits）的有前景平台，但自旋轨道耦合在实现快速电控自旋操作的同时也使量子比特暴露于电荷噪声（charge noise）的影响。

Method: 研究采用g矩阵形式（g-matrix formalism）来区分不同自旋驱动机制的贡献，通过绘制拉比频率（Rabi frequency）随磁场方向变化的依赖关系图，系统分析了平面硅空穴量子点（planar silicon hole quantum dot）中的自旋控制机制。

Result: 研究发现拉比频率在面内方向（in-plane direction）最大，在接近面外方向（out-of-plane direction）最小，这有助于识别自旋对电荷噪声较不敏感的操作区域。

Conclusion: 该研究增强了在工业相关架构中对不同自旋驱动机制贡献的理解，为建立空穴量子比特（hole qubits）快速相干操控的操作条件提供了指导。

Abstract: Hole spins in group IV quantum dots are a highly promising way to develop CMOS compatible spin qubits owing to their inherent spin-orbit coupling, which enables fast, coherent, and electrical spin control. However, spin-orbit coupling not only enables multiple spin-control mechanisms, but also exposes the qubits to charge noise. In this work, we perform a systematic study of the spin control mechanism in a planar silicon hole quantum dot. We use g-matrix formalism to discern contributions from the various spin driving mechanisms and identify regions where spins are less sensitive to charge noise. By mapping out the dependence of the Rabi frequency on the magnetic field orientation, we observe the largest Rabi frequency in the in-plane direction and the smallest Rabi frequency close to the out-of-plane direction. These results enhance the understanding of how different mechanisms contribute to spin driving within an industrially relevant architecture and aid in establishing the operating conditions for the rapid and coherent manipulation of hole qubits.

### [132] [Gate Stack Engineering for High-Mobility and Low-Noise SiMOS Quantum Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02814)
*Md. Mamunur Rahman,Ensar Vahapoglu,Kok Wai Chan,Tuomo Tanttu,Ajit Dash,Jonathan Yue Huang,Venkatesh Chenniappan,Fay Hudson,Christopher C. Escott,Yik Kheng Lee,Arne Laucht,Andrea Morello,Andre Saraiva,Jared H. Cole,Andrew S. Dzurak,Wee Han Lim*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究系统探讨了硅金属氧化物半导体（SiMOS）量子器件中材料工程、量子输运与低频电荷噪声之间的相互作用。通过结合霍尔棒输运测量与栅极定义量子点的电荷噪声谱分析，揭示了栅极堆栈设计、载流子迁移率与静电噪声之间的相关性，为低噪声、高迁移率操作的硅自旋量子比特平台提供了材料与工艺优化指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在系统探究硅金属氧化物半导体（SiMOS）量子器件中材料工程、量子输运与低频电荷噪声之间的相互作用关系。通过建立材料工艺参数与器件性能的关联，为开发低噪声、高迁移率的硅自旋量子比特（silicon spin-qubit）平台提供实验依据。

Method: 采用霍尔棒（Hall-bar）输运测量与栅极定义量子点（gate-defined quantum dots）的电荷噪声谱（charge-noise spectroscopy）相结合的方法。通过系统改变栅极堆栈（gate-stack）设计参数，包括Al₂O₃的原子层沉积温度、氧化剂选择以及HfO₂的引入，对比分析其对载流子迁移率（carrier mobility）和电荷噪声的影响。

Result: 提高Al₂O₃的原子层沉积温度显著增强了载流子迁移率，而氧化剂选择影响甚微。引入HfO₂的器件显示出改善的迁移率，可能归因于铝从栅金属扩散到HfO₂层带来的缺陷钝化（defect passivation）。电荷噪声测量显示高迁移率与低噪声强相关，TiPd栅极器件同时表现出输运性能下降和电荷噪声升高。相比之下，多晶硅栅极（poly-Si-gated）CMOS代工厂器件实现了最低的噪声水平。双反馈点-传感器稳定性映射（dual-feedback dot-sensor stability mapping）证实了所研究栅极堆栈器件具有增强的电荷稳定性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了硅MOS量子器件中材料工艺参数、载流子迁移率与电荷噪声之间的明确关联，为优化栅极堆栈设计提供了指导。多晶硅栅极CMOS代工厂器件表现出最低噪声特性，而所研究的栅极堆栈结构在电荷稳定性方面展现出优势，这为构建可扩展、高保真度的硅自旋量子比特平台奠定了材料基础。

Abstract: We systematically investigate the interplay between materials engineering, quantum transport, and low-frequency charge noise in silicon metal--oxide--semiconductor (SiMOS) quantum devices. By combining Hall-bar transport measurements with charge-noise spectroscopy of gate-defined quantum dots, we identify correlations between gate-stack design, carrier mobility, and electrostatic noise, providing an experimental case study of material and process dependencies relevant to low-noise, high-mobility operation. Hall-bar studies reveal that increasing the atomic-layer-deposition temperature of Al$_2$O$_3$ markedly enhances mobility, whereas the choice of oxidant has little impact. Devices incorporating HfO$_2$ exhibit improved carrier mobility, an interesting observation that can plausibly be attributed to defect passivation associated with aluminum diffusion from the gate metal into the HfO$_2$ layer. Charge-noise measurements show a strong correlation between higher mobility and reduced noise, with TiPd-gated devices displaying both degraded transport and elevated charge noise. In contrast, poly-Si-gated CMOS-foundry devices achieve the lowest noise levels. Finally, dual-feedback dot--sensor stability mapping demonstrates enhanced charge stability in devices with the gate stacks studied here, underscoring their promise for scalable, high-fidelity silicon spin-qubit platforms.

</details>


### [133] [Learning Hamiltonians for solid-state quantum simulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02889)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 训练后的模型能够超越训练域进行泛化，从输运数据（transport data）中准确推断哈密顿量参数。虽然模型具有有限容量——当参数空间变得过大或结构多样时性能会下降——但识别出了保持稳健泛化的区域。进一步展示了模型如何处理噪声测量，反映真实实验条件。

Conclusion: 该框架成功实现了从实验数据中自动表征可编程固态模拟器，通过将物理约束直接嵌入神经网络架构，确保了学习表示的物理意义。尽管存在容量限制，但在特定区域内能够保持稳健的泛化能力，并能处理真实实验中的噪声测量。

Abstract: We introduce a generalizable framework for learning to identify effective Hamiltonians directly from experimental data in solid-state quantum systems. Our approach is based on a physics-informed neural network architecture that embeds physical constraints directly into the model structure. Unlike purely data-driven supervised schemes, the proposed unsupervised autoencoder-based method incorporates the governing physics (here, the S-matrix formalism) within the decoder network, ensuring that the learned representations remain physically meaningful. Through numerical learning experiments, we demonstrate automated characterization of programmable solid-state simulators from transport measurements, exemplified by a triple quantum dot chain. The trained model generalizes beyond the training domain and accurately infers Hamiltonian parameters from transport data. While the model has finite capacity -- leading to degraded performance when the parameter space becomes excessively large or structurally diverse -- we identify regimes in which robust generalization is maintained. We further show how to train the model to handle noisy measurements, reflecting realistic experimental conditions.

Abstract: The Rice-Mele (RM) model, as a paradigmatic extension of the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) chain, plays a pivotal role in understanding topological phases and quantized adiabatic transport in one-dimensional systems. Its realization in acoustic systems, however, has been hindered by the need for simultaneous precise modulation of on-site potentials and couplings. In this work, we demonstrate a method to linearly tune on-site potentials and couplings, thus realizing an acoustic Rice-Mele model. During parameter evolution, the system exhibits a Thouless pump, with the acoustic field distribution adiabatically shifting from the left edge through the bulk to the right edge, fully consistent with tight-binding model predictions. Moreover, the strategy of leveraging geometric parameters to linearly and precisely control on-site potentials and couplings is highly effective and universal for designing acoustic metamaterials, and it can be extended to other classical wave systems.

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the chaotic behavior of spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance in magnetic tunnel junctions (MTJs) with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy under thermal fluctuations. By calculating the Lyapunov exponent based on the Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation, we demonstrate that an MTJ characterized by a double-well potential, composed of uniaxial magnetic anisotropy and an external magnetic field, exhibits chaotic magnetization dynamics that can be controlled by means of the DC current bias. Furthermore, we find that thermal fluctuations help to induce these chaotic magnetization dynamics, which can be regarded as noise-induced chaos. This research provides a basis for brain-inspired computing using spintronic devices and advances the understanding of the interplay between thermal fluctuations and chaos in magnetization dynamics.

### [138] [Scaling of silicon spin qubits under correlated noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03051)
*Juan S. Rojas-Arias,Leon C. Camenzind,Yi-Hsien Wu,Peter Stano,Akito Noiri,Kenta Takeda,Takashi Nakajima,Takashi Kobayashi,Giordano Scappucci,Daniel Loss,Seigo Tarucha*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅基自旋量子比特（silicon spin qubits）作为容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computing）的候选硬件，其空间相关噪声（spatially correlated noise）会同时产生多个错误，削弱量子纠错（quantum error correction, QEC）所需的冗余性，因此需要量化相关噪声的影响。

Method: 研究在五量子比特硅阵列（five-qubit silicon array）中量化了噪声相关的空间范围，并评估其对量子纠错的影响。通过识别两种不同的相关噪声源：全局磁场漂移（global magnetic field drifts）和来自双能级涨落器（two-level fluctuators）的电荷噪声（charge noise）。

Result: 全局磁场漂移产生完全相关波动，会损害量子纠错但可通过缓解措施应对；电荷噪声产生短程相关，在相邻量子比特内衰减，其相关性适中、可电调谐，且与容错操作兼容，仅需最小量子比特开销。

Conclusion: 该研究为相关噪声建立了量化基准，阐明了此类相关性如何影响可扩展量子比特阵列中量子纠错的可行性。结果表明硅基自旋量子比特在适当的噪声管理下具有实现容错量子计算的潜力。

Abstract: The path to fault-tolerant quantum computing hinges on hardware that scales while remaining compatible with quantum error correction (QEC). Silicon spin qubits are a leading hardware candidate because they combine industrial fabrication compatibility with a nanoscale footprint that could accommodate millions of qubits on a chip. However, their suitability for QEC remains uncertain since spatially correlated noise naturally emerges from the resulting close proximity of qubits. These correlations increase the likelihood of simultaneous errors and erode the redundancy that QEC depends on. Here we quantify the spatial extent of noise correlations in a five-qubit silicon array and assess their impact on QEC. We identify two distinct sources of correlated noise: global magnetic field drifts that generate perfectly correlated fluctuations, and charge noise from two-level fluctuators that produces short-range correlations decaying within neighboring qubits. While magnetic drifts represent a critical correlated noise source that can compromise QEC, they can be mitigated. In contrast, the measured charge noise correlations are moderate, electrically tunable, and compatible with fault-tolerant operation with minimal qubit overhead. Our results establish quantitative benchmarks for correlated noise and clarify how such correlations impact the viability of quantum error correction in scalable qubit arrays.

### [139] [Kinetic coefficients of two-dimensional electrons with strong Zeeman splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03105)

Abstract: In nanostructures with two-dimensional (2D) electrons and very low defect densities, a hydrodynamic transport regime has recently been realized. In this regime, 2D electrons form a viscous fluid due to frequent electron-electron collisions. Many unusual and mysterious magnetotransport and high-frequency effects have been observed in these systems. Their understanding is crucial for a general comprehending the formation of hydrodynamic transport. Two-component electronic systems, where there are two types of carriers with different concentrations and relaxation times, are of particularly interest. These systems can be realized by filling two lower subbands in a quantum well with electrons, or by filling one subband and applying a strong magnetic field in the well plane, leading to a Zeeman splitting of the subband. In this work, we construct the hydrodynamic equations for a viscous two-component electronic fluid for a Zeeman-type two-component 2D electronic system. By solving the kinetic equation, we calculate the relaxation rates of the first and second harmonics of the two-component distribution function. The resulting balance hydrodynamic equations take into account the effect of shear viscosity in each component and the effect of the friction between the two components. The lastleads to the alignment of the velocities of the two components of the fluid. The obtained equations can be used to explain magnetotransport measurements in ultra-pure nanostructures in an inclined magnetic field, where two-component electronic fluid is formed.

### [140] [All-Electrostatic Valley Filtering by Barrier Rotation in Tilted Dirac/Weyl Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03117)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克/外尔半金属（Dirac/Weyl semimetals）中具有倾斜各向异性能量色散的载流子在静电势垒界面处表现出谷依赖的折射和反射，这为谷过滤提供了新的可能性。研究旨在探索纯静电途径实现谷过滤，避免使用真实或赝磁场等次级效应。

Method: 开发了适用于倾斜各向异性狄拉克哈密顿量（tilted, anisotropic Dirac Hamiltonian）的广义转移矩阵形式，并将其扩展至处理任意角度的静电势垒。在旋转势垒框架中计算透射率，并在有限器件几何结构中模拟谷分辨轨迹。

Conclusion: 倾斜静电势垒界面提供了一种纯静电途径实现狄拉克/外尔半金属中的谷过滤，为谷电子学器件设计提供了新的思路，避免了传统方法中所需的磁场或赝磁场调控。

Abstract: Charge carriers in Dirac/Weyl semimetals with tilted anisotropic energy dispersion exhibit valley-dependent refraction and reflection at electrostatic barrier interfaces. Here, we show that an angled barrier interface provides a purely electrostatic route to valley filtering, producing finite valley-polarized conductance. We develop a generalized transfer-matrix formalism for the tilted, anisotropic Dirac Hamiltonian, extended to treat electrostatic barriers at arbitrary angles, and calculate the transmission in the rotated-barrier frame. We also present simulated valley-resolved trajectories in a finite device geometry, which clearly show that one valley is selectively transmitted, whereas the other is predominantly reflected by the angled barrier, without secondary effects such as real or pseudo-magnetic fields.
