### [141] [Simultaneous anti-bunched and super-bunched photons from a GaAs Quantum dot in a dielectric metasurface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03186)
*Sanghyeok Park,Oleg Mitrofanov,Kusal M. Abeywickrama,Samuel Prescott,Jaeyeon Yu,Stephanie C Malek,Hyunseung Jung,Emma Renteria,Sadhvikas Addamane,Alisa Javadi,Igal Brener,Prasad P Iyer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体量子点（semiconductor quantum dots）中的激子复合体（excitonic complexes）能够产生反聚束单光子（anti-bunched single photons）和超聚束光子（super-bunched photons），但带电激子复合体的发射通常比中性激子弱数个数量级，限制了同一发射器的双模量子操作。

Method: 研究将单个GaAs量子点嵌入介电米氏共振超表面（dielectric Mie-resonant metasurface）中，该结构为量子点的中性和带电激子跃迁（neutral and charged exciton transitions）提供了数量级的光致发光增强。

Result: 在相同非共振泵浦条件下，中性激子发射呈现反聚束特性（g^(2)(0) < 0.5），而带正电激子复合体发射显示超聚束特性（g^(2)(0) > 3.5），两者计数率相当（约12 kHz）。超聚束仅在带电激子发射与米氏共振光谱重叠时出现。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了光子工程对于访问弱量子光态的重要性，并展示了一个可扩展、位置容忍的平台，可用于充分利用固态发射器的完整激子结构。

Abstract: Semiconductor quantum dots host a rich manifold of excitonic complexes, including neutral excitons that emit anti-bunched single photons and charged exciton complexes capable of producing super-bunched photons via cascade emission. Accessing both emission regimes from a single emitter would open routes to novel quantum protocols, including advanced quantum imaging. In practice, however, emission from charged exciton complexes is intrinsically weak, often orders of magnitude dimmer than neutral excitons, placing simultaneous dual-mode operation out of reach. Here, we overcome this limitation by embedding the quantum dot in a dielectric Mie-resonant metasurface that provides order-of-magnitude photoluminescence enhancement across both neutral and charged exciton transitions of a single GaAs quantum dot. Under identical non-resonant pumping conditions, the emission from the neutral exciton yields anti-bunched emission ($g^{(2)}(0) < 0.5$) and the emission from positively charged exciton complexes shows super-bunched emission ($g^{(2)}(0) > 3.5$) with comparable count rates (~12 kHz). Crucially, super-bunching emerges only when charged exciton emission spectrally overlaps with the Mie resonances and vanishes in un-patterned slabs, demonstrating that photonic engineering, is essential for accessing these weak quantum light states. These results demonstrate a scalable, position-tolerant platform for harnessing the full excitonic structure of solid-state emitters.

### [142] [Direct Scattering of the Focusing Nonlinear Schrödinger Equation with Step-like Oscillatory Initial Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02855)
*Tamara Grava,Robert Jenkins,Xiaofan Zhang,Zechuan Zhang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了非线性薛定谔方程（nonlinear Schrödinger equation）阶梯状行波解（step-like traveling-wave solutions）的正散射问题（direct scattering problem）和逆散射问题（inverse scattering problem），建立了散射数据的解析性质，并将逆问题表述为黎曼-希尔伯特问题（Riemann-Hilbert problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是建立非线性薛定谔方程阶梯状行波解的散射理论框架。具体关注初始数据在无穷远处趋近于椭圆行波（elliptic traveling waves）的情形，这类问题在数学物理中具有重要意义。

Method: 研究方法包括：在适当初始数据假设下，首先构建正散射问题并分析散射数据的解析性质；然后将逆散射问题表述为黎曼-希尔伯特问题，并证明其可解性；最后指出该黎曼-希尔伯特表述是完整孤子气体（full soliton-gas）初始数据情形的特例。

Result: 主要结果包括：建立了阶梯状行波解散射问题的完整理论框架，证明了散射数据的解析性质，将逆问题成功表述为黎曼-希尔伯特问题，并证明了该问题的可解性。同时揭示了该表述与完整孤子气体初始数据问题的联系。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了非线性薛定谔方程阶梯状行波解的散射理论，将逆散射问题转化为黎曼-希尔伯特问题并证明其可解性。这一理论框架为处理更一般的孤子气体初始数据问题提供了基础。

Abstract: In this manuscript we set up the direct and inverse scattering problems for step-like traveling-wave solutions of the nonlinear Schrödinger equation. Specifically, we consider initial data $u(x,0)$ satisfying $u(x,0)\to u_0^\ell(x)$ as $x\to-\infty$ and $u(x,0)\to u_0^r(x)$ as $x\to+\infty$, where $u_0^\ell(x)$ and $u_0^r(x)$ are elliptic traveling waves. Under suitable assumptions on the initial data we formulate the direct scattering problem and establish analytic properties of the scattering data. We then formulate the inverse problem as a Riemann--Hilbert problem and prove its solvability. Finally, we observe that this Riemann--Hilbert formulation is a special case of the one arising for full soliton-gas initial data.

### [143] [Structural Viscosity, Thermal Waves, and the Mpemba Effect from Extended Structural Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02249)
*Patrick BarAvi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了扩展结构动力学（Extended Structural Dynamics, ESD）框架，将流体组分描述为具有取向、角动量和内部变形模式的扩展对象，推导出双曲-抛物型输运方程，预测了有限传播速度、各向异性输运和热波等非经典现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典流体力学基于点粒子理想化，导致抛物型输运方程、无限信号速度，无法捕捉有限时间弛豫、各向异性输运或非傅里叶热现象。需要建立能够描述扩展结构特征的动力学框架。

Method: 引入扩展结构动力学（ESD）框架，从扩展玻尔兹曼方程（extended Boltzmann equation）出发，采用Chapman-Enskog展开和BGK闭合（BGK closure），推导出两个双曲-抛物型输运定律。

Result: 推导出动力学自旋方程（dynamical spin equation）和热流弛豫方程（heat flux relaxation equation），预测动量与热的有限传播速度、固有激波正则化、各向异性输运和热波。自旋方程为微极性流体理论（micropolar fluid theory）提供动力学推导，热流方程为Cattaneo-Vernotte行为提供微观基础。

Conclusion: 结构贡献可主导经典输运系数，BGK闭合保持扩展相空间的几何结构并捕捉正确标度。建立了取向弛豫时间与李雅普诺夫不稳定性（Lyapunov instability）的联系，标度定律源于旋转-平动耦合。预测包括胶体椭球体的Mpemba交叉时间和不对称分子的激波宽度，均可用现有技术验证。

Abstract: Classical hydrodynamics rests on the point-particle idealization, leading to parabolic transport equations, infinite signal speeds, and the inability to capture finite time relaxation, anisotropic transport, or non Fourier thermal phenomena. This work introduces Extended Structural Dynamics (ESD), a kinetic framework in which constituents are described as spatially extended objects possessing orientation, angular momentum, and internal deformation modes. Starting from an extended Boltzmann equation, a Chapman Enskog expansion with BGK closure yields two hyperbolic parabolic transport laws: a dynamical spin equation coupling orientational relaxation to fluid vorticity, and a heat flux relaxation equation with structural thermal conductivity. These equations predict finite propagation speeds for momentum and heat, intrinsic shock regularization, anisotropic transport, and thermal waves. The spin equation provides a kinetic derivation of micropolar fluid theory, while the heat flux equation supplies a microscopic foundation for Cattaneo Vernotte behavior. Quantitative estimates indicate structural contributions can dominate classical transport coefficients. The BGK closure preserves the qualitative geometric structure of extended phase space and captures correct scaling; the connection between the orientational relaxation time and Lyapunov instability is established independently. The resulting scaling laws follow from rotational-translational coupling. Predictions include Mpemba crossover time for colloidal ellipsoids and shock width for asymmetric molecules, both testable with existing techniques.

</details>

Method: 采用三阶展开（third order expansion）近似Wigner-Kirkwood对易函数，通过对动量积分将其从经典相空间转换到位置构型空间；同时使用Metropolis蒙特卡洛（Metropolis Monte Carlo）计算机模拟方法研究液态Lennard-Jones $^4$He体系。

### [145] [Strong Zero Modes via Commutant Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02326)
*Sanjay Moudgalya,Olexei I. Motrunich*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文通过系统搜索发现，许多强零模（Strong Zero Modes）实例可理解为对易代数框架中的对称性，揭示了包括横场伊辛链在内的已知强零模哈密顿量中隐藏的新代数结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强零模（Strong Zero Modes, SZMs）是导致某些哈密顿量整个谱（近似）双重简并的（近似）守恒量，横场伊辛链的马约拉纳零模是主要示例。本研究旨在系统探索强零模的代数本质及其与对称性的关系。

Method: 采用对易代数（commutant algebra）框架进行系统搜索，将强零模理解为该框架中的对称性。利用揭示的代数结构构造破坏可积性但精确保持强零模的相互作用。

Result: 研究发现许多强零模实例可理解为对易代数中的对称性，揭示了包括横场伊辛链在内的已知模型中的新颖代数结构。该框架统一了文献中不同强零模示例的理解，阐明了它们与物质基态相的联系，并揭示了简单模型中的新对称性，如在某些参数值下伴随强零模的精确准局域U(1)对称性。

Conclusion: 强零模存在两种类型：一种在可积性破坏后仍存在，另一种则不能。对易代数理解可扩展至自旋-1/2 XYZ链中著名的Fendley强零模的非相互作用极限，但相互作用情况下的强零模无法在此框架中理解。该框架还提供了构造Fendley强零模替代证明的方法。

Abstract: Strong Zero Modes (SZMs) are (approximately) conserved quantities that result in (approximate) double degeneracies in the entire spectra of certain Hamiltonians, with the Majorana zero mode of the transverse-field Ising chain being a primary example. In this work, we discover via a systematic search that many examples of SZMs can be understood as symmetries in the commutant algebra framework, which reveals novel algebraic structures hidden in Hamiltonians with well-known SZMs, including the transverse-field Ising chain. Our findings unify the understanding of different examples of SZMs in the literature, demystify their connections to ground state phases of matter, and reveal novel symmetries in simple models, such as exact quasilocal $U(1)$ symmetries that sometimes accompany the SZMs such as in the spin-1/2 XY model for certain parameter values. Moreover, while analytically tractable SZMs have mostly been demonstrated only for non-interacting or integrable models, the algebraic structures revealed in this work can be exploited to construct integrability-breaking interactions that exactly preserve these SZMs. Such non-integrable models are expected to show more clear dynamical signatures of SZMs without the interference of other conserved quantities that appear in integrable models, and we discuss many examples, including those of novel hydrodynamic modes associated with such symmetries for some special parameter values. We also show that while this commutant understanding extends to the non-interacting limit of the celebrated Fendley SZM in the spin-1/2 XYZ chain, the SZM in the interacting case cannot be understood in this framework. This suggests that there are two types of SZMs -- those that survive integrability breaking and those that do not. We close by using this commutant understanding to construct an alternate proof of the Fendley SZM, which might be of independent interest.

</details>


### [146] [Low-temperature transition of 2d random-bond Ising model and quantum infinite randomness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02308)
*Akshat Pandey,Aditya Mahadevan,A. Alan Middleton,Daniel S. Fisher*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过重整化群方法分析了二维随机键伊辛模型（2D random bond Ising model）的零温临界点，建立了伊辛模型热力学与量子哈密顿量谱特性的映射关系，揭示了向无限随机性（infinite randomness）的流动行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解二维随机键伊辛模型在低温下经历的由挫败（frustration）驱动的铁磁体-顺磁体转变，该转变由分离铁磁相和自旋玻璃相（spin glass phases）的零温固定点控制。

Method: 通过重整化群变换（renormalization group transformation）构建伊辛模型的基态，从无挫败模型开始迭代添加挫败直至达到目标哈密顿量。将二维伊辛模型的热力学映射到相关厄米矩阵（Hermitian matrix）的谱特性，该矩阵对应非相互作用量子问题的哈密顿量。

Result: 重整化群过程对应于量子哈密顿量的迭代对角化。伊辛图像中向零温的流动表现为量子哈密顿量谱向无限随机性的流动，哈密顿量的对数能隙（log gap）随系统尺寸呈幂律标度：$\log \varepsilon_{\it min}^{-1} \sim L^ψ$。隧穿指数（tunneling exponent）$ψ$等于表征零温固定点的自旋刚度指数（spin stiffness exponent）$θ_c$。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了二维随机键伊辛模型零温临界点与量子哈密顿量谱无限随机性固定点之间的对应关系，揭示了隧穿指数与自旋刚度指数的等价性，为理解这类挫败驱动相变提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: At low temperatures, the classical two-dimensional random bond Ising model undergoes a frustration-driven ferromagnet-to-paramagnet transition controlled by a zero-temperature fixed point separating ferromagnet and spin glass phases. We show that this critical point can be understood through a renormalization group transformation that constructs the ground state of the Ising model through a sequence of Hamiltonians that, starting with an unfrustrated model, iteratively adds in frustration until the target Hamiltonian is reached. Via a mapping of the thermodynamics of the 2d Ising model to the spectral properties of a related Hermitian matrix -- the Hamiltonian of a noninteracting quantum problem -- this RG procedure corresponds to an iterative diagonalization of the quantum Hamiltonian. The flow toward zero temperature in the Ising picture manifests as a flow toward infinite randomness in the spectrum of the quantum Hamiltonian, with the log gap of the Hamiltonian scaling as a power of the system size: $\log \varepsilon_{\it min}^{-1} \sim L^ψ$. The tunneling exponent $ψ$ is equal to the spin stiffness exponent $θ_c$ characterizing the zero-temperature fixed point.

</details>


### [147] [Universality classes, Thermodynamics of Group Entropies, and Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02385)
*Henrik Jeldtoft Jensen,Petr Jizba,Piergiulio Tempesta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出群熵（group entropies）作为超越玻尔兹曼-吉布斯统计力学的统一框架，通过配置空间W(N)的渐近标度定义熵的普适类，并证明其与经典热力学定律的一致性，特别是应用于黑洞热力学时能自然导出负比热等特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统玻尔兹曼-吉布斯统计力学（Boltzmann-Gibbs statistical mechanics）仅适用于弱至中等关联系统，对于强关联或长程相互作用系统，其配置空间呈现非指数增长，现有广义熵理论缺乏与经典热力学定律的连贯联系。

Method: 提出群熵作为统一框架，通过配置空间W(N)的渐近标度定义熵的普适类（universality classes），确保熵的广延性；将熵表达为热力学状态变量，取热力学极限，类比克劳修斯熵从玻尔兹曼-吉布斯形式中的涌现过程。

Result: 群熵框架与经典热力学一致，基于热力学第零定律识别经验温度，利用卡拉西奥多里第二定律表述推导绝对温度；应用于黑洞热力学时，拉伸指数行为的群熵类自然导出黑洞的负比热特性，同时保持熵的广延性，适用于贝肯斯坦-霍金和巴罗熵标度。

Conclusion: 群熵为超越玻尔兹曼-吉布斯范式的热力学表述提供了基础框架，建立了广义熵理论与经典热力学定律的连贯联系，特别在黑洞热力学等强关联系统中展现出理论一致性。

Abstract: Conventional Boltzmann--Gibbs statistical mechanics successfully describes systems with weak to moderate correlations, where the number of accessible configurations $W(N)$ grows exponentially with the number of degrees of freedom~$N$. However, this framework breaks down for systems with strong correlations or long-range interactions, for which the configuration space exhibits non-exponential growth. While numerous generalized entropies have been proposed to address this limitation, a coherent link to classical thermodynamic laws has remained elusive. Here, we propose group entropies as a unifying framework, defining universality classes of entropies through the asymptotic scaling of $W(N)$, each yielding an extensive entropy. We show that this approach provides the basis for a consistent thermodynamic formulation beyond the Boltzmann--Gibbs paradigm. In particular, by expressing these entropies in terms of thermodynamic state variables and taking the thermodynamic limit, we demonstrate their consistency with classical thermodynamics, in close analogy to the emergence of the Clausius entropy from the Boltzmann--Gibbs formalism. Focusing on the zeroth thermodynamic law, we identify the empirical temperature and, by using Carathéodory's formulation of the second law, we derive the associated absolute temperature. As an application of the thermodynamic framework obtained, we analyze black-hole thermodynamics using the group entropy class corresponding to stretched-exponential behavior of $W(N)$. In particular, we show that a hallmark property of black holes -- their negative specific heat -- emerges naturally within this framework while the entropy remains extensive. This result holds for the stretched-exponential entropies associated with both the Bekenstein--Hawking and Barrow entropy scalings.

</details>


### [148] [Enhancing entanglement asymmetry in fragmented quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02338)
*Lorenzo Gotta,Filiberto Ares,Sara Murciano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究纠缠不对称性（entanglement asymmetry）作为多体量子态对称性破缺的度量，特别关注非均匀U(1)荷（如偶极矩和多极矩），建立了典型不对称性的普适上界，并在随机矩阵乘积态中验证了该行为，揭示了局域遍历系统中U(1)荷不对称性的普适动力学结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠缠不对称性为多体量子态中的对称性破缺提供了定量度量。研究聚焦于非均匀U(1)荷（如偶极矩和多极矩），旨在理解这些对称性破缺的普适行为及其在希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert-space fragmentation）系统中的特殊表现。

Method: 通过分析随机矩阵乘积态（random matrix product states）并识别键维数（bond dimension）与有效时间的对应关系，定性再现了随机量子电路中纠缠不对称性动力学的近期发现。使用对易代数形式（commutant algebra formalism）将纠缠不对称性推广到碎片化对称性的情形。

Result: 研究发现典型不对称性受限于其最大值的特定分数，并在多个设定中验证了这一行为。在随机矩阵乘积态中，通过键维数-时间对应关系，揭示了局域遍历系统中U(1)荷不对称性的普适动力学结构。对于碎片化系统，推导了传统对称性和碎片化对称性的普适上界，并识别了达到这些上界的量子态。

Conclusion: 纠缠不对称性在传统对称性中呈对数增长，而在碎片化系统中可以呈现广延标度（extensive scaling），这为区分经典碎片化与真正量子碎片化提供了探测手段。研究结果表明纠缠不对称性能够有效探测希尔伯特空间碎片化系统的对称性结构。

Abstract: Entanglement asymmetry provides a quantitative measure of symmetry breaking in many-body quantum states. Focusing on inhomogeneous $U(1)$ charges, such as dipole and multipole moments, we show that the typical asymmetry is bounded by a specific fraction of its maximal value, and verify this behavior in several settings, including random matrix product states. Within the latter ensemble, by identifying the bond dimension with an effective time, we qualitatively reproduce recent findings on the entanglement asymmetry dynamics in random quantum circuits, thereby suggesting a universal dynamical structure of the asymmetry of $U(1)$ charges in local ergodic systems. Multipole charges naturally arise in systems with Hilbert-space fragmentation, where the dynamics splits into exponentially many disconnected sectors. Using the commutant algebra formalism, we generalize entanglement asymmetry to account for fragmentation. We derive general upper bounds for both conventional and fragmented symmetries and identify states that saturate them. While the asymmetry grows logarithmically for conventional symmetries, it can scale extensively in fragmented systems, providing a probe that distinguishes classical from genuinely quantum fragmentation.

</details>


### [149] [Hyperuniformity of Weighted Particle Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02521)
*Salvatore Torquato,Jaeuk Kim,Michael A. Klatt,Roberto Car,Paul J. Steinhardt*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究将超均匀性（hyperuniformity）概念推广到带权重粒子系统，建立了描述权重空间分布涨落的广义理论框架，并发现粒子系统的超均匀性不一定对应权重系统的超均匀性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超均匀性概念仅描述粒子位置的涨落特性，但许多物理系统涉及带权重的粒子（如具有标量、矢量、张量等内部自由度）。需要建立广义理论来描述权重空间分布的涨落行为。

Method: 通过推导广义加权对关联函数（weighted pair correlation）、自协方差函数（autocovariance）和谱函数（spectral functions），建立描述加权多粒子系统局部方差的理论形式体系。

Result: 应用于键取向有序相（bond-orientational ordered phases）、偶极液态水（dipolar liquid water）、Voronoi胞体积和特定离子液体，发现粒子系统的超均匀性不一定导致权重系统的超均匀性。存在超均匀粒子系统加权后变为反超均匀（antihyperuniform），以及非超均匀或反超均匀粒子系统产生超均匀权重系统的情况。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为量化加权多粒子系统的大尺度涨落提供了路线图，成为识别具有新颖物理性质系统的有力工具。

Abstract: Hyperuniform particle arrangements are characterized by a local number variance that grows more slowly than the volume of the observation window. We generalize this concept to describe particle systems in which particles carry weights: internal degrees of freedom such as scalars, vectors, pseudovectors, directors, tensors, or extrinsic local attributes. Our generalization extends hyperuniformity from fluctuations in particle positions to fluctuations in the spatial distribution of weights. We derive generalized weighted pair correlation, autocovariance, and spectral functions, and show their relation to the local variance in weighted many-particle systems. Applying this formalism to bond-orientational ordered phases, dipolar liquid water, Voronoi-cell volumes, and certain ionic liquids, we demonstrate that hyperuniformity in the particle system does not necessarily translate to hyperuniformity of the weighted system. In fact, cases exist where a hyperuniform particle system becomes antihyperuniform when weighted, and others where nonhyperuniform or antihyperuniform particle systems yield hyperuniform weighted systems. This theoretical framework provides a road map for quantifying large-scale fluctuations in weighted many-particle systems, offering a powerful tool for identifying systems with novel physical properties.

</details>


### [150] [Singularity of information flow at the Hopf bifurcation point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02632)
*Kenshin Matsumoto,Shin-ichi Sasa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析随机热力学中的关键量——学习率（learning rate），探讨了Hopf分岔点附近信息流的奇异行为。以Brusselator为模型系统，研究发现学习率在确定性极限下仍保持有限，表明信息流可通过概率描述在确定性动力学中量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究Hopf分岔点附近信息流的奇异行为，通过分析学习率这一随机热力学中的关键量来理解动力学行为变化如何反映在信息流中，为分析生化振荡中的信息处理提供理论基础。

Method: 以Brusselator作为展示Hopf分岔的模型系统，首先在稳态区域数值计算学习率。线性分析用于再现稳态结果，但在分岔点附近失效。为克服此限制，采用确定性分岔理论中著名的奇异摄动方法，对Langevin方程描述的随机系统进行显式计算。

Result: 数值计算显示学习率在确定性极限下保持有限，表明信息流可通过概率描述在确定性动力学中量化。线性分析能准确再现稳态结果，但在分岔点附近失效。奇异摄动方法成功评估了分岔点附近的学习率，并理论推导了其在确定性极限下的非光滑行为。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明动力学行为的变化会反映在信息流中，这为分析生化振荡中的信息处理提供了基础。通过将奇异摄动方法应用于随机系统，成功量化了分岔点附近的信息流行为，揭示了确定性极限下学习率的非光滑特性。

Abstract: We investigate the singular behavior of information flow near the Hopf bifurcation point by analyzing the learning rate, a key quantity in stochastic thermodynamics. As a model system exhibiting the Hopf bifurcation, we study the Brusselator. We first numerically compute the learning rate in the stationary regime and find that it remains finite even in the deterministic limit, suggesting that information flow can be quantified in deterministic dynamics through probabilistic descriptions. Linear analysis accurately reproduces the numerical results in the stationary regime but fails near the bifurcation point. To overcome this limitation, we employ the singular perturbation method, well known in deterministic bifurcation theory, and carry out the corresponding calculation explicitly for a stochastic system described by a Langevin equation. This allows us to evaluate the learning rate near the bifurcation point. We then theoretically derive its non-smooth behavior in the deterministic limit. Our results demonstrate that changes in dynamical behavior are reflected in the information flow and provide a basis for analyzing information processing in biochamical oscillations.

### [151] [Ising models on the hydrogen peroxide and other lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02962)
*Xiaofeng Qian,Youjin Deng,Lev N. Shchur,Henk W. J. Blöte*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）方法分析三维伊辛模型（Ising model）在多种晶格上的临界行为，结合有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）获得临界点与标度维度，并改进了描述临界奇异性与标度修正的普适参数精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过分析多种三维晶格上的伊辛模型，获取覆盖广泛无关温度场（irrelevant temperature field）范围的数据集，从而更精确地确定描述标度修正（corrections to scaling）的参数，改进三维伊辛临界性的普适参数估计。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟结合有限尺寸标度分析，研究了多种三维晶格上的伊辛模型，特别结合过氧化氢晶格（hydrogen peroxide lattice）与其他五种三维晶格的结果，构建了覆盖广泛无关场范围的数据集。

Result: 所有模型的临界指数均符合三维伊辛普适类（Ising universality class），标度修正幅度显示无关场（irrelevant field）相对较大。研究获得了描述三维伊辛临界性的新普适参数：温度重整化指数（temperature renormalization exponent）$y_t = 1.58693 (9)$，磁重整化指数（magnetic renormalization exponent）$y_h = 2.48178 (5)$，以及无关指数（irrelevant exponent）$y_1 = -0.821 (5)$，误差范围较先前蒙特卡洛分析有所减小。

Conclusion: 通过分析多种三维晶格上的伊辛模型，研究获得了覆盖广泛无关场范围的数据集，成功改进了描述三维伊辛临界性与标度修正的普适参数精度，为理解临界现象提供了更精确的理论参数。

Abstract: We perform a Monte Carlo analysis of the Ising model on many three-dimensional lattices. By means of finite-size scaling we obtain the critical points and determine the scaling dimensions. As expected, the critical exponents agree with the three-dimensional Ising universality class for all models. The irrelevant field, as revealed by the correction-to-scaling amplitudes, appears to be relatively large. Combining the Monte Carlo results for the hydrogen peroxide lattice with those for five other three-dimensional lattices, we obtain a set of data covering a wide range of the irrelevant temperature field. This is helpful in the determination of the parameters describing the corrections to scaling. As a consequence, new results are obtained for the universal parameters describing Ising criticality in three dimensions, with reduced error margins in comparison with earlier Monte Carlo analyses. The critical exponents describing the thermodynamic singularities are determined by the temperature renormalization exponent $y_t = 1.58693 (9)$ and the magnetic renormalization exponent $y_h = 2.48178 (5)$. The corrections to scaling are governed by the irrelevant exponent $y_1 = -0.821 (5)$.

### [152] [Tripartite information of two-dimensional free fermions: a sine-kernel spectral constant from Fermi surface geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03103)
*Aleksandrs Sokolovs*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明自由费米子基态中的互信息单调性（MMI）是观测尺度的性质而非量子态的性质。研究发现三部分信息 $I_3$ 可分解为 $I_3 = \sum_{k_y} g(k_F w)$，其中 $g(z)$ 在临界值 $z^* \approx 1.329$ 处改变符号，表明 MMI 的满足与否取决于费米动量与观测宽度的乘积 $k_F w$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在澄清互信息单调性（monogamy of mutual information, MMI）在自由费米子基态中的本质属性。传统上通过三部分信息（tripartite information）$I_3$ 的符号将量子态分类为"全息"或"非全息"，但本文质疑这种分类是否具有尺度依赖性。

Method: 采用二维晶格上三个相邻宽度为 $w$ 的条带作为观测区域。利用平移对称性将三部分信息分解为 $I_3 = \sum_{k_y} g(k_F(k_y) w)$，其中 $g(z)$ 由正弦核积分算子（sine-kernel integral operator，即 Slepian concentration operator）的谱决定。通过解析方法确定 $g(z)$ 的性质，并在方形和三角晶格上进行验证。

Result: 发现 $g(z)$ 在 $z^* \approx 1.329$ 处存在唯一零点：当 $k_F w < z^*$ 时违反 MMI（$g > 0$），当 $k_F w > z^*$ 时满足 MMI（$g < 0$）。由于 $z^* / k_F w \to 0$ 当 $w \to \infty$，任何费米面在大尺度下最终满足 MMI，而无能隙系统在足够小尺度下违反 MMI。对于 Rényi 熵指数 $α> 1$，函数 $g_α(z)$ 呈现振荡行为并多次改变符号。

Conclusion: 互信息单调性（MMI）是观测尺度的性质而非量子态的固有属性。基于 $I_3$ 符号将态分类为"全息"或"非全息"的做法具有尺度依赖性。相互作用会使临界值 $z^*$ 产生约 1-2% 的偏移。

Abstract: We show that monogamy of mutual information (MMI) in free-fermion ground states is a property of the observation scale, not of the quantum state. For three adjacent strips of width $w$ on a two-dimensional lattice, translation invariance decomposes the tripartite information as $I_3 = \sum_{k_y} g(k_F(k_y)\, w)$, where $g(z)$ is a universal function of the dimensionless product $z = k_F w$, determined by the spectrum of the sine-kernel integral operator (the Slepian concentration operator). We prove that $g(z)$ has a unique zero at $z^* \approx 1.329$: modes with $k_F w < z^*$ violate MMI ($g > 0$), while modes with $k_F w > z^*$ satisfy it ($g < 0$). Since $z^* / k_F w \to 0$ as $w \to \infty$, any Fermi surface eventually satisfies MMI at large $w$, while any gapless system violates it at sufficiently small $w$. The classification of states as "holographic" or "non-holographic" by the sign of $I_3$ is thus scale-dependent. We establish the properties of $g(z)$ analytically and show that $z^*$ is determined to $0.12\%$ by the cancellation of only two Slepian eigenvalue contributions. For Rényi entropies with index $α> 1$, the function $g_α(z)$ oscillates with multiple sign changes. We verify the framework on square and triangular lattices and show that interactions shift $z^*$ by $\sim 1$--$2\%$.

</details>


### [153] [Dynamically Emergent Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03162)
*Satya N. Majumdar,Gregory Schehr*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文讨论了在经典和量子非相互作用系统中，当受到共同随机环境波动时动态涌现相关性（DEC）的情景。这些系统表现出强烈的动态相关性，即使在稳态中也能持续存在，且在某些模型中具有可计算物理观测量（observables）的解析结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动态涌现相关性（DEC）的动机在于探索非相互作用系统在共同随机环境波动下如何产生强烈的动态相关性，这种相关性并非来自内置相互作用，而是从动力学中涌现。DEC代表了非平衡统计物理（out-of-equilibrium statistical physics）中一个快速发展的研究领域。

Method: 论文采用理论分析的方法，研究经典和量子非相互作用系统在共同随机环境波动下的动力学行为。重点分析多个DEC模型的稳态特性，这些模型展现出有趣的解析结构，使得计算物理观测量成为可能。

Result: 研究发现DEC系统的稳态表现出强烈的相关性，这些相关性在长时间尺度上持续存在。尽管系统高度相关，但某些DEC模型的稳态具有特殊的解析结构，允许计算物理观测量。最近的实验表明，这些稳态中的DEC实际上可以被测量。

Conclusion: 动态涌现相关性（DEC）是强关联非平衡统计物理中一个快速发展的研究领域，具有理论和实验、经典和量子的多重维度。DEC展示了非相互作用系统在共同随机环境波动下如何产生持久的相关性，为理解复杂系统的涌现行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this perspective article, we discuss the scenario of dynamically emergent correlation (DEC) arising in classical and quantum noninteracting systems when they are subjected to a common fluctuating stochastic environment. The key property of such systems is that the strong correlations between different particles emerge from the dynamics and not from built-in interactions. In many cases, these strong correlations persist even at long times in the stationary state. Computing observables explicitly for such strongly correlated states in general is very hard. Remarkably, the stationary states in several models of DEC exhibit an interesting analytical structure that allows to compute physical observables, despite being strongly correlated. Recent experiments on trapped colloidal particles have established that these DEC in the stationary state can in fact be measured. DEC is a rapidly emerging domain of strongly correlated out-of-equilibrium statistical physics, with both theoretical and experimental, as well as classical and quantum, components.

</details>


### [154] [Will a Large Complex System be a Maxwell Demon?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03248)
*Matthew P Leighton*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨随机复杂系统中麦克斯韦妖（Maxwell demon）出现的概率，发现随着自由度增加，发现妖的概率至少呈指数下降，表明大型复杂妖只能通过选择过程产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物学中普遍存在类似麦克斯韦妖（Maxwell demon）的物理系统，这些系统似乎局部违反热力学第二定律。研究旨在探讨这种现象是否令人惊讶，以及在大型复杂系统中麦克斯韦妖行为是否不可避免。

Method: 研究提出随机系统作为零模型（null model），考虑连续和离散随机动力学两种情况，分析具有多个自由度的随机随机系统（random stochastic system）中麦克斯韦妖出现的可能性。

Result: 结果显示发现麦克斯韦妖的概率随着自由度数量增加而至少呈指数下降，在某些情况下甚至呈双指数下降。这表明大型复杂麦克斯韦妖不可能在随机系统中自发出现。

Conclusion: 大型复杂麦克斯韦妖只能通过选择过程（process of selection）产生，而非随机系统的自然结果。这解释了为何生物学中观察到的麦克斯韦妖现象需要特定的演化机制。

Abstract: Emerging evidence suggests that physical systems operating as Maxwell demons, in which some subsystem of a larger system extracts heat energy from its environment in an apparent local violation of the second law, are commonplace throughout biology. Should these findings surprise us, or is Maxwell demon behavior inevitable in sufficiently large complex systems? In this Letter we pose the question of how likely it is that a random stochastic system with many degrees of freedom will operate as a Maxwell demon, considering null models for both continuous and discrete random dynamics. Our results show the probability of a finding a demon decreases at least exponentially, and in some cases double-exponentially, with the number of degrees of freedom, ultimately suggesting that large complex demons can only arise through a process of selection.

### [156] [Complexity of quantum cohomology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02736)
*Xiaobo Liu,Chongyu Wang*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二维拓扑量子场论（2D TQFT）的电路复杂度，重点关注紧致辛流形量子上同调给出的TQFT。作者估计了Fano完全交和（余）极小齐次簇的有限近似复杂度状态数量，给出了有限复杂度状态空间维度的上界，并在Gr(2, n)情况下得到了精确描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Couch、Fan和Shashi在文献[12]中定义了二维拓扑量子场论（2D TQFT）的电路复杂度。本研究旨在将这一复杂度概念应用于由紧致辛流形的量子上同调（quantum cohomology）给出的具体2D TQFT，探索其复杂度特性。

Method: 作者采用量子上同调理论框架，研究Fano完全交（Fano complete intersections）和（余）极小齐次簇（(co)minuscule homogeneous varieties）两类具体几何对象。通过分析量子乘法（quantum multiplication）的谱特性，特别是处理元素（handle element，也称为量子欧拉类（quantum Euler class））除以点类的特征值。

Result: 对于Fano完全交和（余）极小齐次簇，给出了具有有限近似复杂度（任意小容差）的状态数量估计。获得了有限复杂度状态空间维度的上界，在Gr(2, n)情况下该上界是尖锐的，并精确描述了该子空间。对于（余）极小齐次簇，证明了处理元素除以点类的量子乘法特征值的正性结果。

Conclusion: 该研究将电路复杂度概念应用于具体几何背景的二维拓扑量子场论，在Fano完全交和（余）极小齐次簇上获得了复杂度状态的定量估计和谱正性结果，深化了对量子上同调TQFT复杂度结构的理解。

Abstract: Circuit complexity for two-dimensional topological quantum field theories (2D TQFT) was defined by Couch, Fan, and Shashi in [12]. In this paper, we study complexity for the 2D TQFT given by quantum cohomology of compact symplectic manifolds. We will estimate the number of states with finite approximate complexity of arbitrarily small tolerance for Fano complete intersections and (co)minuscule homogeneous varieties. We will give an upper bound for the dimension of the space spanned by states with finite complexity. In the case of Gr(2, n), this bound is sharp and we also obtain a precise description for this subspace. For (co)minuscule homogeneous varieties, we prove a positivity result for the eigenvalues of quantum multiplication by the handle element (also called the quantum Euler class) divided by the class of a point.

</details>


### [157] [Commutative $BV_\infty$ algebras, their morphisms and $\frac{\infty}{2}$-variation of Hodge structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02953)
*Hao Wen*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了交换$BV_\infty$代数间的态射，证明在适当条件下，拟同构可诱导极化Hodge结构的$\frac{\infty}{2}$-变体及Frobenius流形的等价性，并以奇点理论为例验证结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究交换$BV_\infty$代数（commutative $BV_\infty$ algebras）间的态射（morphisms），旨在探讨拟同构（quasi-isomorphism）如何影响相关的几何结构。

Method: 在满足适当附加假设的条件下，分析交换$BV_\infty$代数的拟同构，证明其可诱导$\frac{\infty}{2}$-变体Hodge结构（$\frac{\infty}{2}$-variations of Hodge structures）与极化（polarizations）的等价性，进而导出Frobenius流形（Frobenius manifolds）的对应关系。

Result: 建立了交换$BV_\infty$代数的拟同构与极化Hodge结构的$\frac{\infty}{2}$-变体及Frobenius流形之间的对应关系，并通过奇点理论（singularity theory）的显式例子验证了该结果。

Conclusion: 在适当条件下，交换$BV_\infty$代数的拟同构可诱导极化Hodge结构的$\frac{\infty}{2}$-变体及Frobenius流形的等价性，这一结论通过奇点理论的实例得到验证。

Abstract: We study morphisms between commutative $BV_\infty$ algebras and show that, under suitable additional assumptions, a quasi-isomorphism of commutative $BV_\infty$ algebras induces an identification of $\frac{\infty}{2}$-variations of Hodge structures with polarizations, and consequently of Frobenius manifolds. An explicit example arising from singularity theory is provided to illustrate the result.

</details>


### [158] [Hasse-Witt invariants of Calabi-Yau varieties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03055)
*Jin Cao,Mohamed Elmi,Hossein Movasati*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文为Calabi-Yau簇（Calabi-Yau varieties）定义了两种不同的Hasse-Witt不变量（Hasse-Witt invariant）定义方法，并猜想这两种定义是等价的，提供了多个支持该猜想的Calabi-Yau簇实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为Calabi-Yau簇建立Hasse-Witt不变量的精确定义。目前存在多种可能的定义方式，需要明确其数学内涵并探讨不同定义之间的关系。

Method: 本文提出了两种定义方法：第一种通过Cartier算子（Cartier operator）定义；第二种通过第三作者发展的Calabi-Yau模形式理论（Calabi-Yau modular forms）来定义。

Result: 作者为Calabi-Yau簇建立了两种不同的Hasse-Witt不变量定义，并提出了这两种定义等价的猜想。通过提供多个Calabi-Yau簇的具体实例，为这一猜想提供了支持性证据。

Conclusion: 本文为Calabi-Yau簇的Hasse-Witt不变量提供了两种可能的定义途径，并提出了它们等价性的猜想。这些定义和猜想为进一步研究Calabi-Yau簇的算术性质奠定了基础。

Abstract: We define the Hasse-Witt invariant of Calabi-Yau varieties in two different ways. The first method is through Cartier operator and the second method is through the theory of Calabi-Yau modular forms developed by the third author. We conjecture that these two definitions are equivalent and provide many examples of Calabi-Yau varieties in support of this conjecture.

</details>

### [159] [Internal Charge Amplification in Germanium at 77K and 4K: From Single-Free-Flight Bounds to a Physics-Informed Ionization Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02391)
*Dongming Mei,Kunming Dong,Narayan Budhathoki,Shasika Panamaldeniya,Francisco Ponce*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出一个紧凑框架，用于预测低温高纯锗（HPGe）探测器内部电荷放大（ICA）的雪崩起始临界电场 \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\)，该框架结合了基于迁移率的单次自由飞行（SFF）上限和包含能量相关散射、非抛物线（Kane）色散、谷间转移及高能"幸运漂移"尾的物理信息碰撞电离模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低温高纯锗（HPGe）中的内部电荷放大（ICA）可通过在探测器晶体内部提供增益来降低检测阈值，但其可靠运行需要对雪崩起始临界电场 \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\) 进行预测性估计。

Method: 提出一个统一框架，在77K和4K（HPGe典型工作温度）下桥接（i）基于迁移率的单次自由飞行（SFF）上限与（ii）包含能量相关散射、非抛物线（Kane）色散、谷间转移及高能"幸运漂移"尾的物理信息碰撞电离模型。该处理产生了封闭形式的设计有用关系式，包括 \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}^{(\mathrm{PI})}=B(T)/\ln[A(T)d]\)，以及一个实用的校准工作流程。

Result: 示例电子和空穴估计表明，实际传输通常相对于SFF降低了 \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\)，并增加了77K和4K之间 \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\) 的预测变化。所得便携公式将材料/传输输入与几何结构、过量噪声和场成形联系起来。

Conclusion: 该框架为锗和其他低温半导体中具有受控淬灭的稳定、单极偏好的ICA提供了可直接用于设计的指导，通过将测量的低场迁移率 \(μ(T)\) 和增益曲线 \(M(V)\)（Chynoweth分析）映射到具有传播不确定带的器件级偏置目标。

Abstract: Internal charge amplification (ICA) in cryogenic high-purity germanium (HPGe) can lower detection thresholds by providing gain inside the detector crystal, but reliable operation requires a predictive estimate of the avalanche-onset \emph{critical electric field} \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\). We present a compact framework for \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\) at 77~K and 4~K (typical HPGe operating temperatures) that bridges (i) a mobility-based single-free-flight (SFF) upper bound with (ii) a physics-informed impact-ionization model incorporating energy-dependent scattering, nonparabolic (Kane) dispersion, intervalley transfer, and the high-energy ``lucky-drift'' tail. This unified treatment yields closed-form, design-useful relations, including \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}^{(\mathrm{PI})}=B(T)/\ln[A(T)d]\), and a practical calibration workflow that maps measured low-field mobility \(μ(T)\) and gain curves \(M(V)\) (Chynoweth analysis) to device-level bias targets with propagated uncertainty bands. Example electron and hole estimates indicate that realistic transport typically lowers \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\) relative to SFF and increases the predicted change in \(E_{\mathrm{crit}}\) between 77~K and 4~K. The resulting portable formulas connect materials/transport inputs to geometry, excess noise, and field shaping, providing design-ready guidance for stable, unipolar-favored ICA with controlled quenching in Ge and other cryogenic semiconductors.

</details>


### [160] [Improvement and assessment of the radiopurity of Micromegas readout planes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03274)
*Juan Castel,Susana Cebrian,Theopisti Dafni,David Diez-Ibanez,Alvaro Ezquerro,Juan Antonio Garcia,Hector Gomez,Igor G. Irastorza,Gloria Luzon,Cristina Margalejo,Hector Mirallas,Luis Obis,Rui de Oliveira,Alfonso Ortiz de Solorzano,Oscar Perez,Jorge Porron,Maria J. Puyuelo,Ana Quintana,Maria Rodriguez,Laura Segui*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究通过地下实验室多种技术手段，证实了微网气体探测器（Micromegas）作为时间投影室读出装置的极低放射性纯度，其关键同位素活度显著降低，适用于稀有现象探测实验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微网气体探测器（Micromegas）因其良好的空间和能量分辨率以及操作稳定性，被考虑用于核双β衰变、太阳轴子探测和低质量暗物质相互作用等稀有现象实验。此外，其主要由铜和聚酰亚胺（kapton）等潜在放射性纯净材料制成，适合超低本底条件。

Method: 研究在CERN进行专门开发后，于坎弗兰克地下实验室（Canfranc Underground Laboratory）结合多种技术进行新的放射性分析。使用BiPo-3探测器分析BiPo序列来约束²³⁸U和²³²Th天然衰变链低能段的同位素活度，同时使用高纯锗（HPGe）探测器通过γ能谱法测定⁴⁰K含量。

Result: ²³⁸U和²³²Th天然衰变链低能段的同位素活度分别被约束为<0.064和<0.016 μBq/cm²，而⁴⁰K的最低含量为0.102±0.030 μBq/cm²。后者相对于首次分析样品的⁴⁰K活度减少了34倍。

Conclusion: 这些结果证实了微网气体探测器作为极低放射性纯净读出装置适用于稀有事件搜索实验，其放射性本底水平满足超低本底实验的要求。

Abstract: Micromesh Gas Structures (Micromegas) as readout of gaseous Time Projection Chambers (TPCs) are being considered in experiments investigating rare phenomena, like the nuclear double beta decay, solar axion detection and low-mass dark matter interactions, due to their good performance on spatial and energy resolution and operation stability. In addition, as they are potentially made mainly of radiopure materials like copper and kapton, they are appropriate for ultra-low background conditions. After a promising first study of the radiopurity of Micromegas readout planes, here results after dedicated development at CERN obtained from new radioassays, performed at the Canfranc Underground Laboratory combining different techniques, are presented. Activity of the isotopes in the lower parts of the 238U and 232Th natural chains has been constrained by analyzing the BiPo sequences using the BiPo-3 detector to be <0.064 and <0.016 muBq/cm2 respectively, while a lowest 40K content of 0.102+-0.030 muBq/cm2 has been determined by gamma spectroscopy using a HPGe detector; the latter value implies a reduction of a factor 34 with respect to the 40K activity quantified in the first analyzed sample. These results confirm the suitability of the use of Micromegas as extremely radiopure readouts for rare event searches.

</details>


### [161] [Capacitively Coupled GaAs p-i-n/Substrate Photodetector with Ohmic Contacts on Lightly Doped n-GaAs for Hard X-Ray Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02762)
*V. G. Harutyunyan,S. D. Zilio,M. Colja,M. Cautero,G. Cautero,L. Sbuelz,D. Curcio,G. Biasiol*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种电容耦合GaAs p+-i-n/衬底光电探测器（CC-GaAs PIN/S PD），该器件是迈向高能X射线脉冲三维探测（x, y, 时间）的初步步骤。该探测器展示了在轻掺杂n-GaAs上通过多步退火制备Cr/Au欧姆接触的制造策略，并包含减少漏电流的额外接触结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在开发高能X射线脉冲的三维探测（3D detection）技术，其中x和y维度代表空间位置，时间维度记录脉冲时序。虽然最终的三维探测器将基于分离吸收与倍增雪崩光电二极管（SAM APD）设计，但当前器件为理解最终器件性能提供了重要参考。

Method: 采用多步退火工艺在280-330°C低温范围内制备Cr/Au欧姆接触（ohmic contacts），该工艺同时应用于轻掺杂n-GaAs和p+ GaAs。器件结构包含额外的接触设计，通过施加与阳极相同的偏压来减少漏电流（leakage current）。

Result: 使用80 MHz激光进行的测量表明，该光电探测器能够检测每个脉冲对应10^6个电子的脉冲信号。制造策略成功实现了在轻掺杂n-GaAs上制备欧姆接触，这是光电探测器架构所需的关键技术。

Conclusion: 电容耦合GaAs p+-i-n/衬底光电探测器展示了实现高能X射线脉冲三维探测的可行性。该器件的制造策略和性能特征为后续集成倍增层的最终器件设计提供了有价值的技术基础。

Abstract: In this work, we present a capacitively coupled GaAs p +-i-n/substrate photodetector (CC-GaAs PIN/S PD), which also represents a preliminary step toward 3D detection (x, y, time) of high-energy X-ray pulses. Although the final 3D detector will be based on a separate absorption and multiplication avalanche photodiode (SAM APD) design, the present device exhibits characteristics that offer valuable insights into the performance expected once a multiplication layer is incorporated into the final device. In particular, we present a fabrication strategy that employs multi-step annealing in the low-temperature range of 280 330C to achieve Cr/Au ohmic contacts on lightly doped n-GaAs, which is also required for the photodetector architecture. Simultaneously, the same contact preparation process was applied to p + GaAs. Furthermore, the fabricated CC-GaAs PIN/S PD includes an additional contact designed to reduce leakage current by applying the same bias as that of the anode. Measurements performed using an 80 MHz laser demonstrated the photodetector's ability to detect pulses corresponding to 10^6 electrons per pulse.

</details>
